[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#new-premium-music-system-release-beta-november-20th-2025)

New Premium Music System Release (Beta) - November 20th, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Today we’re launching our completely new, fully built-from-scratch **Premium Music System**. This is an entirely new feature set with its own audio engine, Smart Search, actions, events, variables, and a complete music module. The entire system is **Premium-only permanently** and currently available in **BETA ONLY**, so please enable Beta Mode before testing.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FaBgVYk5dmlioplI3dwat%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ad200b1-0853-44a5-9e3f-b893e932e128&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe0e36c2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#how-it-works)

How It Works

**Create Player:** Required before using any music feature. This connects the bot to voice and starts the audio engine. **Search & Add:** Search for songs, browse results, or add tracks directly into the queue. **Play:** Playback begins as soon as the queue has tracks. **Controls:** Pause, resume, skip, stop, replay, and seek. **Queue:** View, remove, clear, or shuffle the queue at any time. **Audio:** Adjust volume, set loop modes, enable AutoPlay, toggle AutoLeave, or apply filters like bassboost, nightcore, vaporwave, 8D, tempo, and more.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#music-smart-search)

Music Smart Search

A new command option type that gives users real-time Spotify autocomplete inside Discord. As they type, the system displays up to 25 formatted results. Selecting one provides: `{option.result}` – stable track ID `{option.title}` – “Song – Artist” label Typing manually without selecting a result returns the raw input, supporting song names, URLs, and custom queries. No setup required and no API keys needed.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#music-actions-19)

Music Actions (19)

Create Player, Add to Queue, Play Queue, Pause, Resume, Stop, Disconnect, Skip, Seek, Set Volume, Set Loop Mode, Set AutoPlay, Set AutoLeave, Replay Track, Remove From Queue, Shuffle Queue, Apply Filter, Clear Filters, Search Tracks. All actions are new, built for advanced command building, automations, menus, DJ tools, and fully custom music systems.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#music-events-29)

Music Events (29)

Track events: start, end, stuck, exception, queue finished Player controls: play, pause, resume, stop, skip, seek, shuffle Queue events: added, removed Settings: volume, loop mode, autoplay, autoleave Connection: connect, disconnect, moved, auto-leave triggered Filters: updated System: player created, updated, destroyed, node switched, socket closed These enable complete automation, reactive features, and dynamic music experiences.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252Ft6PoVwVpCHLukGEMHzqR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf72433e-e8fd-49a4-a057-f36c31a9ad60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63ddf0c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#music-variables)

Music Variables

**Object Variables:** `{MusicPlayer}`, `{MusicCurrentTrack}`, `{MusicQueue}`, `{MusicSearchResult}` **Helper Variables:** Search results, track metadata (title, artist, URL, requester), durations, position, remaining time, progress %, queue length, next track, total queue duration, formatted lists, and player state (playing, paused, connected, ready, loop mode text, volume %, autoplay, autoleave).

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FzbHBzbOp7WcBOUY8bKVQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4dd49b8c-7109-46bc-a71c-8166f3cd5895&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8998d6e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#music-module)

Music Module

A full plug-and-play music system using all the new actions and events. It includes complete prebuilt commands for playback, queue management, filters, and more. You can customize any command, change logic, adjust permissions, reset the module, or remove it entirely. It works as both a ready-to-use system and a blueprint for your own custom features.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252Fs1bdMbKgTQF6C4IsqERq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97a2665a-23f4-44cd-8e17-801bf55a66d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=187fba81&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#whats-coming-next)

What’s Coming Next

Variable support for dropdown options, success/error handlers, improvements to first-track playback stutter, fixes for rare track-related crashes, further Lavalink refinements, and general stability improvements.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#reintroduction-of-the-message-builder-module-november-5th-2025)

Reintroduction of the Message Builder Module - November 5th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve rebuilt and reintroduced the **Message Builder** with a brand-new templating system, improved embed tools, and full integration with the Command and Event Builders.

You can now **create, save, and reuse professional Discord messages** anywhere in your bot. The new Message Builder is **available to all users immediately**.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FjgNICvHT5BiBCuz1VPGs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8343f962-730b-40ac-b955-8f4c7f1cc2d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=334ede54&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#what-is-the-message-builder)

What is the Message Builder

The Message Builder lets you design and manage embeds visually — no code needed. You can preview messages live, save them as templates, send them to channels or webhooks, and load them directly into commands and events.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FDEp15a6v5u3NqnwqUky6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D49e0e2fa-f8a7-461e-915e-7982f0b9980f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79a91b3c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#key-features)

Key Features

*   **Visual Message Creation** – Build up to 10 embeds with markdown, colors, fields, images, and timestamps.
    
*   **Template System** – Save, edit, and reuse templates across your bot.
    
*   **Smart Validation** – Live counters and error checks keep messages within Discord limits.
    
*   **Multiple Send Options** – Send via Bot, Webhook, or load templates in commands/events.
    
*   **Mobile Friendly** – Works seamlessly on all devices with live preview and autosave.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#advanced-message-block-integration)

Advanced Message Block Integration

The **Advanced Message** block in the Command and Event Builders now fully integrates with the Message Builder:

*   **Load templates** you’ve created in the Message Builder.
    
*   **Save new templates** directly from within your command or event — they’ll instantly appear in the Message Builder module.
    

This two-way sync makes it easy to manage and reuse professional messages without recreating them each time.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252Fg0pxWBETAWAuD56FdGSM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b74c4de-edb2-48c2-b563-1c46703ccf4d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f302ad0b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#free-vs-premium)

Free vs Premium

**Free Users:** Up to 5 templates with full builder access. **Premium Users:** Unlimited templates and usage in all commands/events.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#common-uses)

Common Uses

Welcome messages • Server rules • Announcements • Help menus • Event notifications • FAQs • Changelogs

The updated Message Builder is live under **Message Builder** in your dashboard.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#create-transcript-action-beta-october-28th-2025)

Create Transcript Action (Beta) - October 28th, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve released the brand new **Create Transcript** action — a powerful new feature that lets you generate secure, HTML archives of any Discord channel. Perfect for support tickets, meeting logs, moderation evidence, and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252Fq4334LAbwUtxIHQxki3d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3c86964-3b82-4954-b6c8-d980ffaae4cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6b2e4e8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#what-are-transcripts)

What Are Transcripts

Transcripts let you save and view complete chat histories in a clean, searchable HTML format. They include:

*   Full message content with markdown, embeds, and attachments,
    
*   Usernames, avatars, and timestamps,
    
*   Message links that jump directly back to Discord,
    
*   Optional password protection for sensitive data
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#how-it-works-1)

How It Works

Add the new **Create Transcript** action inside your commands or events under **Message Actions**.

*   Choose a **Target Channel** (current or specific),
    
*   Give your transcript a **custom name** (supports variables like `{user_name}` or `{server}`),
    
*   Add an **optional tag** for organization (support, moderation, meetings, etc.),
    
*   Set **message limits** (1–1000),
    
*   Optionally filter by **date range**,
    
*   Choose whether to **include bot messages**,
    
*   You can also access your transcript URLs later in the command via optional variables
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#themes)

Themes

You can choose between two transcript layouts:

*   **Simple Theme** — Clean, modern design with full customization Customization options include:
    
    *   Primary and background colors
        
    *   Message density
        
    *   Avatar and timestamp visibility
        
    *   Custom header text
        
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FWRhcRUYPjqc8qywN6cFj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd88759a3-0697-405f-9c9a-b251320f1d0d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf35f5b9&sv=2)

*   **Discord Theme** — Authentic Discord-style interface that replicates the chat layout
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FFseOKVB6pwdnwepBQSnh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8823a6e9-f61d-4a25-9fec-49fbff2ef11a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c267b7b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#password-protection)

Password Protection

Keep private transcripts secure:

*   Enable password protection in settings,
    
*   Passwords are required for **view**, **download**, and **raw access**,
    
*   Passwords are securely hashed with bcrypt,
    

Ideal for confidential support tickets, HR logs, or moderation records.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#managing-transcripts)

Managing Transcripts

All your transcripts can be viewed directly on the dashboard on the [**Transcripts Page**](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/transcripts)
. From this page, you can:

*   View, download, or delete transcripts,
    
*   Search and filter by name, tag, or server,
    
*   See creation date, message count, and password status
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252F1MerkDe2Tswe4Y9HWcIW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68b6b37a-918d-4de9-aade-01ae721b422b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c48e42c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#tips-and-notes)

Tips & Notes

*   Limit messages to only what’s needed for faster generation,
    
*   Use tags and descriptive names for better organization,
    
*   Secure sensitive transcripts with passwords,
    
*   Transcripts automatically delete after **365 days**
    

Transcripts are currently in **beta only**. You can enable beta in the settings page of your bot.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#module-builder-removal--twitch-youtube-module-depreciation--block-floating-helper-text-october-17t)

Module Builder Removal + Twitch/YouTube Module Depreciation + Block Floating Helper Text - October 17th, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#module-builder-removal)

Module Builder Removal

The **Custom Module Builder** has been removed. While powerful, it was built on top of the **old JSON-based module system**, making it overly complicated, hard to maintain, and confusing for new users. This architecture also made future integration with **BotPanel** difficult and unintuitive.

We plan to rebuild this system from the ground up into something **far simpler and cleaner**, focusing on **assigning inputs and custom variables (BGVARS)** that can be easily controlled and reused. This approach will make future integrations seamless and much easier to understand.

You can still re-enable the old builder from **Settings → Show Custom Module Builder** if you wish to view or edit old modules.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#twitch--youtube-modules-depreciation)

Twitch + YouTube Modules Depreciation

The old **Twitch** and **YouTube Custom Modules** have been **deprecated** (unless already enabled).

They’ve been replaced with new, simplified modules that — when clicked — **instantly open the Custom Event Builder** with the **corresponding Twitch or YouTube event pre-selected**. This removes unnecessary steps and aligns everything under the cleaner **event-based workflow**.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#new-helper-text-for-blocks)

New: Helper Text for Blocks

You can now add **Helper Text** to any block:

*   Floating label beside your block for quick notes,
    
*   Customizable **icon**, **border color**, and **position**,
    
*   Great for reminders, explanations, or TODOs inside complex setups
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252F2ufoTGzYpEaZQ7pOIcXb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1e77609-ec0f-4c79-a45f-d8df77928f32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a80f0bed&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#youtube-video-upload-action-event-october-16th-2025)

YouTube Video Upload Action Event - October 16th, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve added a new **YouTube Video Upload** Action Event to BotGhost. Your bot can now automatically notify your Discord server whenever a YouTube channel uploads a new video — no webhooks or external integrations required.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FveicQ3MGF87wgS84xMgX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7d18b903-0b34-48d2-9483-e0abb6ba436b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91da620b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#overview)

Overview

The **YouTube Video Upload** event monitors any YouTube channel and posts an automatic message when a new video is uploaded. You can include the video’s title, description, thumbnail, duration, and live subscriber count directly in your Discord message or embed. Perfect for communities that want instant updates from their favorite creators, gaming channels, or news sources.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#key-features-1)

Key Features

*   Instant notifications within seconds of a new upload
    
*   No IFTTT, webhooks, or external setup needed
    
*   Works with any YouTube channel
    
*   Accepts all formats: URLs, @handles, or Channel IDs
    
*   Includes 19 dynamic variables for channel and video info
    
*   Automatically filters private, unlisted, and premieres
    
*   Built-in duplicate protection
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#setup-guide)

Setup Guide

1.  Go to **Custom Events** in your BotGhost dashboard
    
2.  Click **\+ New Event**
    
3.  Select **YouTube Video Upload** from the Action Events list
    
4.  Enter any YouTube channel — paste a link, handle, or channel ID
    
5.  Click **Validate Channel** to confirm the channel and subscribe
    
6.  Configure your **Send or Edit a Message** block
    
7.  Save the event
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#available-variables)

Available Variables

**Channel Data:**

*   `{event_youtube_channel_name}` – Channel name,
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_title}` – Display title
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_icon}` – Channel avatar
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_description}` – Channel description
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_subscribers}` – Subscriber count
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_videos}` – Total videos
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_views}` – Total views
    
*   `{event_youtube_channel_url}` – Channel link
    

**Video Data:**

*   `{event_youtube_video_title}` – Video title
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_description}` – Video description
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_thumbnail}` – HD thumbnail
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_url}` – Video link
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_duration}` – Duration
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_upload_time}` – Upload date/time
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_views}` – View count
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_likes}` – Like count
    
*   `{event_youtube_video_comments}` – Comment count
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#highlights)

Highlights

*   Works instantly — typically under 30 seconds
    
*   Always accurate — stats are updated every upload
    
*   Handles high-frequency channels reliably
    
*   Fully customizable messages and embeds
    
*   Uses your own bot to post directly to your server
    

This new Action Event makes YouTube notifications effortless to set up and fully customizable inside the BotGhost builder. Just validate a channel, configure your message, and your bot will automatically post new video alerts.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#twitch-alerts-action-event-october-15th-2025)

Twitch Alerts Action Event - October 15th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve added a new **Twitch Alerts Action Event** to BotGhost. This event makes setting up Twitch alerts simple and automatic — no need for webhooks, IFTTT, or any external setup.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FjKwrlhBqgjwT3JGqPkhA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddee255d8-ca0b-4f41-a2a5-0586ddfc4900&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=968e941e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#overview-1)

Overview

The new **Twitch Stream Online** Action Event instantly notifies your Discord server when a Twitch streamer goes live. Your bot can post messages or embeds with full stream information such as title, game, thumbnail, and viewer count. This replaces the old manual process and allows you to create alerts entirely within the BotGhost builder.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#key-features-2)

Key Features

*   Instant notifications when a stream goes live
    
*   No IFTTT, webhooks, or external setup required
    
*   Pre-configured block for fast setup
    
*   Full Twitch data available as variables
    
*   Works with any public Twitch channel
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FPB8yC0WmBrgBHL06CejV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad99168b-47e3-427a-94ee-fca9769c224d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8af160be&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#how-to-use)

How to Use

1.  Go to **Custom Events** in your BotGhost dashboard and create a new event.
    
2.  Select **Twitch Stream Online** from the Action Events list
    
3.  Enter a Twitch username or URL and click **Validate Channel**
    
4.  Customize the **Send or Edit a Message** block for your alert
    
5.  Save the event
    

This update makes setting up Twitch alerts effortless — just one click and your bot will automatically announce when your favorite streamers go live.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#slash-command-autocomplete-october-8th-2025)

Slash Command Autocomplete - October 8th, 2025


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve added support for **Autocomplete** in slash command options. This feature allows your commands to provide dynamic, searchable suggestions to users as they type into a text option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FbN3oWQmn835xFEnTJts6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D616859e5-6ebf-4ea8-a732-a569a888383a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4ea3104&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#what-is-autocomplete)

What Is Autocomplete

Autocomplete displays a list of suggestions while a user types into a slash command field. It helps users quickly find valid inputs without needing to remember exact terms or make guesses.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#how-it-works-2)

How It Works

*   **Available on Text Options** – When creating a slash command, you’ll now see an “Autocomplete” toggle on text options.
    
*   **Configure Choices** – Click “Configure Autocomplete” to open a modal where you can add up to 25 choices.
    
*   **Label & Value Pairs** – Each choice has a label (visible to users) and a value (sent to the command).
    
*   **Automatic Filtering** – Discord automatically filters these suggestions based on what the user types.
    
*   **Easy Management** – You can reorder, add, or remove choices as needed with a live counter showing how many are configured.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#benefits)

Benefits

*   **Improved User Experience** – Users can easily find valid command options without typing errors.
    
*   **Cleaner Commands** – Avoids typos and inconsistent input.
    
*   **Dynamic & Modern** – Makes slash commands feel smoother and more interactive.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#notes)

Notes

*   Only available on **Text options**.
    
*   You can configure **up to 25 choices per option**.
    
*   Autocomplete and static choices cannot be used together.
    
*   Variables cannot be used in autocomplete since it runs before the command executes.
    

This feature was suggested by the community [here](https://discord.com/channels/822426820447567872/1421016837558374502)
 — thank you to everyone who shares their ideas.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#components-v2-message-builder-6th-october-2025)

Components V2 Message Builder - 6th October, 2025


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve introduced the new **Components V2 Message Builder**, which brings Discord’s latest **Display Components system** to BotGhost.

This allows you to visually create advanced messages with up to **40 components** in a single layout.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FZ0289en3xNWBimypKRhH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da374ce49-22be-4357-a743-e32224d9b9f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7381a6f8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#overview-2)

Overview

Components V2 lets you build Discord messages using a **drag-and-drop interface** that supports containers, sections, text, buttons, menus, and other display elements.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252Foted0OKdvzKemEwZoWVy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59021a80-8671-45cb-a30c-72a4ae5d61d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5b9217d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#available-component-types)

Available Component Types

*   **Container:** Root wrapper for grouping sections and text
    
*   **Section:** Organizes content and can include an accessory button
    
*   **Text:** Add formatted text with mention control
    
*   **Button:** Interactive button component
    
*   **Select Menu:** Dropdown menu for user selections
    
*   **Thumbnail:** Displays images with optional spoilers or descriptions
    
*   **Separator:** Divider line between content
    
*   **Media Gallery:** Show multiple media items
    
*   **File:** Attach files with optional spoiler protection
    
*   **Action Row:** Automatically created for buttons and menus
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#buttons-and-menus)

Buttons and Menus

Buttons and select menus are now created **directly inside the builder**:

*   Dropping one onto the canvas automatically creates an **Action Row**
    
*   Each Action Row can contain **up to 5 buttons** or **1 select menu** (not both)
    
*   Buttons can also be added as **accessories** to sections
    
*   The builder automatically validates and prevents invalid configurations
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#structure-and-limits)

Structure and Limits

*   **40 components maximum** per message
    
*   **Containers** must be top-level elements
    
*   **Sections** can be nested within Containers but not each other
    
*   **Action Rows** can only contain buttons or menus
    
*   Empty Containers or invalid setups will show validation warnings
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#allowed-mentions-beta)

Allowed Mentions (Beta)

A new **Allowed Mentions** system has been added to both the standard Message Builder and Components V2. You can now control who gets pinged in messages:

*   **Simple Mode:** Allow or block user, role, or everyone mentions
    
*   **Advanced Mode:** Specify exact user or role IDs allowed to be pinged
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252F1B7fdHR7SPJeXjKVGGTP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ace97c6-1428-484b-a708-dadb926f3dfb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8500cc34&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#beta-status)

Beta Status

Components V2 is currently in **BETA**. This means it is buggy and subject to change. A preview for the message builder is still in the works. Enable Beta Features in your settings to access it.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#whats-coming-next-1)

What's coming next?

*   Full music update with actions and events
    
*   Update regarding what we have planned for free users (tomorrow)

What This Means

*   Automate **auto-moderation**, **reactions**, **voice activity**, **scheduled events**, **stickers**, and more
    
*   Access detailed context with simple **object variables**
    

This update is fully **backward compatible** – your existing events still work, but now you can do so much more.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#add-roles-to-all-users--remove-roles-from-all-users-september-28th-2025)

Add Roles to All Users + Remove Roles from All Users - September 28th, 2025


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FfolR3Q3X9PeG9nLvTUhG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbee2cba1-0581-44c4-8563-56872b4e5339&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f272ebd8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#add-role-to-all-users)

Add Role to All Users

*   Instantly give a role to everyone in your server,
    
*   Perfect for server events, promotions, or new role setups,
    
*   Saves hours of manual assigning on large servers
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FXUuYxDybEJTaIfZdlV7G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D611e9d95-9f19-410e-8b25-2d1a89e3911e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f53385f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#remove-roles-from-all-users)

Remove Roles from All Users

*   Instantly remove a role from everyone in your server
    
*   Clean up old or unused roles in one click
    
*   Restructure or reset your permission system with ease
    
*   Includes a **“Nuclear Option”** to strip _all roles from all users_ (with built-in safety checks)
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252F9OK4F8L0TMj2B5sNqP9S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7efc09f6-b730-4ff2-98b0-fd55a3ec1474&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35e84be3&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#safety--configuration)

Safety + Configuration

*   Respect's role hierarchy (won’t touch roles above your bot)
    
*   Option to include/exclude bots
    
*   Custom audit log reasons
    
*   Double confirmation + extra warnings for irreversible actions
    

These new role actions are now available in the **Role Actions** section of your Command + Event Builder.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#new-forum-post-option--auto-role-on-join-event-september-25th-2025)

New Forum Post Option + Auto Role on Join Event – September 25th, 2025


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#send-a-message-update)

Send a Message Update

We’ve added a new **“Send the message in a new forum post”** option to the **Send a Message** action. With this, you can now:

*   Create a brand-new forum post in any forum channel.
    
*   Set a custom title for the new post.
    
*   Use all the normal message options inside the post.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#update-auto-role-on-join-event)

Update: Auto Role on Join Event

We are introducing a new category of Action Events – powerful pre-built events and actions that act like multiple blocks in one, making it much easier to create common bot features. The first of these is the Auto Role on Join event. When a user joins your server, this event will automatically assign roles to them.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#features)

Features:

*   Roles to Assign – Pick one or multiple roles that should be added automatically.
    
*   Reason Logging – Provide a reason that shows in the server’s audit log.
    
*   Assignment Delay – Delay role assignment by up to 5 minutes (useful for spam prevention).
    
*   Filter Bots – Optionally prevent bots from being assigned roles.
    
*   Require Verification – Only assign roles to members with verified phone numbers.
    
*   Customizable – Add more blocks (welcome messages, logging, etc.) to the event like a normal custom event.
    

This is just the beginning – more pre-configured events and blocks are on the way, including:

*   Welcome card events/blocks
    
*   YouTube/Twitch/Reddit notification events
    
*   Temp Ban/Unban + Temp Mute
    
*   Auto moderation logging
    
*   Add/Remove roles from all users
    
*   Reaction Role menus
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FEKkb9ZxR8Ed44LXOj2Pz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0da1af53-61a6-431e-b4aa-a2cda8f8dad4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4959c27&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#major-command--event-builder-overhaul-september-12th-2025)

Major Command + Event Builder Overhaul - September 12th, 2025


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’ve merged core bot management directly into the Builder. You can now work end-to-end without leaving the page—fewer tabs, less context switching, faster iteration.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#whats-included-all-inside-the-builder)

What’s Included (All Inside the Builder)

*   **Error Logs** • View recent errors with a quick **Refresh** button.
    
*   **Custom Variables / Data Storage** • Create, edit, and delete variables in place; newly created variables appear instantly in all selectors.
    
*   **Custom Commands & Events** • Enable/disable, delete, and (soon) jump straight into editing other commands/events from here.
    
*   **Timed Events** • Create, manage, delete, and set your **Timezone** and **Default Server** for timers.
    
*   **Block Templates** • Your saved templates live here. We’ll be shipping curated defaults for common patterns (CDs, loop users, etc.) next.
    

> This overhaul aims to flatten the learning curve and keep everything you tweak most often within arm’s reach. In-builder, step-by-step tutorials for each tab are coming soon.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#variables-tab)

Variables Tab

*   Create, edit, and delete **custom variables** without leaving your flow.
    
*   **Instant availability**: new variables show up immediately in any variable selector.
    
*   Get a clear, at-a-glance view of what exists before you wire it into logic.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#errors-tab)

Errors Tab

*   A focused **feed of your bot’s errors**, right inside the Builder.
    
*   Functions like the old error logs page, now with a handy **Refresh**.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#commands-events-tab)

Commands / Events Tab

*   Quickly **enable/disable** or **delete** existing commands and events.
    
*   **Coming soon:** jump into editing another command/event without leaving the Builder.
    
*   **Also coming:** create brand-new commands/events directly from this tab.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#timed-events-tab)

Timed Events Tab

*   **Create, manage, and delete** timers from one place.
    
*   Configure your **Timezone** and **Default Server** so schedules behave exactly as expected.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#block-templates-tab)

Block Templates Tab

*   Find and organize your **block templates**.
    
*   **Soon:** a growing library of curated templates for high-demand patterns (CDs, user loops, and more).

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#object-variable-collections--variable-selector-update-september-11th-2025)

Object Variable Collections + Variable Selector Update - September 11th, 2025


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#exposing-collections-on-object-variables)

Exposing Collections on Object Variables

All object variable **properties that return a Manager or Collection** will now return an **array of IDs** (or values if IDs aren’t available). This means you can now directly work with lists inside your commands and events, without needing extra steps.

**Examples:**

*   `{Role.members}` → `[memberId1, memberId2, ...]`
    
*   `{Channel.members}` → `[memberId1, memberId2, ...]`
    
*   `{Member.roles}` → `[roleId1, roleId2, ...]`
    

This is a **major update** — every object property that previously gave a manager/collection will now return a usable array.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FGwWxKM8s0wfc2EHsW1LQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62107795-280d-460c-8a99-c7d82f9653b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c3269bb&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FV8TsGPRee3lz5SLht0ja%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6aee87c0-3aa5-465f-93f8-6e8b2681b74c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d276db7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#updated-variable-selector-easier-object-usage)

Updated Variable Selector (easier Object usage)

*   **Secondary page** on click for all object variables showing **all available properties**.
    
*   **Context-aware insertion:** the object changes based on the event.
    
    *   Example: in a **Message Send** event, the **Message** object is inserted as `{Message.}` (no `[id]` part).
        
    
*   Designed to make selecting and using object properties **faster and clearer**.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#interaction-token-update-and-bug-fixes-june-2nd-2025)

Interaction Token Update & Bug Fixes - June 2nd, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#interaction-token-vulnerability)

Interaction Token Vulnerability

We were recently made aware of a potential vulnerability that, under very specific conditions, allowed the `interaction_token` button/select menu variable to be hijacked by echoing user input in specific custom events. This could be used to force the bot to send a message containing a button that, when clicked, executed API requests — and in some cases, was exploited to retrieve bot tokens.

We’ve now implemented **guardrails** around the `interaction_token` variable, similar to how we protect the `TOKEN_SECRET` variable. This issue has been fully **fixed**.

This vulnerability was **largely contained to bots within this server and GhostBuddy**, and the user who discovered it **responsibly reported it to us early**, which helped limit any impact.

If your bot uses modals or reflects user input (e.g., echoing messages in embeds or **ModMail** systems), we **recommend regenerating your bot token** as a precaution — even though the vulnerability is now resolved.

While we take every precaution to secure your bots and their data, **you are solely responsible for your bot’s security**. Please practice safe development habits and stay vigilant.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#botghost-proxy-downtime)

BotGhost Proxy Downtime

We recently experienced downtime with our proxy provider, which led to latency in API actions and Discord-based features. This issue has now been **fully resolved** and things should be back to normal.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#custom-slot-bug-fix)

Custom Slot Bug Fix

We’ve fixed a visual bug where custom slots weren’t properly creating their associated events when added. This should now behave as expected.

Economy Updates - May 26th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   New command - /money audit
    
    *   This command will allow you to track your most recent 20 economy money changes. Did someone steal from you? How much did you get from /work? It will all be tracked here.
        
    
*   New minigame - /chance-dice
    
    *   This minigame is all about luck... With a teeny bit of strategy. You need to roll dice, collect points and be the first to hit the winning number. The game takes place over multiple rounds but be careful, the more you roll, the higher the chance of hitting ☠️ and scoring 0 for that round!
        
    
*   New minigame - /turbotac
    
    *   TurboTac _(patent pending)_ is a new version of Tic Tac Toe where you can only have a total of 4 pieces on the board. This means that when you place your fifth piece, your oldest placed piece will be removed. This adds a new spin on the original game and should make for some interesting matches!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#major-release-custom-module-builder-beta-may-10th-2025)

Major Release: Custom Module Builder (Beta) - May 10th, 2025


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’re excited to announce the full release of the **Custom Module Builder**, a powerful new system that lets you design, build, and manage your own feature modules for your bot — all through a clean drag-and-drop interface!

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FmUmZ65gDMgemyhxRxFVN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d1c7fbd-06a9-470f-b5f1-d15c654fb9be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a598408e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#what-is-the-module-builder)

What is the Module Builder?

The Module Builder allows you to create **fully customizable modules** made up of **input blocks and sections**. These sections define configurable fields that your users can interact with — such as dropdowns, text inputs, toggles, and more.

Each input you add becomes a variable that can be referenced directly in your commands and events, giving you a flexible way to create dynamic behavior based on server-specific settings.

*   Drag and drop input blocks like **short text**, **channel select**, or **role select**
    
*   Group blocks into **sections** like "Command Settings" or "Moderation Settings"
    
*   Use the collected values inside commands/events using smart variables
    

With this system, you no longer need to hard-code settings — just let server owners configure them through BotPanel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FMxhyJOwjICgOJiGX7BNN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De986c287-8f0c-4be6-9e15-388d753de0ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6659eb5&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FtCfZf9WG0w9nKdH1g6qY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaa59c82-5d87-4cdf-ba56-60c0ac266020&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d718cac0&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252F29NB6RimkR1z0zxhjII1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42c372a7-e76b-47be-b599-d5e94be5946f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f932943&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#why-use-the-module-builder)

Why Use the Module Builder?

*   **BotPanel Integration** — Let users tweak your bot’s features for their specific server needs, without touching your source logic.
    
*   **Edit bot behavior without editing commands/events directly** — Perfect for separating config from code.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#beta-status-1)

Beta Status

The Module Builder is currently in **beta** and may contain bugs or unfinished elements.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#variable-and-formatting-improvements)

Variable & Formatting Improvements

*   Formatted the **timestamp variable** in the message delete event to use **seconds** instead of milliseconds (works better with Discord formatting).
    
*   Added two new variables:
    
    *   **numberWithCommas** – formats large numbers like `1,000,000`
        
    *   **numberWithDots** – formats large numbers like `1.000.000`
        
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#builder-improvements)

Builder Improvements

*   Increased the **block template limit** from 100 to 1000.
    
*   Updated the **server selector** in timed events to match the new scalable selector system.
    
*   Increased the **z-index** of the channel selector so it doesn’t get placed under other elements.
    
*   Added **"The Message"** option to the **React to Message** action.

*   Added guardrails to prevent invalid **permission bitfields** in edit actions.

*   Added the new **USE\_EXTERNAL\_SOUNDS** permission bit field.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#role--channel-selector-rework-april-17th-2025)

Role + Channel Selector Rework - April 17th, 2025


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Today we’ve reworked how role and channel selectors function throughout the dashboard to improve performance and usability.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#new-selector-system)

New Selector System

Users in 200+ servers were experiencing infinite loading issues when opening role/channel dropdowns. We've fixed this by introducing a new method:

*   Select a specific server before loading roles/channels
    
*   OR manually input a Role/Channel ID if you already know it
    

This makes selection faster and removes unnecessary load times on large bots.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#priority-hosting-now-available-march-29th-2025)

Priority Hosting Now Available - March 29th, 2025


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’re excited to introduce **Priority Hosting**, our new premium hosting tier designed for developers who need enhanced performance, stability, and influence.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#key-features-3)

Key Features

**Infrastructure**

*   Exclusive server pods (~10 bots per pod vs 1–2k standard)
    
*   AWS m8g.8xlarge with Graviton4 processors
    
*   32 vCPUs, 128 GiB memory, 15 Gbps bandwidth
    
*   Sub-1 minute downtime during updates
    
*   Enhanced API rate limits, 40k IOPS, 1,250 MB/s throughput
    

**Storage & Reliability**

*   365-day button/menu retention (vs 30 days)
    
*   Advanced back-off and monitoring systems
    

**Community & Access**

*   VIP Discord role + private Priority Hosting Member channels
    
*   Monthly Q&As with staff/founder
    
*   Early access to features via alpha.botghost.com
    
*   Priority bug fixes and feedback influence
    
*   Real-time downtime and maintenance alerts
    

**Subscription & Benefits**

*   $15/month, managed via Stripe
    
*   One subscription covers all bots on your account
    
*   Cancel anytime; benefits last through the billing cycle
    
*   7-day money-back guarantee
    
*   Enterprise-grade performance, optimized for high-traffic and large-scale bots
    
*   Improved reliability, multi-tasking, and latency handling
    

To learn more and upgrade, visit: [**https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/priohosting**](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/priohosting)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#why-does-priority-hosting-cost-extra-on-top-of-a-premium-subscription)

Why does Priority Hosting cost extra on top of a premium subscription?

Priority Hosting is designed primarily for larger bot developers with bots in thousands of servers who need **enterprise-grade performance and reliability**. The significantly higher server costs of the **AWS m8g.8xlarge instances with Graviton4 processors**, combined with the **drastically reduced bot density** (only ~10 bots per instance vs 1–2 thousand), requires additional investment beyond our standard premium subscription. This specialized infrastructure ensures your high-traffic bots receive the **dedicated resources, processing power, and reliability** needed to serve large communities — without performance degradation.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FDSpuW0JtW7nM34wffVTP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D060c13f5-05c0-4928-890a-8257f5993359&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d11cfcdf&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#server-migration-march-25th-2025)

Server Migration - March 25th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We recently undertook a server migration to move the bots to much larger more powerful servers. These servers are much more burstable and should provide more overhead for more resource intensive bots.

This was also done to make way for a new Priority Hosting update.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#mobile-builder-experimental)

Mobile Builder (Experimental)

You can now use the builder easily on mobile devices! This version includes a new layout optimized for smaller screens and better touch controls.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#how-to-enable)

How to Enable:

*   Head over to the **Builder**
    
*   Click **Settings**
    
*   Toggle **"Experimental Mobile Mode"**
    
*   The builder will automatically refresh with the new layout!
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FUo70kKDdUhKnHgFGOWJK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf47f659-16d8-4841-8e6f-3779277a25e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1009bc10&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#module-updates-march-23rd-2025)

Module Updates - March 23rd, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#translation)

Translation

*   Bot will respect the emojis selected and only attempt to translate when a configured emoji is used
    
*   Removed "Bot is thinking" API call as it was causing event delays
    
*   Added some additional error management
    
*   Updated the translation embed to use the new message block
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#moderation)

Moderation

*   Autopunishments have been adjusted. The previous system would only trigger an autopunishment ONCE, and it was expected that the bot creator would add additional autopunishments for greater and greater numbers of rule breaks. This system wasn't as intuitive as I had originally thought. Autopunishments now work by resetting the number of warns/mutes when a configured autopunishment triggers. For example if a user received 3 warns which triggers a timeout, his autopunishment warn counter will RESET so that the autopunishment can trigger again in the future.
    
*   The temporary Role and Ban timed event has been updated to check every 20 seconds, down from 3 minutes.
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#economy-module-updates-march-21th-2025)

Economy Module Updates - March 21th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Some updates have been released for the Economy Module:

*   Changed all "Send Error Log" blocks to Embed replies so that our error logs stop getting spammed
    
*   Safe mode slightly changed - the only way to disable safe mode now is to earn 10k or more
    
*   Lucky Box logic in /shop buy changed to match on itemid instead of name. This will mean that Lucky Box functionality no longer breaks if you change the name of the box in the dashboard
    
*   Lucky Box (slight) rework - Lucky boxes have had a rework that removes the ability to purchase multiple boxes at once. The command logic for this was clunky and caused issues with balance, so now Lucky Boxes can only be purchased one at a time.
    
*   Lottery fix for 10+ entrees. It should no longer give the EOF error when announcing the winnings
    
*   Timed event for Lottery set to "Run once for all servers" to accomodate BotPanel
    
*   Scratchcard and Matchpairs have been updated to use the Emoji field on buttons, making the emojis standardised across platforms
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#botghost-fixes-updates-march-17th-2025)

BotGhost Fixes/Updates - March 17th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Fixed an issue where 2 reward codes were being generated for GhostBuddy voting. If you got both, enjoy.
    
*   Fixed a bug affecting the additional roles field in add/remove role actions.
    
*   Fixed a dashboard crash when trying to edit a Role or Channel menu using the edit component action.
    
*   Resolved an issue where adding a 5th server would sometimes incorrectly enforce a 4-server limit.
    
*   You can now edit buttons on ephemeral (hidden) messages—only for buttons attached to the original interaction.
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#botghost-fixes-updates-march-4th-2025)

BotGhost Fixes/Updates - March 4th, 2025


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Added the channel component to the thread delete event.
    
*   `Set Variable`, `Delete Variable`, and `Equation Variable` no longer rely on API requests to retrieve member IDs, reducing 404 errors.
    
*   These actions also no longer require API requests for channel IDs, further minimizing errors.
    
*   Fixed an issue where events requiring a server ID would not save properly when "Run once for all servers" was enabled.
    
*   The `{Role.}` variable now works correctly in role events.
    
*   `Add Role` and `Remove Role` actions now support cross-server role management.
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#top.gg-autoposter-and-botghost-updates-february-28th-2025)

Bug Fixes, Module Changes - February 27th, 2025


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**We have released some bug fixes and updates to modules. Details below:**

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#economy)

Economy:

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#minor-changes)

Minor Changes:

*   Lottery Event is set to "Run once for a specific server" by default
    
*   Various fixes to /rob bank. It should be more reliable when users join the heist with more validation. Percentage split also adjusted
    
*   Blackjack money added should not be incorrect in some cases anymore
    
*   /ec cooldowns will now show you your cooldowns in a better format
    
*   /rob player now steals a percentage of their holding balance, making it more effective on users with a higher balance
    
*   /ec admin - When uploading emojis the error message is more descriptive. 90% of failures are usually because the emoji already exists on the bot, but the command was not clear on how to solve this issue.
    

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#major-changes)

Major Changes:

*   Many of the minigames that relied on editing the component array via API have been completely revamped to use the new Edit Component Block (yay!). This has resulted in significant performance improvements across the board with these games. Notably matchpairs and hangman
    
*   /tictac - Updated to use the Edit Component block
    
*   /matchpairs - Updated to use the Edit Component block
    
*   /hangman - Updated to use the the Edit Component block
    
*   /scratchcard - Updated to use the Edit Component block
    

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#new-games)

New Games:

*   The economy module is a gift that keeps on giving! In this update we have added TWO new minigames.
    
*   /lightout - Lights Out is a puzzle game where the objective is to turn off all the lights on a grid. Pressing a button toggles that light and the adjacent lights directly above, below, and to either side.
    
*   /mastermind - The goal of Mastermind is for the Codebreaker (you) to guess the exact colors and positions of a secret code created by the Codemaker (the bot) in as few attempts as possible.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#weather)

Weather:

*   There was an issue with the weather module where users who ran the command that were too far behind (or ahead) of UTC+0 would see a discrepancy in the Day + Timestamp in the 3 day forecast. To correct this we have added the option for users to select a default timezone that they reside in when running the command. This will show up inside the embed to inform the user that they should set a default timezone. It can be reset using the command as well.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#invite-tracker)

Invite Tracker:

*   The /invites-leaderboard had some issues in the command tree which caused it to run slowly. We have redesigned it completely to drastically improve performance
    
*   A bug in the Leaves Handler event has also been fixed
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#status-module)

Status Module:

*   Fixed an issue where the status could cause some error log messages to appear
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#botghost-updates-february-26th-2025)

BotGhost Updates - February 26th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#botghost-api-and-bug-fixes)

BotGhost API & Bug Fixes

*   **Increased API Limit** - Premium users now have a raised API limit of **100 requests per 10 seconds** (previously 20).
    
*   **Fixed Button/Menu Interactions** - Resolved an issue where interactions were being deleted even if used in the past 30 days.
    
*   **Fixed Webhook Event Loops** - Loops inside webhook events no longer return a Custom Events error.
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#webhook-object-updates-february-25th-2025)

Webhook Object Updates - February 25th, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've got a few quick updates for you, along with a quick reminder about our **40% off sale** ending soon!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#new-webhook-object-beta-only)

New Webhook Object (beta only)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can now use the `{Webhook}` object to access:

*   `**{Webhook.body}**` – View the data sent with a webhook.
    
*   `**{Webhook.url}**` – Get the URL that triggered the webhook.
    
*   `**{Webhook.headers}**` – Access the headers for advanced integrations. This opens up more possibilities for interacting with external services!
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#edit-component-action-february-10th-2025)

Edit Component Action - February 10th, 2025


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Today we are releasing the edit component action to the beta servers. This button allows you to edit buttons and select menus attached to a previously sent message.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#edit-component-action)

Edit Component Action

Simply select any amount of buttons or menu and you can then change the settings of them after they have been sent. For example this allows you to:

*   Disable a button/menu after it is sent
    
*   Change the style of a button
    
*   Change the label of a button
    
*   Add options to a select menu
    
*   Change component ordering on a message
    
*   Remove components from a message
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252Fd6ew1WWoDTT1QmyJlJQF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5ff95ec-529d-4dda-96db-a6a89a399b0f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=767f1cb4&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#example-commands)

Example Commands

To help you all understand how this block works <@225647195771240448> has created 2 example commands which you can import:

*   **A Basic Edit Button Command (CMD\_8c136d10-75a3-438b-a8b6-30a0d4458413)** - A basic command showing how to disable buttons and reset their state.
    
*   **Lights Out Game (CMD\_302d7ca9-c9ee-4df5-9eb3-de384eb19686)** - An advanced command that lets you play the Lights Out game where the goal is to turn out all the lights with the minimum amount of clicks.
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#hiding-of-old-reply-blocks)

Hiding of Old Reply Blocks

I have also hidden by default the old outdated reply blocks. If you still want to use them, you can go to settings and untick **Hide Legacy Reply Actions**

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FYYmU6CQBGxdRebAsJmYs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e32de31-a2ee-4c80-9370-eb8bc0fdcdb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fa4c164&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#qol-additions--builder-settings-january-30th-2025)

QOL Additions + Builder Settings - January 30th, 2025


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#builder-settings)

Builder Settings

Added the start of a builder settings page. This page houses various settings and defaults that change how the builder works. More settings will be added later, for now we have added:

*   **Auto Save** - automatically saves the command or event every X seconds if possible.
    
*   **Color Settings** - change the default colors of every block in the builder
    
*   **Block Defaults** - added a default color option for embeds and default condition type for the comparison condition
    

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FSG4UiRgiPlqIezQ0GM1l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D023a00e3-7f56-471a-82ca-3b7a7a962121&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e7685c1&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FLUnNegn3pyGRBwEEYpLg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbec01932-278b-44bf-8a1b-ba51b3e7bc48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdae1bbf&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1194150090-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FlqJCocmqzKryU9USp1nO%252Fuploads%252FSsGy4gfyyhJdzK0mvXlX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc123a92d-318e-4e5c-bae2-c15883034ed3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b1203f2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#qol-improvements)

QOL Improvements

We have also added a few QOL improvements throughout the dashboard.

*   **Module Search Bar** \- Added a search bar to the modules page. You can now search modules/builders by name.
    
*   **Note block**\- Added a new note block. This block lets you set a title, description and color and is useful for documenting how your command/event works.
    
*   **Last Saved Warning** - Added a last saved warning if you havent saved in a while.
    
*   **Set Comparison type before adding** - Set comparison type of comparison condition before adding it.
    
*   **Set default comparison condition type** - Set the default comparison condition type to equals to.
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#bug-fixes-january-28th-2025)

Bug Fixes - January 28th, 2025


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Fixed a bug with the {Invite} Object. It should now work with {Invite\[ID\].property} as expected.
    
*   Fixed the Role delete event.
    
*   Fixed a bug that caused buttons to not send on large commands
    
*   Fixed a bug that caused a visual error when deleting slots in custom modules.
    
*   Fixed a bug that caused error logs to not be sent to the error handling tree inside of events.
    
*   Fixed a bug with variables inside of the add/remove role action.
    
*   Fixed a bug with errors not being sent when a member could not be retrieved inside of the add/remove role action.
    
*   Fixed some bugs resulting around free limits switching up after sending an update to your bot. (Command limits, guild limits, activity warnings etc).
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#module-updates-bug-fixes-january-3rd-2025)

Module Updates/Bug Fixes - January 3rd, 2025


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We have released some updates/bug fixes to the following modules:

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#counting)

Counting

*   Fixed an issue with the webhook setting where the webhook was not being created successfully
    
*   Added a check to stop the count increasing if the webhook failed to send
    
*   Added an automatic channel slowmode if the 5 second cooldown option is toggled on
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#youtube)

YouTube

*   Corrected issue that could cause errors in the error-log if the API query did not return the correct status code
    
*   YouTube Module compatibility with BotPanel
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#verification)

Verification

*   Changed the limit and restrictions on how long someone can go unverified in a server before being kicked. New limits are - 60 seconds min, 850 seconds (~15 minutes) max
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/changelog/2025#weather-1)

Weather

*   Fixed an issue where mph was being displayed for Wind Gusts despite kph being selected
    
*   Updated the module to use the new Send a Message block, making edits to the weather embed much, much easier
    
*   Various formatting improvements
    

**Head to the respective module page via the** [**BotGhost Dashboard**](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/modules)
 **and hit Update Module and Save Changes to apply the changes.**

Last updated 5 months ago
