# Emoji Manager | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMBbrbi6OtYIbhfzDe3BB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8d5913f-4fbc-4a67-bb5c-c91b24bf8117&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6068537&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Emoji Manager](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/c2cde45e-a789-4b31-ad44-5c7ceca5a5cd/emojimanager)
 module will allow you to view a list of custom emojis, create a new one in your server, restrict the use of an existing emoji, and copy an emoji from a different server to yours.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#settings)

Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#permissions-setup)

Permissions Setup

This section is how you can configure all the permission based necessities for the emoji commands.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F5u0fyhUm0svbZwzXvZ5l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd491d132-206c-4da1-b62f-6f216375b798&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d55b260&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#sync-default-permissions)

**Sync Default Permissions**

This option when enabled, will force users to have the manage expressions permission along with the role based permissions in the rest of the settings.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#role-permissions-selection-type)

**Role Permissions: Selection Type**

Type

Details

Only selected roles

If this option is selected then only the selected roles in the field below will be allowed to use the emoji manager commands.

All roles except

If this option is chosen instead, then all roles in the field below will be the ones which aren't able to use the commands, and the rest of the server roles can.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#role-permissions-roles)

**Role Permissions: Roles**

This field is where you can specify and select the server roles that are going to be applied towards the setting above.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#commands-setup)

Commands Setup

Define how many emojis should display while using the /emojis-view command, enable logging, and select the desired channel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FEdHLOF32ZZKPbJ6KwDEo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df338b632-820f-4a97-8c81-c0ef5d2f0ee4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a516186&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#emojis-view-emojis-per-page)

**Emojis-View: Emojis per Page**

This field is where you can input the amount of emojis shown when using the emoji-view command. There is a maximum of 25 emojis and this field only accepts integers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#enable-logging)

**Enable Logging**

Enable this option to log all actions / changes applied to your server's emoji in a channel. This includes the usage of all commands except `/emojis-view`.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#logging-channel)

**Logging Channel**

Select a channel in which actions of the module will be logged. _This setting is only visible with_ [Enable Logging](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#enable-logging)
 _enabled._

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#commands)

Commands


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Emoji Manager module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FAcRy983iiQ2kPB0fBi7u%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9424e8c3-b8e7-4bd4-a97a-8b1ee0349f49&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b66bf923&sv=2)

/emojis-view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#emojis-view)

This command allows you to view all created emojis that were made via this module and other server emojis.

/emoji-create[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#emoji-create)

With this command you can create emojis and add them to the server's emojis.

/emoji-restrict[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#emoji-restrict)

This command will restrict certain users based off the roles they have from using the commands.

/emoji-copy[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/emoji-manager#emoji-copy)

This command can copy an emoji from another server and upload it to your server.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Auto-React | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FwaF9Jt8bPMCF7UJR0sTQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ef1e6e1-8de4-4d6c-8c52-6084c096c136&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2c86e89&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

BotGhost provides an [Auto-React module](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/d12ee953-765f-47bd-b855-b9dd18fe052e/auto-react)
 for its users. This module will allow you to automatically add reactions on newly sent messages.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#basic-setup)

Basic Setup

In this area, you can view and modify the settings of the Auto-React module. Below you may find some information on each setting of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Felt8dWvc4Jk7XOgsFqjS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28fcb162-09d0-4863-a65e-e29bd501c2ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80438f47&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#enabled-channels)

Enabled Channels

This setting allows you to enable automatic reactions in specific channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#reaction-emojis)

Reaction Emojis

This setting allows you to set the emoji to react with. You can use default and custom emojis.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#condition-setup)

Condition Setup

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FHCTGk4lDVWVYpRttx8Ah%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D628b4f57-c1c8-432c-abaf-fa612a4a9aab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=606a8665&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#ignore-embeds)

Ignore Embeds

This setting allows you to only react to messages that include plain text.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#allowed-roles)

Allowed Roles

This setting allows you to specify what roles the author of the message must have for automatic reactions. By refraining from setting any roles, all users will be subject to the filter regardless of their roles.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#check-for-words)

Check for Words

This setting allows you to specify what words the message must have for automatic reactions. By refraining from setting any words, all messages will be subject to the filter regardless of their content.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#events)

Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Auto-React module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fu8qoDEEG66h8ngdwqCly%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4adeaf94-5f86-4ed4-9323-dd6a06b60be6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=887d6be3&sv=2)

Auto-React[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/auto-react#auto-react)

This event is the core of the module: it triggers upon newly sent messages and ensures to filter all messages and automatically react based on the settings you set.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Discord Automod | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPtBx2N1jid3MKz1EgnP2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7b49c06-070a-406f-9c70-0f9b6138dc41&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ed2dee1&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Discord Automod](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/e8564ca2-721a-4257-885a-43d740a67296/discordautomod)
 module will allow you to edit, add and remove rules from your discord server's automod through your BotGhost bot as well as give you the method to get the new 'Automod Badge' for your bot.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#settings)

Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#basic-settings)

Basic Settings

In this area, you can setup and customize the general settings for the commands and events of this module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FN8gS33bQ2CuPhMCpHE9u%252FScreenshot_3-7-2024_234249_dashboard.botghost.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D995cf707-8c45-4e83-97db-86d39aba27aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24e7ed7a&sv=2)

**Allowed Roles**

Here you can select roles which can edit, add & remove automod rules, users without these roles will not be able to remove or add rules.

**Logging Channel**

Here you can select the channel in which automod logs are sent to, users who trigger the automod will also trigger a message to be sent to the channel specified here.

**Default Moderator Message**

Here you can set the default moderator message that is displayed to users who break one of the defined automod rules.

**Whitelisted Roles**

Here you can define some roles that will not trigger the automod, users with these roles will be completely immune to the automod rules and will not trigger the module.

**Whitelisted Channels**

Here you can select some channels that the automod will ignore, messages sent in these channels that would normally trigger the automod will be ignored.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#punishment-settings)

Punishment Settings

Here you can customise the punishments members get when they break one of the automod rules or set it to a set amount of rules to be broken before punishment is given.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FD9387ENLZEi70zwGNYBX%252FScreenshot_3-7-2024_235353_dashboard.botghost.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1cea3eb2-7d02-4a1b-99c0-9dd5ffd53558&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df18f542&sv=2)

**Broken Rules Needed**

Here you can define the amount of rules needed to be broken by a user before punishment is given.

**Punishment Type**

Here you can change the type of punishment the bot will give when a user reaches the defined number of broken rules needed to trigger a punishment. Below are the punishment types you can select:

Punishment Types

Timeout Member

Kick Member

Ban Member

**Punishment Length**

Here you can change the duration for the 'Timeout Member' punishment option.

**Checked Rule**

Here you can enter the name of the automod rule the event will issue punishments upon. **If you leave the input empty, all automod filters will count!**

**Send a DM**

**H**ere you can enable/disable DMs being sent to the user upon punishment.

**DM Message**

Here you can edit the message that is sent to users when they have been punished if you have enabled the '**Send a DM'** setting.

To save the punishment settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another punishment.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#viewing-active-punishments)

Viewing Active Punishments

You can edit all active punishments through a list right below the menu.

To save the edits you made on the punishment settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FAB4uuzjqF7l3UcxVgNxe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D156c10d4-a76a-418c-be10-874a944194cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=83ae76fe&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#commands)

Commands


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Discord Automod module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FS8cUqtFbWmmx9lojrI7Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09864247-04c1-45f2-aaa4-0472d02a664c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=908ac00f&sv=2)

**/discord-automod**[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#discord-automod)

The discord-automod command allows you to edit, add or remove Discord automod rules with your bot in your server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FujBl0JpoadWhlzXi7taF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4bacd12-eefe-4aef-b8bc-2bf1e7f7a9b7&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=659649f2&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#events)

Events


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Discord Automod module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module. All punishments will be ordered by the number in which they were created.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FexKvpTOxEohFkgbhjRaI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db94e6b06-6aa7-4a63-a899-e3991f41ce3f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71943f43&sv=2)

Punishment #...[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/discord-automod#punishment)

Once you add an automatic punishment, the corresponding event will be created. This will handle the newly created punishment.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Sticky Messages | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1EYEpH5Z8KKW6dxQ27oC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ae912fd-f75a-4a4b-aaa6-9125ba095586&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e656f4e2&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Sticky Messages](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/1acdd900-f547-481f-b1ef-725384b5884b/stickymessages)
 module allows you to send a message to a channel of your choice after a number of messages. This is great for highlighting important information or adding frequent reminders!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#settings)

Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#setup)

Setup

Here you can configure all the settings for the sticky messages module from changing the actual message, the frequency and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FLzUMcDSqIsU7QvbJwNpQ%252Fimage_2024-07-09_112831757.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16f96859-9f7e-4929-8d27-ddfe2f99b4d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e81be6e2&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#manager-role)

**Manager Role**

In this dropdown, you can select a role to allow users with this role to add / remove messages set with the module.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#default-sticky-message)

**Default Sticky Message**

This field is where you can change the default message that's sent to the channel after a number of messages as defined in the module settings below.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#repost-message-count)

**Repost Message Count**

In this field you can change how frequent the message is sent. The number that's input is the basis for how many messages until the sticky message is sent. The default value for this is set to 10 and the field only accepts integers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#show-author)

**Show Author**

This toggle allows you to enable / disable the ability to show the sticky message author in the embed message. The author is the user who originally posted the sticky message and only works in embeds.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#add-reactions)

**Add Reactions**

With this toggle, you can enable / disable the option for the bot to add a specified or default reaction to the sticky message when it is sent.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#reaction-emoji)

**Reaction Emoji**

In this section, you can set the emoji that is added as a reaction to the sticky message, if the above toggle is enabled. You can use both custom emoji's or basic discord emoji's for this. You can find a guide [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/getting-started/standard-practices/advanced-practices#how-can-i-get-a-custom-emojis-id)
 on how to get the ID and name of a custom emoji.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#commands)

Commands


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This area is where you can enable / disable the sticky post command as well as configure the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FciGckNsW6mpRBorc7l1G%252Fimage_2024-07-09_112753471.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9f7c274-759d-415e-9151-88d4fa814693&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a1b0af49&sv=2)

/sticky-post[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#sticky-post)

When triggered this command will allow you to send a new sticky message to any channel you select from the command option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FRARMXPgIGhXRdyUwLtuj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D413abc11-7a9a-4aaa-ba78-ed7e15adba10&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=758088d&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#events)

Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Sticky Messages module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FlHvdir035OgVihIOvcEH%252Fimage_2024-07-09_112804930.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da660a2f9-23fa-40ba-b263-ce9eb636c69e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7852e758&sv=2)

Sticky Messages (Poster)[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#sticky-messages-poster)

This event will count the messages in the channels and send the designated sticky message when it reaches the defined message count as set in the settings above.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#settings)
    
*   [Setup](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/sticky-messages#setup)

# Action Events | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/action-events.md)
.

Action Events are a category of pre-built, powerful events in BotGhost that combine multiple actions into a single block. They are designed to simplify the creation of common bot features, allowing you to accomplish complex tasks without needing multiple custom event blocks.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPQX9CXx3R4QarmLV2hXp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D345eb1f9-af5f-4644-819c-31bf93919e3d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1fa218c3&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/action-events#action-event-block)

Action Event Block


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8WatmpZSfLh3U2Ejm8kw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a66d490-8734-4aac-b7bd-6befcbdf4dcc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74c080a7&sv=2)

All action events come with a pre-added block where you can configure settings for the event or other automated actions. In the screenshot above for example, the Auto Role on Join Block is a default block that appears on the Auto Role on Join custom event. It alllows you to add one or more roles to a specific member on join and configure details.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/action-events#available-action-events)

Available Action Events


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Event

Information

Auto Role on Join

Adds a role when a user joins the server.

Twitch Stream Online

The event will run when a streamer goes live on Twitch.

YouTube Video Upload

Triggers when a new video is posted on a YouTube channel.

Last updated 8 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Available Action Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/action-events#available-action-events)

# IFTTT | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FGk57sAONqUgYbQ6oKqJP%252F1280px-IFTTT_Logo.svg.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D67ba4c21-da18-4328-b872-892cf87f1a13&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fbc5de1&sv=2)

IFTTT is short for "If This Then That" and allows you to link up to 700 different apps and services, including Twitter, DropBox, Twitch, and Google Sheets. IFTTT works by creating applets with triggers, queries, and actions.

The IFTTT x BotGhost link allows you to trigger IFTTT applets through custom commands and events, as well as triggering BotGhost custom events when other services trigger fires.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#linking-ifttt-to-botghost)

Linking IFTTT to BotGhost


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To get started with IFTTT you must first link your IFTTT account to your BotGhost account. To do so head over to the [BotGhost IFTTT page](https://ifttt.com/botghost)
 and click **Connect** to begin this process.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FiVDqAw1vcnZ6vOMb4quf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0337a28b-cf5d-422e-9954-e83485cb1d1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e2257e5&sv=2)

This will prompt you to log in and redirect you to the BotGhost dashboard where you must give permission to link your BotGhost account to IFTTT. Click **Authorize** to confirm the BotGhost x IFTTT link.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F56k9Ag7VyupQAH2b9UVK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D529ab779-60ea-4c3c-9a24-d5e654102f0e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3069274&sv=2)

Once complete your accounts are now linked. You can now begin creating Applets using BotGhost triggers, queries, and actions on IFTTT.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#applets)

**Applets**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Applets are the backbone of IFTTT. Applets use a customizable script to link two or more apps that normally remain separate. Within BotGhost, we use IFTTT Applets to either trigger custom events or trigger other services actions on IFTTT.

To create an Applet, once again head over to the [BotGhost IFTTT service page](https://ifttt.com/botghost)
 and click **Create.**

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FDRGFqafYTBaAPQhEuike%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D087ab478-1674-4d4e-ba4f-7b98d9c8b9c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=172b4f4a&sv=2)

You will then be prompted to Add at least one trigger and action. Triggers are what causes an applet to run, whilst actions are the end result of an action. Within BotGhost, the IFTTT trigger is executed through an Action block in custom commands or events.

In your applet, click **Add** in the If This section and select the **Action Block triggered** IFTTT trigger.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FP2VigRk5RrQ0iI47bkDh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29f83ac2-b51f-46d8-8983-9a7df42cd10e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a82e062&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#action-block-triggered-ifttt-triggers)

Action Block Triggered (IFTTT Triggers)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Action Block Triggered IFTTT Trigger executes an Applet when an **Execute an IFTTT Trigger** action block in a custom command or event is run.

On IFTTT the Action Block Triggered Trigger has three options.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FdqvUtLkwMriHKRVB44Nh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D160a8369-97ae-4bf2-9e0d-536315eb4ab1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80c7c2ca&sv=2)

First, select your linked BotGhost account in the **BotGhost account** dropdown.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#action-id)

Action ID

The action ID field is what links your action in BotGhost to your trigger on IFTTT. This field must match the Action ID field in an **Execute an IFTTT Trigger** action in a BotGhost custom command or event. You can name this action ID anything you wish.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOWVrnsFl9TAQ2Hho0TiC%252Fifttt.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87091ac0-42cb-43e5-b824-5078702e5c7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cb57c42&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#bot)

Bot

Select the bot you wish to trigger the action from.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#execute-an-ifttt-trigger-action)

Execute an IFTTT Trigger Action

Once you have set up your trigger on IFTTT, you can execute it through an **Execute an IFTTT trigger** action block in a custom command or event on BotGhost. To do so, first, create a custom command or event and drag in the action.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FIXj9q03WoVx1wu6VfC1N%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98d27e25-297c-4615-90e2-36ba67ec581d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=69ed06e2&sv=2)

In the action, set the **Action ID** to the same Action ID you specified in your trigger on IFTTT.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOWVrnsFl9TAQ2Hho0TiC%252Fifttt.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87091ac0-42cb-43e5-b824-5078702e5c7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cb57c42&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#variables)

Variables

You can pass information from your command or event to the action triggered in your Applet through IFTTT ingredients. The **Action Block Triggered** IFTTT Trigger has 10 variable slots you can use to pass through as ingredients. All BotGhost variables can be used in these slots including custom variables.

These variables will come through as ingredients named Variable1, Variable2, Variable3... in any connected IFTTT action in your applets.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FNt93rB1gmTWh2TocvEDZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D98a20bea-a970-4271-9f00-d9b006d99483&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29804388&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FdoSpzJMyJqaDxrsADW3I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35f41e7b-7135-45c9-b08a-1970cb157971&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9126e1d&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#trigger-a-custom-event-ifttt-actions)

Trigger a Custom Event (IFTTT Actions)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In IFTTT actions are the end result of an Applet. They are what are run when triggered by an IFTTT trigger. In BotGhost, the IFTTT Action is the execution of a custom event.

Once again create an applet and set a trigger of your choosing. Click the **Add** Section in Then That and choose BotGhost. Click on **Trigger a Custom Event** to add the BotGhost IFTTT Action to your Applet.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjgusZiZKk86uudZOPTKN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaf2524a-1c40-47f3-bab9-7672dfd636c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20fb6d7a&sv=2)

You will then be shown the options for the Action. Once again select your BotGhost account and input the Bot ID of the bot you wish to trigger the custom event of.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#event-id)

Event ID

Similarly to the IFTTT Trigger, we must provide an ID that is the same in BotGhost and IFTTT. If you have not done so already, head over to your BotGhost and create a Custom Event with the type **When an IFTTT Action is executed.**

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FzhBUDkd1F1rFwLvlxirH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13a70be3-3e75-4687-b3d4-79e95586efc5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10d4a146&sv=2)

You will need to input an IFTTT Event ID and then select that Event in your IFTTT Action.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXA3cLChsZPk4lA8MfruS%252Fiftttt2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D000dd65b-0b53-4aed-a54f-53d727d08a36&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5eabc994&sv=2)

Enter an event ID and then select that same event in your IFTTT Action.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJ889K3aipyxxE8nnZ5UG%252Fifttt1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5061b8dd-deba-4fac-bb39-5b630eab2d36&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a208b4ed&sv=2)

Then make sure to enter your server ID in the Discord Server ID field in your event. You can then continue to build out your custom event like normal.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#ifttt-event-variables)

IFTTT Event Variables

You can pass variables through to your BotGhost custom event using the 10 IFTTT Variable slots. You can input your text or use ingredients from the execution action.

Each variable has its corresponding variable in the event builder. For example, any text or ingredients you put into the **Variable 1 slot**, can be used in your custom event as **{ifttt\_variable1}**.

Last updated 2 years ago

# Timed Events | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events.md)
.

The timed events module allows users to setup events to be triggered on the specified days/times selected. This is super handy for reminders or other important messages that need to be sent every so often.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here you can customise the settings for the module, create new events, edit events and more.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#timezone)

Timezone

The timezone section allows you to specify the timezone you wish the events to trigger in. By default it will be set to your current timezone on your computer/device.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#add-a-new-timed-event)

Add a new timed event

Below you can see a image of the event creator. Here you can select the trigger time, trigger day, name and type of event.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhDjYIb1gv3D6GBzuXn3q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77e618f9-dc88-4713-8651-f234e953177b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef09efbf&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#event-type)

Event Type

Here you can select between 'Schedule' or 'Interval'. By default it is set to 'Interval'. Selecting the 'Interval' type will allow you to make the event trigger on a interval (Run events every X amount of seconds, minutes, hours or days. The minimum interval is 10 seconds.) (Green = active Red = Disabled)

Setting this to Schedule will display some new options:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fd0lGatVZdFR3POa7A2oH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5cfb843e-0e54-4f1e-8f0c-945744754df8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6e75133&sv=2)

Here you can set the event to tigger every X day(s) at X time. Example, run the event every Monday at 12:00:00PM. (Green = active Red = Disabled)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#active-timed-events)

Active Timed Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here you can find all of your created timed events, you will be able to modify each one by clicking on the event.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvPi9K3K0quIzHN9hxvSA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d256e57-afa6-4403-995c-a157240dd6aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=197e2a1&sv=2)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#settings)
    
*   [Timezone](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#timezone)
    
*   [Add a new timed event](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#add-a-new-timed-event)
    
*   [Event Type](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#event-type)
    
*   [Active Timed Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events#active-timed-events)

# Modmail | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8ON64yxy6qAsTL9yElv0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8dd5586d-4cc8-4a22-be6a-48b6a07adf32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb862647&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Modmail](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/249b4aee-5617-4985-b60b-be262e567fc7/modmail)
 module allows users to send a Direct Message to your bot to open a form thread in a form channel of your choice to contact server staff privately, or report server members and more.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#settings)

Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#settings-1)

Settings

Here you can configure the settings for the modmail module, from changing the DM Messages to selecting the form channel you would like it to be posted in.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FshgkeLIRHjhv9YRR5YUR%252Fimage_2024-07-07_212652574.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78ab5a6b-8a15-4317-9b8d-1a64e4128f0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=455140d&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#receive-requests)

**Receive Requests**

This option is enabled by default and disabling this setting will stop users from opening a modmail thread and instead return a closed message when they direct message your bot.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#form-channel)

**Form Channel**

Here you must paste your forum channels ID to allow users to open modmail threads, you can create a forum channel in your discord server, for a guide on how to get a channel ID you can check [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/getting-started/standard-practices/advanced-practices#how-can-i-get-a-channel-id)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#dm-message-title)

**DM Message Title**

This field is where you can edit the direct message title which is sent to users upon contacting your bot via direct messages.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#dm-message-description)

**DM Message Description**

Here you can edit the message that is sent to the user upon contacting your bot via DMs. All [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 may be used.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#ban-command)

Ban Command

This is where you can configure the settings for the `/modmail-ban` command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2bLRt58xPrQQ1nov3fBP%252Fimage_2024-07-07_213041071.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e97e445-4429-45f4-bb1f-34349afd3fd2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b821bfac&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#enable-ban-command)

**Enable Ban Command**

This toggle is where you can enable/disable the ability for staff to use the `/modmail-ban` command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#select-the-needed-permissions)

Select The Needed Permissions

This dropdown section is where you can change the permissions for use of the `/modmail-ban` command, the default value of this is set to **Administrator** but can be changed to:

Permission

Details

Administrator

Requires the administrator permission in your server.

Server Manager

Requires the manage server permission.

Moderator

Requires the manage permissions.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#ban-message)

**Ban Message**

In this field, you can set the message that is displayed to a user when they attempt to make a modmail thread after they have been banned from using modmail.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#commands)

Commands


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Modmail module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FcCsGPzZGDGT1iU3jnjmP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc38fad9d-8080-4c77-be59-30665358329e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fba8beb&sv=2)

/modmail-ban[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#modmail-ban)

When triggered, this command will restrict a selected users ability to use the modmail system resulting in a ban message being displayed upon trying to open a new modmail thread.

/modmail-clear[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#modmail-clear)

When triggered this command will clear the modmail data for a user allowing them to use the modmail system again, this is useful incase the system breaks and acts as though a user has a thread already open.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#events)

Events


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Modmail module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhKyuqlF50mdyLTZCZPXH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9dd6b69f-d7d2-4a5f-bf51-db2221beb8ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eee9fcee&sv=2)

Modmail[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#modmail)

This is the main event which detects when a user sends a DM to your bot and starts a thread. Here you can edit the event and customise it to your liking and add onto the pre-existing functionalities of the module.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#settings)
    
*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#settings-1)
    
*   [Ban Command](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#ban-command)
    
*   [Commands](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#commands)
    
*   [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/modmail#events)
    

Was this helpful?

# Polls Filter | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FW9gvaGyAo3hd6HdYBZaI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D879a0750-2167-4c02-b361-75266cc2855a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1ea98be&sv=2)

The [Polls Filter module](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/5631dcc3-4ef8-49ee-8ab0-7dc763ad44ff/pollsfilter)
 allows you to filter newly sent messages that contain polls.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#settings)

Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the settings of the Polls Filter module. Below you may find some information on each setting of the module.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#bot-response)

Bot Response

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FQa5zJHY3wB94usYkVMU9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25f70e7d-379d-413d-8354-6c3234c66f0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c71613ef&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#delete-message)

Delete message

This setting allows you to automatically delete the filtered message.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#timeout-user)

Timeout User

This setting allows you to automatically mute the author of the filtered message for a specified number of seconds.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#timeout-member)

Timeout Member

This setting allows you to customize how long, in seconds, the author of the filtered message should be muted. _This setting is only visible with_ [_Timeout User_](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#timeout-user)
 _enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#send-a-message-when-the-filter-is-triggered)

Send a message when the filter is triggered

This setting allows you to automatically send a specified message to the channel the message was filtered in, and optionally delete it after a specified number of seconds.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#message)

Message

This setting allows you to customize the message that should be sent to the channel the message was filtered in. _This setting is only visible with_ [_Send a message when the filter is triggered_](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#send-a-message-when-the-filter-is-triggered)
 _enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#delete-notification)

Delete Notification

This setting allows you to customize how long, in seconds, the specified message should be visible before it gets deleted. To ensure the message does not get deleted, set this setting to `0`. _This setting is only visible with_ [_Send a message when the filter is triggered_](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#send-a-message-when-the-filter-is-triggered)
 _enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#send-a-dm-when-the-filter-is-triggered)

Send a DM when the filter is triggered

This setting allows you to automatically direct message the author of the filtered message.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#message-1)

Message

This setting allows you to customize the direct message that should be sent to the author of the filtered message. _This setting is only visible with_ [_Send a DM when the filter is triggered_](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#send-a-dm-when-the-filter-is-triggered)
 _enabled._

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#filters)

Filters

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FTvWuGrpZfbi9S5AT0POx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b374e8a-09d0-499d-87b0-38327be827f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52b3dba7&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#channel-restrictions)

Channel Restrictions

This setting allows you to customize what channels can and cannot contain polls.

Restriction Type

Information

No channel restrictions

Server members will be able to send polls everywhere.

Enable for all channels except...

Server members will be able to send polls in all channels except the channels provided in the menu below.

Disable for all channels except...

Server members will be able to send polls only in channels provided in the menu below.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#role-restrictions)

Role Restrictions

This setting allows you to customize what roles can and cannot send polls.

Restriction Type

Information

No role restrictions

All server members will be able to send polls.

Enable for all channels except...

All server members except those with the roles provided in the menu below will be able to send polls.

Disable for all channels except...

Only server members with the roles provided in the menu will be able to send polls.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#events)

Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Polls Filter module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJZX9kUT7OQBljUvmV950%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded38a2f4-46b6-441d-8d0e-34b16f7d71b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=623a6b52&sv=2)

Polls Filter[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/polls-filter#polls-filter)

This event is the core of the module: it triggers upon newly sent messages and ensures to filter all messages that contain polls based on the settings you set.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited command / event will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Reaction Roles | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FsTdnN13VRwx29bRY5IlB%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-09%2520212426.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40bb7b01-17bb-4156-ae77-6a68b3251630&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a30056&sv=2)

The Reaction Role module allows you to configure messages that allow users to assign and remove roles by reacting to a message.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#common-issues)

Common Issues


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Experiencing issues with the module? Check out the common issues below. If your issue is not listed in this page, make sure your module is updated to the latest version. If you are still experiencing issues with the module, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#the-bot-is-not-reacting-to-the-message)

**The bot is not reacting to the message**

If the bot is not adding the first reaction to the message, try the following steps:

1

Make sure the [Remove Reaction](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#remove-reaction)
 setting is disabled.

2

If this didn't solve the issue, add the reaction to the message yourself.

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#the-bot-doesnt-recognize-an-emoji)

**The bot doesn't recognize an emoji**

If the bot is not recognizing an emoji and not adding the role, try the following steps:

1

Make sure you added the right unicode character for default emojis, like this: `1️⃣`, or the right name for custom emojis. For instance, if your custom emoji is called `<:BotGhostWave:1048697598355189850>`, only add `BotGhostWave`.

2

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#the-module-is-not-working-at-all)

**The module is not working at all**

If the module is not doing anything, try the following steps:

1

Check if your bot is on [BotPanel](https://botpanel.gg/)
. If it is, enable the module there too and set it up from BotPanel, or remove the bot from BotPanel if you're not intending to use it.

2

Reset your bot's token on the [Discord Developer Portal](https://discord.com/developers/)
. Paste your token into your bot's [settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/general-settings-and-collaboration/settings#bot-token)
 and start the bot.

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#watch-the-tutorial)

Watch the Tutorial


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#settings)

Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#setup)

Setup

The Reaction Role module has different configurations which change how roles are given or removed.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F6gkQbtEx8cHwp4q9N4N2%252FScreenshot_9-7-2024_175519_dashboard.botghost.com.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59c87f53-2f76-4e3a-b602-8d95fc712bae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a59157a4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#message-id)

**Message ID**

Here you will need to enter the [message ID](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/206346498-Where-can-I-find-my-User-Server-Message-ID)
 of the message you wish to use as the reaction roles panel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#reaction-emoji)

**Reaction Emoji**

Here you can enter the emoji that is used on the reaction message, this can be discord emojis or custom emojis.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#roles-to-add)

**Roles To Add**

Here you can select the roles to add to the user when they react to the message.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#roles-to-remove)

**Roles To Remove**

Here you can select some roles the bot should remove when the user reacts to the message.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#restrict-to-one-reaction)

**Restrict To One Reaction**

Here you can enable/disable the option to restrict a user's reaction to one reaction at a time.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#remove-reaction)

**Remove Reaction**

Here you can enable/disable the option for the bot to remove the user's reaction once they have been given the role.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#blacklisted-roles)

**Blacklisted Roles**

Here you can select some roles that are unable to use this reaction message. Users with this role will not be able to react to the message as the bot will instantly delete it.

To save the reaction roles settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another reaction role.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#active-reaction-roles)

Active Reaction Roles

Once you have added a reaction role from the settings above, a new area will appear that contains all the active reaction roles. You may edit / delete any of these active reaction roles on the bottom right of the image below.

To save the edits you made on the reaction role settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F0pWv2jqdCpigtgi7mLkr%252FScreenshot_10-7-2024_152239_dashboard.botghost.com.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D421118d8-cd4a-4c9f-9d22-7c50430a7610&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8dc8cca&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#events)

Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Reaction Roles module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FWOdO6snsoK2G1QL82cOQ%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-10%2520143001.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97615e94-f165-4ce2-b1d0-17ef6de5ae7d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2db7f6b5&sv=2)

Reaction Roles #...[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/reaction-roles#reaction-roles)

Once you add a Reaction Role, the corresponding event will be created. This will handle the newly created Reaction Role.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Event Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Question Of The Day | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1mPzD5kY7IHrHfpN58dc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da01e1135-028d-484a-ba01-42fea48a50c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3873620e&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Question Of The Day](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/7996e599-c1e4-4975-9f49-928c029a7d70/questionoftheday)
 module encourages members to engage in your server by answering a daily question that is automatically posted by your bot into a specific channel.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#main-settings)

Main Settings

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FfgkZUB4xr9C1W1rewQem%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8727a5e7-fe0d-40da-8b24-ff64377d412b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=248d8f3a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#qotd-channel)

**QOTD Channel**

The channel where all questions will be automatically posted by your bot including the thread it creates. Inside of the thread is where users can give their answer to the question.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#mentioned-roles)

**Mentioned Roles**

Select roles that will be automatically pinged when a new question is posted.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#private-mode)

**Private Mode**

When enabled only people with the roles selected under 'Mentioned Roles' will be able to answer questions of the day.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#qotd-announcement-message)

**QOTD Announcement Message**

The format of the daily question can be customized here, you can choose between an embed or plain text message. When a new question of the day is created, this message will be sent alongside with the thread connected to it. Below you can find the variables you can use in the message.

Variable

Description

`{question}`

Returns the current question of the day.

`{day}`

Returns the total number of days the module has been posting questions for.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#created-thread-name)

**Created Thread Name**

The name of the thread that is created with the daily question, users may put their answer to the question inside of this thread.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#thread-archive-duration)

**Thread Archive Duration**

Choose between one of the four options to customize when the thread will be archived when no message has been sent in the thread in the specified duration.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#thread-slowmode)

**Thread Slowmode**

The duration of slowmode in seconds for messages that will be applied to the created thread for the question. The maximum slowmode is 6 hours (21600 seconds), this is recommended to use if you want users to only send 1 answer to the question.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#question-setup)

Question Setup

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FcMEwzjz4ked8FP8JSmDJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da325a379-55e6-4a1d-b025-a24f2e54abf8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1f267aa&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#question-generation-setup)

**Question Generation Setup**

Choose the type of questions that are sent daily, either the ones already created with the module or custom questions that you can input.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#custom-questions)

Custom Questions

Input your custom questions in this section, make sure to separate each question with a normal comma. You can use special comma characters such as `٫` to put commas inside of your actual questions. _This setting is only visible with_ [Question Generation Setup](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#question-generation-setup)
 _set to "Customize Questions"._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#skip-previously-asked-questions)

**Skip Previously Asked Questions**

When enabled all existing questions will be asked first before starting a new round. This can be used to prevent questions from being sent more than once.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#events)

Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the event of the Question Of The Day module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FfzCKmjQFHIjlFOyTxOGl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D217fef45-f8d9-4a23-853c-0d271adceaf2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=426d600c&sv=2)

QOTD Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#qotd-handler)

The event that manages the questions that are sent daily along with the threads that are automatically created when a new question is posted. Make sure to not delete the associated timed event in the [timed events](https://docs.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events)
 module.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the event of this module unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command and Event Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#settings)
    
*   [Main Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#main-settings)
    
*   [Question Setup](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#question-setup)
    
*   [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/question-of-the-day#events)
    

Was this helpful?
