# Moderation | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOaSmaIu2ZBvZQMnktq9Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c7d06d2-4787-451f-a42c-c9cdb8019bb4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76bb1ca4&sv=2)

The [Moderation](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/ce84a76f-f0cc-42ce-8ebb-3790db06e943/moderation)
 module allows you to setup a highly customizable moderation system you can create for your server, with warnings, timeouts, auto-punishments and more features.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#common-issues)

Common Issues


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Experiencing issues with the module? Check out the common issues below. If your issue is not listed in this page, make sure your module is updated to the latest version. If you are still experiencing issues with the module, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

It is advised that you [Enable Moderation Logging](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#enable-moderation-logging)
 to make sure you can see details about possible errors.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#roles-not-being-added-removed)

Roles not being added / removed

If the `/role add`, `/role remove` or `/role temp` commands are not working, it is likely because the role that you are trying to add or remove is above the bot's role in your server settings. The steps below will most likely solve your issue:

1

Make sure your bot has the administrator permission in your server. You can check this by looking at the permissions from your bot's role.

2

Make sure the bot's role is at the top of the role list. If this is not the case, drag the role to the top.

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help, we'll do our best to solve your issue!

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#users-not-being-muted-kicked-or-banned)

Users not being muted, kicked or banned

If the `/mute add`, `/kick`, `/ban add` or `/ban temp` command is not working, it is likely because the role of the target user is higher than the role from the bot. You are likely to solve this with the steps below:

1

Make sure your bot has the administrator permission in your server. You can check this by looking at the permissions from your bot's role.

2

Make sure the bot's role is at the top of the role list. If this is not the case, drag the role to the top.

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help, we'll do our best to solve your issue!

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#watch-the-tutorial)

Watch the Tutorial


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#command-settings)

Command Settings

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2vakL4JTqDyxrZDY3wsi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da626db5e-8d17-48a5-b4c8-b341608ea00b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=770b0c22&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#default-permissions)

Default Permissions

If you have this enabled, users with the manage messages permission will be able to use moderator commands. Users with the administrator permission will be able to use admin commands.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#admin-roles)

Admin Roles

Here you can select one or more roles that you want to allow to use admin commands. Admin roles can access commands that are only meant for managing the server. Examples of these are: `/role add`, `/role remove`, `/role temp` and `/user clear-history` but those may not be all. You can view a list with all commands in [the commands section](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#commands)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#moderator-roles)

Moderator Roles

Here you can select one or more roles that you want to allow to use moderator commands. Moderator roles can only access commands meant for moderating the server, such as: `/ban add`, `/case view` and `/warn`, but those are not all. You can view a list with all commands in [the commands section](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#commands)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#enable-moderation-logging)

Enable Moderation Logging

When enabled, all moderation actions will be logged to a channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#moderation-log-channel)

Moderation Log Channel

Here you can select the channel where you want to log moderation actions. _This setting only shows if you_ [Enable Moderation Logging](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#enable-moderation-logging)
_._

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#visual-settings)

Visual Settings

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F5ND3d7RLdZMRTR9FKcs9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D372ee7e3-b73e-447b-8a20-987b0551ebec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92537abc&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#punishment-color)

Punishment Color

Here you can select what color that you want to use for punishment messages. Punishment messages are sent to the channel where the punishment has been issued.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#logging-color)

Logging Color

Here you can select what colour you want to give to log messages. Log messages are sent to the moderation log channel, if enabled.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#behaviour-settings)

Behaviour Settings

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2yZTCwLZILcYiSXamfx6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3a81d78-6680-41ae-8f49-28b7aace3e94&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=90b268b4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#send-direct-messages)

Send Direct Messages

Here you can select whether you want to send a direct message to the user that has been punished.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#direct-message)

Direct Message

Here you can edit the message that a user gets after being punished. If the setting above has been disabled, the user will not get any direct message. You can use a set of variables in the direct message, you can read more about that [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#variables)
. _This setting only shows if the_ [Send Direct Messages](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#send-direct-messages)
 _setting is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#ban-delete-messages)

Ban: Delete Messages

Here you can select whether or not you want to delete a user's messages when they have been banned from the server.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#auto-punishment-settings)

Auto-Punishment Settings

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FBvzp2F242VgSRIekjOb8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D842e6fae-5fd4-46ad-9713-4b705e26c0a0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b691d75&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#trigger-punishment-type)

Trigger Punishment Type

In this selection, you can select what type of punishment should trigger the auto punishment.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#warnings-timeouts-needed)

Warnings / Timeouts Needed

This is the number of warnings or timeouts needed before the auto punishment is triggered.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#punishment)

Punishment

Here you can select the type of punishment that a user should get when they reach the amount of warnings / timeouts entered above.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#timeout-duration)

Timeout Duration

This is the time a user should be timed out when they trigger an auto-punishment. _This setting is only shown if you selected "Timeout User" in the_ [_Punishment settings_](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#punishment)
_._

To save the punishment's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another punishment.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#punishments)

Punishments

Here you can manage your currently active punishments. The same settings as [Auto-Punishments](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#auto-punishment-settings)
 apply. You are able to edit / delete these punishments. A maximum of 10 punishments is present.

To save the edits you made on the punishment's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fl8ouWMUuC8g1QxGQPt6k%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34c46d98-dfbf-4fa5-a7d5-3da7a6a29560&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db79f7b5&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#variables)

Variables


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here are some module variables that can be used in [the direct message section](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#direct-message)
.

Variable

Details

`{action}`

This variable will show the type of punishment the user got. For example: warn, mute or ban.

`{moderator}`

This variable will mention the moderator that gave the punishment.

`{time}`

This variable will show you the timestamp of the moment the punishment was issued.

`{case}`

This variable will show you the ID of the moderation case.

`{reason}`

This variable will return the reason for the punishment, this reason was provided by the moderator.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#commands)

Commands


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F0CSClvuUOr7KqwOf7Vax%252FScreenshot_26-9-2024_193555_dashboard.botghost.com.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd433b72b-788d-4612-b3e3-4ed3e548e0da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ca99523&sv=2)

/ban add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#ban-add)

This command allows you to ban a user from the server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FYayxX62u3nJwtz1eXkBM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D604d7f28-8866-48b6-b733-8dd6b6505215&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3dd15549&sv=2)

/ban remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#ban-remove)

This command allows you to unban a user from the server on ID

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FV1P6hUwVtWpRe0mU9npK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7b9a4af0-9c5a-4984-b1dd-9a9cbdc35f6d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40f174a5&sv=2)

/ban temp[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#ban-temp)

This command allows you to temporarily ban a user from the server

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9XN2vfzkMUsr3wb3RXSw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c03007e-e21e-4572-9237-124f6bef95a5&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52d0c4ed&sv=2)

/mute add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#mute-add)

This command allows you to put a user in time-out

/mute remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#mute-remove)

This command allows you to remove a timeout from a user

/role add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#role-add)

This command allows you to ddd a role to a user

/role remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#role-remove)

This command allows you to remove a role from a user

/role temp[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#role-temp)

This command allows you to temporarily give a user a role, this role will be removed after a selected amount of time

/voice deaf[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#voice-deaf)

This command allows you to deafen someone in a voice channel

/voice undeaf[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#voice-undeaf)

This command allows you to undeafen someone in a voice channel

/kick[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#kick)

This command allows you to kick a user

/case view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#case-view)

This command allows you to get the content of a moderation case

/note add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#note-add)

This command allows you to add a note to a user

/note remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#note-remove)

This command allows you to remove a note from a user

/note view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#note-view)

This command allows you to get the content of a note from a user

/case remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#case-remove)

This command allows you to delete a moderation case

/user history[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#user-history)

This command allows you to view the punishment history of a user

/slowmode[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#slowmode)

This command allows you to enable or edit the slow mode setting of a channel

/user clear-history[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#user-clear-history)

This command allows you to clear the punishment history of a user

/warn[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#warn)

This command allows you to warn a user

/ping[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#ping)

This command allows you to get the latency of the bot

/purge[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#purge)

This command allows you to delete up to 100 messages at the same time from a channel

/server-info[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#server-info)

This command allows you to get information about the server, such as the server name, member count, description and more

/user nick[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#user-nick)

This command allows you to change the nickname of a user

/channel lock[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#channel-lock)

This command allows you to change the channel permissions so that no one can send messages anymore

/channel unlock[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#channel-unlock)

This command allows you to change the permissions in a channel back so that everyone can send messages again

/say[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#say)

This command allows you to send a message with the bot.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#add-command)

\[👑\] Add Command

By clicking the add command button you can create your own command for the moderation module using all the module [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#variables)
 and settings.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#events)

Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fo04VONv6EDaawrOvLM1x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab9303f4-f614-46a4-aebb-4da8b24d21e2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2aa3a05&sv=2)

Moderation Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#moderation-handler)

This event will enforce [the auto-punish settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#auto-punishment-settings)
.

Temporary Role & Ban Check[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#temporary-role-and-ban-check)

This command will make sure temporary roles or bans are removed on time.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#add-event)

\[👑\] Add Event

By clicking the add event button you can create your own event for the moderation module using all the module [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/moderation#variables)
 and settings.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Timed Messages | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F5QkFF2zKuzTPdCvbTxrI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8a63c2c-66e8-42e0-bbee-0b1beb41552e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd689bb8&sv=2)

The [Timed Messages](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/5f1b4c67-b37b-487c-8287-a694b1e01ce8/timedmessages)
 module will have your bot send a message to channels at repeated scheduled intervals.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#settings)

Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#create-timed-message)

Create Timed Message

New timed messages may be created within this part of the module. Click the add button at the very bottom left of this image to add it to the active timed messages.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJtdTKtfFDMmgPq4eo4QB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78b230c8-11c2-44fd-8ae5-91374df5e7ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63c0984a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#timed-message-name)

**Timed Message Name**

This field is the input for a unique name for the timed message.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#channel-selection)

**Channel Selection**

Select any text or announcement channel in your server to send the timed message to.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#time-interval-days)

**Time Interval - Days**

In this field is the delay amount in days between timed messages (If blank it defaults to 0).

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#time-interval-hours)

**Time Interval - Hours**

In this field is the delay amount in hours between timed messages (If blank it defaults to 0).

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#time-interval-minutes)

**Time Interval - Minutes**

Choose a delay between 0 and 60 minutes with 5-minute intervals. Default is 0 minutes.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#message)

**Message**

This is where you can setup the contents of a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 message. You may toggle it by clicking on the switch in the corner.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#block-stacked-messages)

**Block Stacked Messages**

If enabled, when the timed message is executed the bot will check if the last message in the channel was by your bot. If so it will skip the sending of this timed message.

To save the timed message settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another timed message.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#active-timed-messages)

Active Timed Messages

These are timed events that are already created in the module and can be edited or deleted underneath the options to create / edit a new timed message.

To save the edits you made on the rotating status's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FP55Pp3IIZxi5pFjPHqdh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5fa8dd0-e19b-42d0-9fca-91de6fd46284&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a1eb7132&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#events)

Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Discord Automod module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FbI5XsbUFZqwRykk8nH4k%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0271c964-4b22-49fb-b4e1-dcc039123531&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27813131&sv=2)

Timed Messages Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#timed-messages-handler)

This event will search for all active timed events, loop through and send them at a specific interval.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#settings)
    
*   [Create Timed Message](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#create-timed-message)
    
*   [Active Timed Messages](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#active-timed-messages)
    
*   [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/timed-messages#events)
    

Was this helpful?

# Polls | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F4dsZwmnQrnFzbTJgkMag%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1a52022-5542-4a87-92e5-2a9b5d592525&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb985953&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

Using the [Polls](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/a1cb21af-b61d-44a6-86b7-5180920fd49d/polls)
 module you can create and deploy fun and interactive polls for your server members to vote on that are highly customizable.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#settings)

Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#permission-settings)

Permission Settings

Customize the permissions for the polls. Ranging from editing role and channel permissions and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FtBXTL4iKweD6lBwafwst%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da388a15d-362e-4549-971c-8807f1fb9018&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae4fabee&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#manager-roles)

Manager Roles

This option will allow you to select some roles to grant manager permissions to using the role dropdown, users with these roles will be able to run the poll-management commands of the module.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#whitelisted-channels)

Whitelisted Channels

This option will allow you to select some channels to restrict the modules usage. When at least one channel is added, users with the manager roles are the only ones who can post polls in that channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#blacklisted-roles)

Blacklisted Roles

In this field you can select some roles to block by using the role dropdown. Any user who has the blacklisted role will not be able to vote in a poll.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#single-choice)

Single Choice

This toggle will allow you to enable / disable single choice restrictions for polls. When enabled, users will only be able to choose a single option of the poll. This restriction only applies to one poll at a time. By default this is active.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#poll-settings)

Poll Settings

Configure the message and the contents of the poll in this section.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fw93kvXllu8RCJgtoPH7f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48943e48-63b7-4ce2-8292-c9d2c6b3f79e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b111fde9&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#embed-title)

Embed Title

This field allows you to define the title of the poll messages that get sent. The `{poll.question}` [variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used to return the configured question.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#embed-footer)

Embed Footer

In this field you can edit the [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 footer for poll messages.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#embed-color)

Embed Color

With this field you can change the color of the poll embeds that get sent.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#show-posters-name)

Show Posters Name

Using this toggle you can choose whether to show the name of the user who posted the poll message. By default this is active.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#choice-reactions)

Choice Reactions

This section is where you can edit the poll emojis. They are in exact order as the questions are presented so it is not recommended to edit this. You can input the [Emoji ID](https://docs.botghost.com/getting-started/standard-practices/advanced-practices#how-can-i-get-a-custom-emojis-id)
 for custom emojis, or [unicode](https://emojipedia.org/)
 emojis supported in Discord.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#commands)

Commands


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Polls module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F7P3YAeVgEzfFQMp1XlK6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5df59707-c7d2-4333-b6c6-2b349513a007&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=15068338&sv=2)

/poll-create[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#poll-create)

This command allows a user to create a poll with a number of questions.

/poll-end[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#poll-end)

This command is meant to end a active poll and can only be used by manager roles / admins.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#events)

Events


------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Polls module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F5tv698iD9z3tkuU8KhqQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8d9ade8-8a2b-46b5-9eec-b52bbf330c19&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cf3b18&sv=2)

Polls Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/polls#polls-handler)

The Polls Handler event is the main event that tracks user reactions and counts the total poll votes for any active poll ongoing.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Starboard | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fr809Kc8C0I5BoriBAM5H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff637a86-7c38-4b70-a364-9c73f00fafa2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff639809&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Starboard](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/25f958e7-536c-464c-b3de-d8d4d07eb75a/starboard)
 module allows users in your server to vote for the most liked message, the message that has the most amount of votes is shared on a starboard for all users of your server to see! The system is based on users reacting to messages with a certain emoji, which are converted into "votes".

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#settings)

Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#settings-1)

Settings

In this section of the module, you can edit the main settings of the module. Some of these options are required for the module to work.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F6KknlY9xSdxrQfztpHLy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D853d2c0a-c276-4c75-994e-b885888b7321&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6800acf8&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#emoji)

**Emoji**

Here you can edit the emoji that the bot counts as a reaction, you may press on the plus (+) sign to add an emoji that will be used for the module.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#reactions-required)

**Reactions Required**

Here you can set the total number of reactions needed before the message is added to the starboard, the default value is set to 10. After the number is reached, the message will be posted into the starboard's channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#starboard-channel)

**Starboard Channel**

Set the channel that the starboard will be sent to when a message reaches the chosen number of reactions set in the [Reactions Required](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#reactions-required)
 setting.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#embed-color)

**Embed Color**

Edit the color of the embed message that is sent to the starboard channel. You can add custom colors by taking advantage of the HEX code input section.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#react-to-the-starboard-message)

**React to the starboard message**

Here you can enable or disable the bot automatically reacting to the starboard message when its posted to the starboard channel. Reactions to this message will not count towards the reaction count defined in the [Reactions Required](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#reactions-required)
 setting.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#delete-the-starboard-message)

**Delete the starboard message**

Here you can enable/disable a setting to make the bot automatically delete the starboard message sent in the defined starboard channel if the original message falls below the required reactions as defined in the [Reactions Required](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#reactions-required)
 setting.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#channels)

Channels

Here you can configure the channel settings for the module, this includes changing the blacklist type and picking the channels for the module to use in your server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FYKdlsDnDudemWsi7d1Lc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3705d8f3-8727-48cf-ae35-50dac7779958&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c217e36f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#channel-restrictions)

**Channel Restrictions**

You can setup channel restrictions to allow the usage of voting on messages in certain channels.

Blacklist type

Description

No Channel Restrictions

Users will be able to vote on messages in all channels.

Disable for these channels...

Setting this blacklist type will disable voting on all channels selected.

Enable for these channels..,

Setting this blacklist type will enable voting on all channels selected.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#events)

Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Starboard module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FdnDhAal7Xu4Q1MuDZmK3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38366a27-7383-4410-a255-9aa589a8553e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fe764c3&sv=2)

Starboard Add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#starboard-add)

This event is the main function for the starboard and counts all reactions added to the message if they meet the settings as defined in the module.

Starboard Remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#starboard-remove)

This event will detect when reactions are removed from messages and trigger the [Delete the starboard message](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#delete-the-starboard-message)
 setting if it is enabled.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Custom Events Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#settings)
    
*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#settings-1)
    
*   [Channels](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#channels)
    
*   [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/starboard#events)

# Premium Check Condition | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/premium-check-condition.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FEc40Jwt2CoiI9etIcAbc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89c0c4df-32a7-4996-b9c8-15d308565486&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f9e98c1&sv=2)

The premium check condition allows you to run actions based off if your bot has premium or not. This condition is mainly used in BotGhost's pre-built modules, however it can be used in any command / event you create. The red block runs when the bot is not premium, while the green one runs when the bot is currently premium. The condition has no settings.

Here is a layout for this condition:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FymtEexK6YwZ140TpEDnc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91a21c39-9a11-4db9-96aa-7d34ddf9ef42&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3af51afe&sv=2)

# Objects | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects.md)
.

Objects are a special data type usually used to store a "group" of data. For example, they can be used to store the birthday of an user, which is made by the day of birth, month and year. They can also be helpful when creating an economy system: you can use an object to store the inventory of a specific user.

Here are some examples of object references and their values:

*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day}` - 1
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.month}` - 7
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.year}` - 1979
    

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#how-values-are-stored-in-objects)

How Values Are Stored In Objects


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Objects store values as properties. Each property has a name (key) and a value that you can assign as base value. In the example above, the "object variable" variable has three properties: "day", "month", and "year". These properties hold the values "1", "7", and "1979", respectively.

Objects also have default values you are able to set when creating them in [data storage](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage)
. Likewise you are able to remove keys from here as well. In addition to default values, you can create new keys during commands or events by using either the [Set Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/set-variable)
 or [Run Equation on Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/run-equation-on-variable)
 action blocks.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUqPPwq8o5MkUqVkDvKyh%252Fimage_2024-06-06_182806236.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea4026dd-db0c-4c0d-a5df-4b4564ba0cfa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8894a588&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#displaying-object-values)

Displaying Object Values


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To display values stored in the object variable, you use a dot notation between the object's variable name, followed by a dot, and the property (key) name. The same key name can be used across different objects, but cannot be used twice in the same object. For example:

*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day}`
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.year}`
    
*   `{BGVAR_cool_variable.day}`
    

This variable can be used anywhere in your command builder and will retrieve the corresponding value for the given object and property.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#targeting)

Targeting

Targeting also works for object variables, when they are user or channel specific. Just like regular variables, you can add the square brackets \[\] at the end of the variable providing the user / channel target, for example:

*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day[option_user]}`
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day[{bot_id}]}`
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day[136327647792726016]}`
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day[option_channel]}`
    
*   `{BGVAR_object_variable.day[{first_channel_id}]}`
    

If no target is provided, the value of the user who triggered the last interaction (command, event, button or select menu) will be returned for user objects, and the value of the channel the last interaction has been triggered in (command, event, button or select menu) will be returned.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#updating-values)

Updating Values


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To update a value into an object using any of these 3 action blocks:

Block

Information

[Set Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/set-variable)

Object variables selected in this block will allow you to set a value for a specific key.

[Run Equation on Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/run-equation-on-variable)

For this action block, a specific key's value will be set as the result of an equation.

[Delete Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/delete-variable)

This action block will allow you to delete a specific key's value or all key values from an object.

Check out the object sections on the pages for these actions by clicking the links above for more information.

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [How Values Are Stored In Objects](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#how-values-are-stored-in-objects)
    
*   [Displaying Object Values](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#displaying-object-values)
    
*   [Targeting](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#targeting)
    
*   [Updating Values](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects#updating-values)
    

Was this helpful?

# ChatGPT | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FIGEqfo6ah0JC5a0kx2F8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db822a1c9-c7da-4e63-b1dd-8b0bc79329a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a1e98946&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [ChatGPT](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/6e8c5384-e6f8-4282-8125-5ca9b53242c8/chatgpt)
 module allows users to hold conversations with their bot by using the OpenAI GPT 3.5 Turbo - GPT 4 software. Get it to tell you stories or ask some advanced questions.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#common-issues)

Common Issues


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Experiencing issues with the module? Check out the common issues below. If your issue is not listed in this page, make sure your module is updated to the latest version. If you are still experiencing issues with the module, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#ai-commands-return-a-429-error)

AI commands return a 429 error

If a `429` error is returned when trying to use ChatGPT's AI commands, please try the steps below.

1

The OpenAI (ChatGPT) 429 error means your free trial of the API key you're using has expired. To extend your quota and continue using OpenAI, you need to enter your billing details. You can do that in the [OpenAI Developer Platform](https://openai.com/api/)
.

2

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help, we'll do our best to solve your issue!

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#credentials-setup)

Credentials Setup


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Click [here](https://platform.openai.com/account/api-keys)
 to get started. Log into OpenAI. If you haven't already, Open AI might ask you to verify your phone number before proceeding.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fq9GPD8gYEEKSUJUdOUT0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21258ead-278d-4369-9e6e-8c74720216e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4db4d6a7&sv=2)

2

Once you logged in, click on the "Create new secret key button.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FS7gwMVMFJzgROIn9FgNg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c28f2f7-66d6-4ffc-a30c-fca4aa336669&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a7c3f78&sv=2)

3

This will prompt you to make a key. Set Owned by "You" and give your app a name. Set the "Permissions" to all. Once done, click on "Create Secret Key"

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8jDcjid6nM0pn1C4FEQY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def74a1c9-be35-4a97-8993-e0f087a4c170&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=372fc88c&sv=2)

4

Copy your key. Make sure to not share it with anyone.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Ft5wYLfCDF4amFI8F4pjO%252FUntitled%2520design.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92f2b404-4afc-45c8-93ba-6316f89c861f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60a63e3b&sv=2)

5

Paste your key into the BotGhost Dashboard in [the OpenAI API Key field](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#openai-api-key)
.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#general-settings)

General Settings

In this area, you can setup and customize the general settings for the commands and events of this module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FyDrSuSkd8Cg52JGEd2GW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b4f24e7-c0e1-4d7e-bfc7-1b2a45277739&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99c24fb4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#embeds-color)

Embeds Color

In this setting you can select the color of the embeds in this module. When the bot responds using an embed, the embed will use this color.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#openai-api-key)

OpenAI API Key

In this field is where you will need to enter your OpenAI API key to be able to use the module, you can follow this guide [here](https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/authentication)
, to generate your own API key.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#respond-command)

Respond Command

In this area, you can setup and customize the settings of the response command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FlBlUGizCM3CF76GyXwga%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da414152a-d965-47e4-b3a8-00759d65be91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=319bfc0e&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#response-command)

Response Command

You can toggle this switch to either enable or disable the respond command. This toggle needs to be enabled in order to show the settings below.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#model)

Model

In this section you can select what model of ChatGPT you want to use. The selected Model will reply to the respond command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#channel-restrictions-blacklist-type)

Channel Restrictions - Blacklist Type

In this menu you can choose the criteria you want to follow to disable the command in certain channels. In the table below you can read what you can choose from.

Type

Details

No Channel Restrictions

If this option is selected, no channel restrictions will be applied.

Disable for these channels

Based on the channels input, the module will not respond in this channel.

Enable these channels

Based on the channels input, the module will only respond in this channel

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#channel-restrictions-select-channels)

Channel Restrictions - Select Channels

In this channel selector you can select the channels that you wish to allow or that you wish to disallow, depending on the selection you made in the [Blacklist Type](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#channel-restrictions-blacklist-type)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#role-restrictions-blacklist-type)

Role Restrictions - Blacklist Type

In this menu you can choose the criteria you want to follow to blacklist certain roles from using the command. In the table below you can read what you can choose from.

Type

Details

No Role Restrictions

If this option is selected, no role restrictions will be applied.

Disable for these roles

Based on the role input, the module will not respond to this role.

Enable these roles

Based on the channels input, the module will only respond to this role.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#role-restrictions-select-roles)

Role Restrictions - Select Roles

In this channel selector you can select the roles that you wish to allow or that you wish to disallow, depending on the selection you made in the [Blacklist Type](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#role-restrictions-blacklist-type)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#personality)

Personality

In this field you can describe the personality the responses from the command should follow.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/chatgpt#edit-text-command)

In this area, you can setup and customize the settings of the text command.

 and settings.

# Sticky Roles | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FfmzU0qWKkiLl0djSGk6O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2980beda-2307-42e1-9811-ea23dd3a4234&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fef757e&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Sticky Roles](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/911f6c91-a771-4cd7-b848-807bf4bd6588/stickyroles)
 module will allow server members to regain some or all of their roles upon leaving and rejoining the server.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#settings)

Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#role-settings)

Role Settings

In this area, you can customize how the module functions.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1HOPihtxYb7baJ3iFiff%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84c36b54-ccee-4c3a-bfc8-8c2ef05cd3b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bd3849&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#role-filtering-type)

**Role Filtering Type**

This is how you specify if certain roles should be added upon rejoining or excluded.

Type

Details

Ignored Roles

This selector is how you choose what roles should not be added when a user rejoins. Keep in mind that if this option is enabled, then all other roles besides the ones selected will be added to the user.

Allowed Roles

This selector is how you choose sticky roles that get added to a user when they rejoin. Excluding roles from the selector while this option is enabled will result in those roles simply not being added.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#ignore-moderation-actions)

**Ignore Moderation Actions**

If this switch is enabled then the bot will ignore moderation actions, so if a user is banned or kicked it will still add them upon rejoining. However it is the opposite if it's disabled.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#send-direct-message)

**Send Direct Message**

Here you may toggle whether members who get roles back upon rejoining will receive a direct message with a list of those roles.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#direct-message-setup)

**Direct Message Setup**

If the direct message option is enabled, then you can configure the message. The message can be toggled to [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 type and will be sent upon rejoining along with the roles. You can use the `{roles}` [variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 to list all the roles that were added when the user rejoined.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#events)

Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Sticky Roles module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FI6aKSsuvAhoygE0obSn6%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-12%2520210341.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D674e09a4-af99-4103-90ea-acbac33a0d01&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d4fac36&sv=2)

Events of the sticky roles module

Leave Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#leave-handler)

This event stores the roles that a user had upon leaving the server into a custom variable.

Join Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#join-handler)

This event re-assigns the stored roles that should be assigned according to the module's customization, and DMs the user if/with any roles were re-assigned (if enabled).

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#settings)
    
*   [Role Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#role-settings)
    
*   [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/sticky-roles#events)
    

Was this helpful?

# Collections | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections.md)
.

Collections or arrays are a special data storage type that allows you to store a group of text or numbers. Collections consist of an ordered list using numbered indexes starting from 0 to access specific data.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#how-values-are-stored-in-collections)

How Values Are Stored In Collections


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Collection values are stored on positions in the collection. Each position has it's own number to access it, starting at 0. Every value is seperated with a comma.

Collections also have default values you are able to set when creating or editing a variable in the [data storage](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage)
 module.

Here are some examples of collection references and their values or arrays:

*   `{BGVAR_collection}` - \[hello, world, abc, xyz\]
    
*   `{valueAtPosition({BGVAR_collection}),[2]}` - abc
    
*   `{lengthOfCollection({BGVAR_collection})}` - 4
    

Collection positions always start at 0.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPoHv00NF79HdRjbbyAXY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01d6801d-1366-433b-aad9-ed6f8ed4416d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb97bc45&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#displaying-collection-values)

Displaying Collection Values


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To display values stored in the collection variable, you can target the position of the value. You can also use other variables to access the data in other ways. Below are some examples of targeting positions in the collection variable:

*   `{BGVAR_collection}` - \[hello, world, abc, xyz\]
    
*   `{valueAtPosition({BGVAR_collection}),[0]}` - hello
    
*   `{valueAtPosition({BGVAR_collection}),[1]}` - world
    
*   `{valueAtPosition({BGVAR_collection}),[2]}` - abc
    

This variable can be used anywhere in your command and event builder and will retrieve the corresponding value for the given position of the collection.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#collection-variables)

Collection Variables

BotGhost offers some variables you can use for any array or collection (even from an [API response](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/api-actions/send-an-api-request)
), which allow you to retrieve specific information of the collection. To know more about them, check out the [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables#collection-array-variables)
 page.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#targeting)

Targeting

Targeting also works for collection variables, when they are user or channel specific. Just like regular variables, you can add the square brackets \[\] at the end of the base variable providing the user / channel target, for example:

*   `{BGVAR_collection[user_id]}`
    
*   `{valueAtPosition({BGVAR_collection[user_id]}),[0]}`
    

If no target is provided, the value of the user who triggered the last interaction (command, event, button or select menu) will be returned for user collections, or the value of the channel the last interaction has been triggered in (command, event, button or select menu) will be returned for channel collections.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#updating-collection-values)

Updating Collection Values


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To update a collection value, you can use one of the [variable actions](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions)
 below:

Block

Information

[Set Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/set-variable)

Collection variables selected in this block will allow you to set a value somewhere in a collection.

[Delete Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions/delete-variable)

This action block will allow you to delete a collection value.

You can not use the Run Equation on Variable action on collections.

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [How Values Are Stored In Collections](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#how-values-are-stored-in-collections)
    
*   [Displaying Collection Values](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#displaying-collection-values)
    
*   [Collection Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#collection-variables)
    
*   [Targeting](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#targeting)
    
*   [Updating Collection Values](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections#updating-collection-values)
    

Was this helpful?

# Text Option | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOEnyceQEyRuR0vXgO2jn%252Fimage_2024-06-07_184243639.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dce229746-94be-4e37-ae3c-540f85cc7383&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49959e31&sv=2)

This block is a plain text option which allows you input a text value when entering your command on Discord.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FZP6uX7IQrs9XWxdqOctu%252Fimage_2024-06-07_152906910.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93573c75-2de7-4f75-9b96-08486e96f4ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b472c4d8&sv=2)

You can retrieve the variable of the option via the **Clipboard** or the block itself. The format of the variable is `{option_optionname}`, where `optionname` is the [name](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#option-name)
 of the option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F5dvEmba03gvfHMjFjokE%252Fimage_2024-06-08_123442535.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1564e92-1ba0-4fbf-9151-003521c47a41&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7426c7ee&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#option-name)

Option Name


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This field requires an input for your unique option name. The designated name will then be the reference for your option variable.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FwTAFb2w3JpWegq566V00%252Fimage_2024-06-07_153049549.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50705416-b8b0-419a-a0c3-79c3dd81af18&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d437f60&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#option-description)

Option Description


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The option description field allows you to assign a custom description to your option. It is useful to describe what the option is used for.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvOMtQ8MVXEwV3Bu4T1zJ%252Fimage_2024-06-07_153207575.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6cf2c0c3-3507-42fd-9569-0139e423c7d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c48cd3fe&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#set-required)

Set Required


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this switch you are able to toggle if the option should be required or not in order to execute the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8ZGjl7ltB5dMKqO6Xbja%252Fimage_2024-06-07_153303596.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De487b34e-973a-4c52-93db-c2ebebfb6669&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60842cc5&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#add-choices)

Add Choices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is an optional section is where you can add choices into your option. Choices allow the user to select something from a fixed set of values. There is a maximum number of 25 choices.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvBWwEUVG2a0f7KvvrqQw%252Fimage_2024-06-07_153511286.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd5dfd36-b4ec-4be1-9bc2-4f2f1c3a72c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ff0b47f&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FVGSWUkH0jSJP5LfJxZIc%252Fimage_2024-06-07_180957726.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c8a00d0-c11e-452f-bd49-c041d43c31e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96d08a8e&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#autocomplete)

Autocomplete


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Autocomplete is a feature for slash command text options that shows users a list of suggestions as they type. It makes commands easier to use, reduces typing errors, and creates a smoother experience.

Unlike [choices](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#add-choices)
, the autocomplete feature will add choices to the action that are not required to be the same, meaning you can follow them, but it's not mandatory.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPmwaUKOrDBtewSRJGSbb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D039c0fdf-2ef8-4725-bf31-76618ad10b81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2ce88a3&sv=2)

Autocomplete can be configured by pressing the "Configure Autocomplete" button located in the settings of the text option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F12rlKhf0Dha47i8rIS5I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46f816ff-701a-4bee-b8c9-3b8984aaf696&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc8630b9&sv=2)

Basic Mode

Bulk Mode

The basic settings have been enabled by default when you start to configure autocomplete.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F4oN6zQgQuGEoyIyHI63A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6ed9f219-f07c-4b9c-ba07-244788b8a691&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2dbb4839&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#choices)

Choices

Choices can be addded by pressing the "Add Autocomplete Choice" in the image above.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#label)

Label

The label is what's shown as choice to the user when they use the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPmwaUKOrDBtewSRJGSbb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D039c0fdf-2ef8-4725-bf31-76618ad10b81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2ce88a3&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#value)

Value

The value is what is returned as the `{option_optionname}` variable. The value is not visible to the user and can be something else than the label.

To access bulk mode, you have to enable it in the top of the autocomplete configuration.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhOQwoxnPMhOO6H82nBXb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fc2e502-4201-46a3-bbe7-51f1baaa36af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=192a8ffc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option#bulk-choices)

Bulk Choices

Bulk choices can be added by pasting the lable and value seperated with a comma. An example can be found below:

When you have added the choices, simple press the "Parse and Replace Choices" button below the field. The choices will then also be visible when in Basic Mode.
