# Suggestions | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FECBha9Elhl6l0VgBCqpz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd78ec4d0-9be2-4907-9221-81ae219604db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c026c6c9&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

With the [Suggestions](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/17d130ca-5b40-4554-b11d-ffd889673915/suggestions)
 module you can setup a system that allows users to provide suggestions for your server or other things to suggest on of your choice. Users can create suggestions, vote or downvote on other suggestions, and more. Your server's moderators may approve or deny your server's suggestions.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#settings)

Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#submit-a-suggestion)

Submit a Suggestion

In this area, you can customize how your bots' users will submit their suggestions.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2dDdyxSl5ozjaD7QFyU8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd185d3fd-b213-4b51-906b-3f32aed66a0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1877b6d6&sv=2)

Submit a suggestion portion of the suggestions module

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#title)

**Title**

Here you may choose whether you want your members to be able to, unable to, or have to add a title. The default value for this is set to Disabled.

Value

Details

Disabled

Users cannot add a title for their suggestion.

Enabled

Users can optionally add a title for their suggestion.

Enabled and Required

Users are required to add a title for their suggestion.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#image)

**Image**

Here you may choose whether you want your members to be able to, unable to, or have to add an image. The default value for this is set to Disabled.

Value

Details

Disabled

Users cannot upload an image for their suggestion.

Enabled

Users can optionally upload an image for their suggestion.

Enabled and Required

Users are required to upload an image for their suggestion.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#title-minimum-length)

**Title minimum length**

Here you may choose how long the title of the suggestion may be at its shortest. The default value for this is set to 10. _This setting only shows if_ [Title](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#title)
 _is enabled (and required)._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#title-maximum-length)

**Title maximum length**

Here you may choose how long the title of the suggestion may be at its longest. The default value for this is set to 200. _This setting only shows if_ [Title](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#title)
 _is enabled (and required)._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#description-minimum-length)

**Description minimum length**

Here you may choose how long the description of the suggestion may be at its shortest. The default value for this is set to 10.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#description-maximum-length)

**Description maximum length**

Here you may choose how long the description of the suggestion may be at its longest. The default value for this is set to 4000.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggestions-management)

Suggestions Management

In this area, you can customize who can manage your server's suggestions and how.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOcYiuAIQKtfHJzJrSgQL%252Fqq.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadd081c3-3133-4699-88db-f22e72cbc416&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=813271f&sv=2)

Suggestions Management portion of the suggestions module

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#manager-roles)

**Manager Roles**

Here you may choose the roles users must have in order to approve and deny suggestions.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#enable-logging)

**Enable Logging**

Here you may toggle whether logs about suggestions are sent to a specific channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#logging-channel)

**Logging Channel**

Here you may choose the channel where logs for the module will be sent. _This setting only shows if_ [Enable Logging](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#enable-logging)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#send-all-suggestions-to-a-channel-for-approval)

**Send all suggestions to a channel for approval**

Here you may toggle whether suggestions are sent to a private channel where they must be approved or denied.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#approval-channel)

**Approval Channel**

Here you may choose the channel where suggestions for approval will be sent. _This setting only shows if_ [Send all suggestions to a channel for approval](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#send-all-suggestions-to-a-channel-for-approval)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#hide-the-user-who-approved-or-denied-the-suggestion)

**Hide the user who approved or denied the suggestion**

Here you may toggle whether the user who approved or denied a suggestion is made public.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggestion)

Suggestion

In this area, you can customize how the suggestion appears in the voting channel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FWb9XOcLiA7mHw97xLggJ%252Fscreencapture-dashboard-botghost-dashboard-module-17d130ca-5b40-4554-b11d-ffd889673915-suggestions-2024-07-25-21_23_45%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De38abc14-2d8e-4dce-9337-aa4cf5e06a91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=236e5277&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggestions-channel)

**Suggestions Channel**

Here you may choose the channel where suggestions will be posted and voted on. This is required for the system to function correctly.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#create-thread)

**Create Thread**

Here you may toggle whether a thread for discussion will be created and attached to the suggestion/voting message in the suggestions channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#lock-thread-on-verdict)

**Lock Thread on Verdict**

Here you may toggle whether the thread attached to the suggestion will lock when a suggestion is approved or denied. _This setting only shows if_ [Create Thread](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#create-thread)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#neutral-option)

**Neutral Option**

Here you may toggle whether a reaction for indecisiveness is added to the suggestion / voting message in the suggestions channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#upvote-emoji)

**Upvote Emoji**

Here you may choose the first emoji on the suggestion / voting message, which members can use to show their approval of the suggestion.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#neutral-emoji)

**Neutral Emoji**

Here you may choose the next emoji on the suggestion/voting message, which members can use to show they are indecisive on the suggestion. _This setting only shows if_ [Neutral Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#neutral-option)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#downvote-emoji)

**Downvote Emoji**

Here you may choose the last emoji on the suggestion / voting message, which members can use to show their disapproval of the suggestion.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggestion-embed-color)

**Suggestion Embed color**

Here you may choose the color of the embed in the suggestion/voting message.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#anonymous-suggestions)

**Anonymous Suggestions**

Here you may toggle whether the author of a suggestion is hidden from the public.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#message-suggestion-author-for-updates)

**Message Suggestion Author for updates**

Here you may toggle whether the author of a suggestion receives a direct message when there is an update on their suggestion.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#automation)

Automation

In this area, you can customize how a suggestion can automatically be approved or denied based on its votes.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FlXL0xhHz8h3nDczkZKBo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D504b4eff-267d-42f9-bc1d-1287d220d309&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9227fc40&sv=2)

Automation portion of the Suggestions module

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-approve-type)

Auto Approve Type

Use this feature to automatically approve a suggestion by a certain type of condition.

Disabled

Number of Upvotes

Difference between upvotes and downvotes

Percentage of upvotes

Suggestions will not be automatically approved on any condition.

The number of upvotes needed for suggestions to be automatically approved.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FCg5MzoaMqgH2A1w9o2kS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D151ad81b-e062-47ce-bcd3-d1cafc81c064&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3242dc5c&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-approve-number-of-upvotes)

Auto Approve - Number of upvotes

This setting allows you to set the minimum number of upvotes required to approve the suggestion automatically. You can only provide whole, positive numbers.

Difference between upvotes and downvotes needed for automatic approval of the suggestion.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FO8F3fbxytQy8nPqtHrTk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45054912-1087-458b-8dfb-31a3e6ffa612&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1352b6e&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-approve-difference)

Auto Approve - Difference

This setting allows you to set the minimum difference between the upvotes and the downvotes required to approve the suggestion automatically. This means that, if you set this setting to 10, there must be 10 upvotes more than downvotes in order for the suggestion to be approved. You can only provide whole, positive numbers.

Percentage of upvotes required for automatic approval of the suggestion. A minimum of upvotes required for the percentage to be checked is required. If there aren't enough upvotes, the suggestion won't be approved, even if the required percentage is reached.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FD1I5RtXxxEgwdAxhpTER%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b7ce844-e110-4cee-956f-ea8a77126646&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb000a4e&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-approve-percentage-of-upvotes)

Auto Approve - Percentage of upvotes

This setting allows you to set the minimum percentage of upvotes the suggestion must have in order for it to be approved automatically. You can only provide whole, positive numbers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-approve-minimum-upvotes)

Auto Approve - Minimum upvotes

This setting allows you to set the minimum number of upvotes required for the filter above to work.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-deny-type)

Auto Deny Type

Use this feature to automatically deny a suggestion by a certain type of condition.

Disabled

Number of downvotes

Difference between downvotes and upvotes

Percentage of downvotes

Suggestions will not be automatically denied on any condition.

The number of downvotes needed for suggestions to be automatically denied.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FKttnUPAcchJERzckLtFB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D562f8622-2435-49e1-91b7-c5b46053d361&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c269b02&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-deny-number-of-downvotes)

Auto Deny - Number of downvotes

This setting allows you to set the minimum number of downvotes required to deny the suggestion automatically. You can only provide whole, positive numbers.

Difference between the downvotes and upvotes needed for automatic denial of the suggestion.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FgKn2xWOOr4WjZ7IxV7IT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0ba6a9c-fdfe-4596-85b3-369a4641dc2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db0b62c8&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-deny-difference)

Auto Deny - Difference

This setting allows you to set the minimum difference between the downvotes and the upvotes required to deny the suggestion automatically. This means that, if you set this setting to 10, there must be 10 downvotes more than upvotes in order for the suggestion to be denied. You can only provide whole, positive numbers.

Percentage of downvotes required for automatic denial of the suggestion. A minimum of downvotes required for the percentage to be checked is required. If there aren't enough downvotes, the suggestion won't be rejected, even if the required percentage is reached.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FNNfGkYA8bUUAQMcnBZdM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8657a1d5-63a6-4aea-a174-b946dc47c7a3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cd3c528&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-deny-percentage-of-downvotes)

Auto Deny - Percentage of downvotes

This setting allows you to set the minimum percentage of downvotes the suggestion must have in order for it to be denied automatically. You can only provide whole, positive numbers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#auto-deny-minimum-downvotes)

Auto Deny - Minimum downvotes

This setting allows you to set the minimum number of downvotes required for the filter above to work.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#restrictions)

Restrictions

In this area, you can customize who is restricted from posting suggestions and who is not.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJXA8clh6kPokAsB0qTZG%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-12%2520185054.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db45ac183-3cd8-49fa-99c0-d693b690a73f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66b759f0&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#role-restrictions)

**Role Restrictions**

Blacklist Type

Description

No Role Restrictions

All users of your server may create suggestions.

Disable for these roles...

Set this blacklist type if you want everyone to be able to create suggestions, except users with at least one of the roles provided in the menu below.

Enable for these roles...

Set this blacklist type if you want that only users with at least one of the roles provided in the menu below can post suggestions.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#commands)

Commands


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here you can find the commands for the suggestions system and modify them to your liking.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FxxdYR7f5zW7b8Eu1AFqS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def3b0425-72d6-4ea3-8566-fefa6752b3d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1633744a&sv=2)

Commands of the suggestions module

/suggest[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggest)

This command is what your users can run to make and post suggestions.

/suggestion-view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggestion-view)

This command will allow you to view the information of a suggestion by its suggestion ID or message ID in the suggestions / voting channel.

/suggestion-verdict[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#suggestion-verdict)

This command will allow suggestion managers to approve or deny suggestions by their suggestion ID or message ID in the suggestions / voting channel.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#events)

Events


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here you can find the events for the suggestions system and modify them to your liking.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fdsqv7WwITMdSlof42MNT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52975354-842c-4e02-975e-c107c26bc9e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5f605d5&sv=2)

Events of the suggestions module

Reaction Add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#reaction-add)

This event modifies the percentage of the votes and removes other reactions from the post when a reaction is added if it is in the suggestions/voting channel.

Reaction Remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/suggestions#reaction-remove)

This event modifies the percentage of the votes when a reaction is removed if it is in the suggestions/voting channel.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Statistic Channels | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FM9dyYIkY6iVpMmGigg03%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3639798-c114-454e-b361-061f2c3ccee4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=488c7376&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

BotGhost provides a [Statistic Channels module](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/ee045a3d-05a6-409a-b435-7d170c5e70c3/statisticchannels)
 for its users. This module will allow you to keep track of metrics and statistics for your server within voice channels in your channel list.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#settings)

Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#new-counter-setup)

New Counter Setup

In this area, you can view and modify the settings of the Statistic Channels module. Below you may find some information on each setting of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fn6yN2g3zwUme1UIDc13J%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf93e3d8-1019-4e8b-8248-0a9f40fadfbc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c9634c8&sv=2)

**Note:** To set up a new statistic channel, you'll need to create a voice channel. Need help? [View Discord's guide on how to create a voice channel](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/19583625604887-Voice-Channels-FAQs#h_01HGXJWRPAZBM3FY6333C9WBQ3)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#channel-selection-type)

Channel Selection Type

This setting allows you to customize how to select your voice channel.

Dropdown Menu

Channel ID Input

The Dropdown Menu option allows you to select your voice channel from a dropdown list of channels in your server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F7sac76vUENmY8RK6vacZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcbc9e178-7ac0-4092-ad30-d97f01c3ed12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad9845da&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#channel-selection)

Channel Selection

This setting allows you to select your voice channel to track the metrics you set for this channel.

The Channel ID Input option allows you to select your voice channel by pasting the ID of the channel into the dashboard.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F7YwB8fSfhmLU0PZgmPQW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87c2bb8f-5987-41d5-b84d-8660fac06082&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49dd2668&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#channel-id)

Channel ID

This setting allows you to paste the ID of your voice channel to track the metrics you set for this channel. You can also use a variable.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#channel-name)

Channel Name

This field is where you input the channel name for the statistic channel. You can use the `{value}` [variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 to reference the metric.

To save the statistic channel's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will create an [Active Counters](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#active-counters)
 and an [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#events)
 for those settings. Additionally, the fields in this section will be reset so you can setup another channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#statistic-type)

Statistic Type

You will be able to choose from one of these metrics to track.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FDHtxlg56UPzpKyHqDHQC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D812dece1-26b3-4a4d-b940-cd6152fdc6a0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91191d24&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#auto-lock-channel)

Auto-Lock Channel

If this switch is enabled then the channel will be locked, meaning no users will be able to join those channels, unless there is a role or admin permission overriding that.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#active-counters)

Active Counters

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FHMKIcra656xBXyDgdABI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1609a363-288b-45da-bc77-38b99276da01&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c129487b&sv=2)

When adding a new statistic channel, it and its settings will appear in this section. All statistic channels will be ordered by the number in which they were created. To view, edit, and delete the settings you selected for that channel, simply click the statistic channel you wish to do so for.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXTN7nBpHZnVVhASCCf6D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec63bdf4-f2f9-4b18-a9f0-5638b22349fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf26c889&sv=2)

To save the edits you made on the statistic channel's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#events)

Events


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Statistic Channels module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module. All statistic channels will be ordered by the number in which they were created.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2bl8cHtoNN24RBndNr5m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9945e76e-d4e7-484b-8365-4f9b962247bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cee1ec&sv=2)

Statistic Channel #...[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/statistic-channels#statistic-channel)

Once a active counter has been added, the corresponding event will be shown in this section. You can edit the logic within them to your liking.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Roblox Verification | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FmrP8EmmnCOqUfkvu76EB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17b52d25-9317-4933-9526-0e00da0bdd8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ca41e10&sv=2)

**T**his module is only available to user with a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
.

The [Roblox Verification](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/ab8c166e-af43-46b7-8077-d92b4817b755/robloxverification) module allows users to connect their Roblox account to their in server Discord account, this is incredibly helpful for servers made for a Roblox group or if you want to setup some form of Roblox verification system for your Discord server.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#settings)

Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#setup)

Setup

The setup section of this page allows you to customize your experience with the module. From changing the trigger to adding a role to users upon successful verification and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FtG8XepPyCemUygxiX527%252Fimage_2024-07-17_162109728.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63f8f131-5088-4b65-a142-3fd3723e71f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=820fccd&sv=2)

Roblox Verification Module Settings

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#button-or-command)

**Button or Command**

Here you can change the trigger method for the verification to either a button or command.

Command

Button

Setting it to a command (default) will allow users to run the `/roblox-verify` command in the server to begin the verification.

If the button type is selected then it will send a embed message with a button attached for users to click to start the verification.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#message)

Message

In this field is where you can edit the button message. You can switch it from an [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 type to a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 type using the toggle in the top right of the image.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FsujexInapAYbmFUtJHuV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd584bb56-a2d7-4a45-9fe5-fe297d23bbb5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5b4bdc7&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#start-verification-button-text)

Start Verification Button Text

This field is where you can edit the text of the button that users will click to start the verification.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FNRqTKquCnEkXO5Pwt2ZG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba357eeb-45dc-4688-9e0a-7952452636e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=abc1e7b8&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#confirm-verification-button-text)

Confirm Verification Button Text

This field is where you can edit the text of the button that users will click to confirm the verification.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F4lZ2yxyCrhcHqpf63aV6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc1599fc-1d97-4c63-ae28-a5e12e44b641&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3398d03&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#grant-role)

**Grant Role**

Toggling this setting on and off will enable / disable the function of the bot giving a role upon successful verification. By default this option is enabled.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#verified-role)

**Verified Role**

This setting will allow you to choose a role to be granted to the user upon successful verification. _This setting is only visible with_ [Grant Role](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#grant-role)
 _enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#change-nickname)

**Change Nickname**

Toggling this setting on and off will enable / disable the function of the bot changing the users nickname upon successful verification. By default this option is enabled.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#username-or-display-name)

**Username or Display name**

This setting will allow you to choose what nickname the bot should change the users name to upon successful verification. You are able to choose between their Roblox display name or username. _This setting is only visible with_ [Change Nickname](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#change-nickname)
 _enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-rankbind-groups)

Roblox Rankbind Groups

In this section you can paste the ID's of the Roblox groups you wish to attach with rankbinds. There is a limit of 5.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-gamepasses)

Roblox Gamepasses

In this section you can paste the ID's of the Roblox gamepasses that should be integrated with the module.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#commands)

Commands


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Roblox Verification module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FGYoGtFV8zwop1RxSz0KS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b333917-fad0-415c-abcf-46f829585327&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af52857d&sv=2)

/roblox-verify[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-verify)

Depending on the [Button or Command](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#button-or-command)
 setting, this command will start the verification when the user runs it or it will post the button message in the channel the command was ran in for users to click to start the verification process. Note, for the button message to be sent, the command user must have the manage channel**s** permission.

/roblox-profile[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-profile)

When this command is ran, it will display the selected users Roblox profile. Additionally, if you leave the user option blank, it will display the command runners profile. This command has a 30 second cooldown period by default, this can only be changed in the command builder itself.

/roblox-rank-binds-view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-rank-binds-view)

When this command is run, it will display the rankbinds for your connected Roblox groups.

/roblox-rank-binds-remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-rank-binds-remove)

When this command is run, it will allow you to remove one of the rankbinds for your connected Roblox groups

/roblox-rank-binds-add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-rank-binds-add)

When this command is run, it will allow you to add to the rankbinds for your connected Roblox groups.

/roblox-gamepass-view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-gamepass-view)

When this command is run, it will display the gamepass links for your connected Roblox groups.

/roblox-gamepass-add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-gamepass-add)

When this command is run, it will allow you to add to the the gamepass links for your connected Roblox groups.

/roblox-gamepass-remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-gamepass-remove)

When this command is run, it will allow you to remove one of the gamepass links for your connected Roblox groups.

/roblox-update-user[](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#roblox-update-user)

When this command is run, it will allow you to update a users profile to get up to date information and role connections.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#settings)
    
*   [Setup](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#setup)
    
*   [Commands](https://documentation.botghost.com/game-integrations/roblox-verification#commands)
    

Was this helpful?

# Welcomer | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FtZBcU2ZLLXaqRv7baPoD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D697190cb-47e8-4193-88e2-03116b6007f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=871142ac&sv=2)

Some of the features of this module require a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function. You can however use the module with a free subscription.

The [Welcomer](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/b65529b9-b196-4088-8fef-3eaff0b0c047/welcomer)
 module will allow you to send custom welcome banners, messages, reactions, and add roles to users when they join the server. This module will also allow you to send a message when a user is kicked or banned, all in one.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#common-issues)

Common Issues


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Experiencing issues with the module? Check out the common issues below. If your issue is not listed in this page, make sure your module is updated to the latest version. If you are still experiencing issues with the module, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#message-not-sending)

Message not sending

If your welcome message is not being sent, try the following steps:

1

Check the Discord server permissions of your bot: make sure your bot has the "Send messages" and "View Channel" permissions and that there are no overwrites for the selected channel, or just give your bot the "Administrator" permissions.

2

Check if your bot intents (message intent) are enabled on the [Discord Developer Portal](https://discord.com/developers/applications)
. Ensure the message intent is also enabled in the settings page. See [Privileged Intent Options](https://documentation.botghost.com/general-settings-and-collaboration/settings#privileged-intent-options)
 for more info.

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#welcome-card-not-working)

Welcome card not working

If the welcome card isn't working/sending you can try:

1

Check if the image URL is a valid file type (PNG, JPG, JPEG). A valid image url should end with `.png`, `.jpg` or `.jpeg`.

2

Don't use Discord attachment links: after some time, they expire and cannot be used outside of Discord (including BotGhost).

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 for further assistance.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#watch-the-tutorial)

Watch the Tutorial


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#settings)

Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#welcome-card)

**Welcome Card**

Customize the card to your liking. You can configure many different aspects of the card as below.

Features in this section are limited to [Premium](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 users.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FeMndv0VwNXFFyOSXhhVD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f44f329-6f53-42b1-b397-a7dbd9d4befe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53df9909&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#welcome-card-1)

\[👑\] Welcome Card

Type

Details

Disabled

If the welcome cards are disabled then no cards will be sent when a user joins the server.

Send to a channel

This selection type will send the welcome card to a specified channel when someone joins.

Message the user

This dropdown type will send a direct message to the user.

Send to a channel and message the user

If this option is selected it will send the message to both the channel and the user's direct messages.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#channel)

\[👑\] Channel

Select a channel from your server to send the welcome card to.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#background)

\[👑\] Background

Choose a custom background from your card. You have 3 options for this. Depending on the option chosen it will change the background color.

Plain Color background

Default Background Image

Custom Background Image

If "Plain Color" is chosen, you will simply choose from the default color panel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FVRsUUMt0PfI2R5o8oyfz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad9fffa0-de6e-4ebb-8ee7-1568cd2570d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5615d6d2&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#background-color)

\[👑\] Background - Color

This allows you to select the background color that will be used for the card.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#example-card)

Example Card

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FYJIVpvOh5UQLhW1ZB1rG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D826d0475-deaa-454e-bebb-4ea0877ebdc8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73c6bd33&sv=2)

If "Default Background" is chosen you can pick one of the default background cards BotGhost provides, available in 8 colors including Red, Yellow, Blue, Purple and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FosPagjanF4QlcKbdOEbw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deeca02d8-46f7-42ee-b4f1-cfe1c6ee3708&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbfe30ee&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#background-default-card-color)

\[👑\] Background - Default Card Color

This setting allows you to pick your favorite color for the default background card.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#example-cards)

Example Cards

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1jDmoyTYKfGHEVGvWQOR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De13ab161-2725-4c03-a273-b01bef395db8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28c23fcf&sv=2)

If "Custom Background" is chosen then the card can be a color or any image you provide by entering it into the field below.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FfFZtRpkThLnkcQsM5pE9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D569af822-9b39-4215-b0a5-fa941170ae3f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4467e96&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#background-image)

\[👑\] Background - Image

Paste the URL of the image that will be used as a background. Make sure it's a valid image URL (ends with `.png`, `.jpg` or `.jpeg`). You should not use Discord attachment links as they expire after some time and cannot be used outside the platform. The recommended size of the image is 1024x500 pixels.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#example-card-1)

Example Card

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1ctD1NXn7A2mKVP455lK%252FWelcome%2520Card%2520reference%2520of%2520the%2520Welcomer%2520Module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0bda508-1219-4c74-83c0-0eb5c985943a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=544242e1&sv=2)

Welcome Card reference

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#title-color)

\[👑\] Title Color

This section represents the color for the title of the welcome card.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#description-color)

\[👑\] Description Color

This section represents the color for the description of the welcome card.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#avatar-border-color)

\[👑\] Avatar Border Color

This section represents the color for the avatar border of the welcome card.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#banner-title)

\[👑\] Banner Title

This section is how you can edit the banner title for the welcome card. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#banner-description)

\[👑\] Banner Description

This field is how you can edit the banner's description. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables) can be used as well.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#channel-reactions)

\[👑\] Channel Reactions

Choose up to 5 reactions that can be added to the welcome card message.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#message-on-join)

Message on Join

When enabled, this action allows for a message to be sent to a specific channel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F0OQD3qUcZMrWZK4aFqPt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37c9434c-b06c-416d-82c6-3b4453aca86e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e6d2b42&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#channel-1)

Channel

Select the channel from this dropdown for the message to be sent to.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#welcome-message)

Welcome Message

This field is where you input the welcome message for when the user joins. You are able to pick from either [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 response types. You are also able to use the `{card}` variable inside the image url section of the embed response type to show your welcome card in the same message. Some [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can also be used, such as `{user}`.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#reactions)

Reactions

Choose up to 5 reactions that can be added to the message.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#direct-message-on-join)

Direct message on Join

When enabled, this action allows for a message to be sent as a direct message to the user who joined.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXKuv8gphqlcgR5tjoLHf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfab4093f-385e-4ce2-9fac-2b572a213549&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7257b813&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#welcome-direct-message)

Welcome Direct Message

This field is where you input the welcome message for when the user joins. You are able to pick from either [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 response types. You are also able to use the `{card}` variable inside the image url section of the embed response type to show your welcome card in the same message. Some [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can also be used, such as `{user}`.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#add-role-on-join)

Add Role on Join

When this switch is enabled, it acts as an auto-role feature for the server, adding any roles from the server to the user who joined.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FzDslxkIlGOeDDzA69uHW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb1ff3cd-7f58-43a4-a4e8-b48ae278866d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e079b8db&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#roles-to-add-on-join)

Roles to add on join

This section is where you can add any roles you wish from any server the bot is in. The roles will be added to the user from the respective server they joined.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#wait-for-rules-acceptance)

Wait for rules acceptance

Enabling this switch will add the roles only after the user has accepted the server rules from the membership screening page. The server must have this setup for this to function correctly.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#message-on-leave)

Message on Leave

Define whether you wish to enable or disable the message that gets sent when a user leaves the server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FBAZm3mzNXUYlmOzd9JW7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff062b4d-24c1-4d2c-b5ec-826bce2a956d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cde9590b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#channel-2)

Channel

Select the channel from the dropdown that the message will get sent to upon a user leaving.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#leave-message)

Leave message

This field is where you will input the message that gets sent when the user leaves. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used. You can also choose from either a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 response type.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#reactions-1)

Reactions

Choose up to 5 reactions to be added to the message.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#message-on-kick)

Message on Kick

Define whether you wish to enable or disable the message that gets sent when a user is kicked from the server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FbEtuvP2RSpWas3IwFLTb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D159c90f4-1ca5-4d3a-856a-e71c508f374e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f925c21b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#channel-3)

Channel

Select the channel from the dropdown that the message will get sent to upon a user that gets kicked.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#kick-message)

Kick message

This field is where you will input the message that gets sent when the user is kicked. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used. You can also choose from either a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 response type.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#reactions-2)

Reactions

Choose up to 5 reactions to be added to the message.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#message-on-ban)

Message on Ban

Define whether you wish to enable or disable the message that gets sent when a user is banned from the server.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FFXUtbGwUJxlJulIGoz2D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D236322a8-8e9d-41a0-8f5e-80aacee37cbf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=980aeaf0&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#channel-4)

Channel

Select the channel from the dropdown that the message will get sent to upon a user that gets banned.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#ban-message)

Ban message

This field is where you will input the message that gets sent when the user is banned. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used. You can also choose from either a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 or [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 response type.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#reactions-3)

Reactions

Choose up to 5 reactions to be added to the message.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#events)

Events


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Welcomer module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FIke7U5B3GXJjMUKXPQev%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62100a0d-061b-462b-a1e6-9be4ca51e26c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b091066e&sv=2)

Joins Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#joins-handler)

This event contains the welcoming card, the message on join, and the role addition.

Leaves and Kicks Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#leaves-and-kicks-handler)

These events contain the message on leave and the message on kick.

Bans Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/server-management/welcomer#bans-handler)

This event contains the message on ban.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FF52F06AdM7ZTVHswxfF9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf4bca83-1388-426b-aacd-4968b3b6c81f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b9dd89e&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Global Chat](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/41821e81-015f-463d-9999-c5d89b064608/globalchat)
 module will allow users to connect multiple text channels, even in different servers!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#settings)

Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#global-chat-settings)

**Global Chat Settings**

These are the settings that allow you to customize the [Global Chat](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/41821e81-015f-463d-9999-c5d89b064608/globalchat)
 module, this will allow you to configure permissions, cooldowns and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FrCHeJofqBqX3JqtgzlAK%252Fimage_2024-07-09_113445404.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff7a6c00-206c-4396-bfa5-7845b09149aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e93d358&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#admin-role)

**Admin Role**

This selection will allow you to setup an admin role. Users with these roles will be able to run admin commands paired with the module. They will be able to reset settings, blacklist users and globally delete messages.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#manager-role)

**Manager Role**

This selection will allow you to setup a manager role. Users with the roles selected will be able to manage global chat channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#manager-permissions)

**Manager Permissions**

This setting will allow you to toggle the manager permission and when enabled, users with the manage guild permission can moderate and configure global chat channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#message-type)

**Message Type**

In this field you can change the type of message that is sent to the other channels, by default this is set to webhook.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#message-cooldown)

**Message Cooldown**

This setting will allow you to choose a rate limit in seconds users can send messages with. There is a minimum of 5 seconds.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#forward-attachment)

**Forward Attachment**

This toggle will allow you to enable whether or not to include attached images, videos, or GIFs in the message sent to the global chat channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#automatic-reaction)

**Automatic Reaction**

If you add an emoji to this setting, the bot will automatically react with this emoji to messages sent to global chat channels. You can use the format [here](https://docs.botghost.com/getting-started/standard-practices/advanced-practices#how-can-i-get-a-custom-emojis-id)
 or a default discord emoji. A default emoji is applied, and if made blank then this setting is disabled.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#message-settings)

Message Settings

This section will allow you to customize the global chat messages. The settings are different depending on the type chosen from [Message Type](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#message-type)
.

Webhook Message

Bot Message

Choosing this type will make the message sent be in the form of a webhook.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1AdszOx8sG5OR53r36w1%252Fimage_2024-07-09_113321963.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05fcc7f8-74f3-4dc9-862d-ed2d8c440c8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=105f1434&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#webhook-name)

**Webhook Name**

This field configures the text that will appear in the username section of the webhook message. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used in this field.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#webhook-icon)

**Webhook Icon**

This field configures an image that appears in the user icon section of the webhook message. You may use the {user\_icon} [variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 / image link.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#webhook-message-1)

**Webhook Message**

In this field you can input the message that is sent to the global chat channels. All [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used.

Choosing this type will make the message be in the form of the bot's message.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fm3M7pkYwPSLquBg7i3aZ%252Fimage_2024-07-09_113250552.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6da5cad6-2b76-420b-8491-adc85ca3ecb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d6d8790&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#message)

Message

In this field you can input the message that is sent to the global chat channels. All [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#blacklist-settings)

Blacklist Settings

In this section, you can configure the blacklist settings such as blacklisted roles or blocked expressions.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FtOuqx2CZS4qAmIgPeTVV%252Fimage_2024-07-09_113157215.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D520f2e02-ad9b-4b65-b08d-40201d6453a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c06b6075&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#blacklist-users)

**Blacklist Users**

This toggle if enabled, allows you give permissions to users with the manager role to be able to blacklist users using the `/globalchat-moderate` command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#blacklisted-roles)

**Blacklisted Roles**

This selection will allow you to choose some roles to restrict the global chat from. Users that have one of these roles can't chat in global-chat channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#blocked-expressions)

**Blocked Expressions**

In this section you can set some keywords / phrases to block when using global chat. Any global-chat message that contains any of those blocked expressions won't be sent.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#commands)

Commands


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Global Chat module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjYuFiUUjHGLvNpmx8uRv%252Fimage_2024-07-09_113122555.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd044421-594e-4ca9-813c-df9a508e5d0d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96c7f627&sv=2)

/globalchat-setup[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#globalchat-setup)

This command will allow you set a global chat channel for the entire system to use.

/globalchat-disable[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#globalchat-disable)

This command will disable a current global chat channel so that messages sent in this channel won't be global anymore.

/globalchat-moderate[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#globalchat-moderate)

With this command you can punish users and moderate global chat channels.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#events)

Events


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Global Chat module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUSEjQtYq3tWlaEK8fGrj%252Fimage_2024-07-09_113138561.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96881ed2-1791-4454-afc6-4341461e606a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=278c4e49&sv=2)

Global Chat[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/global-chat#global-chat)

This event handles the main core functions of the module and connects the global chat channels across different servers to each other.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago
