# Media Channels | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvEAkbnnhwHD21LMOAruf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9878d44d-1768-4749-9e28-49aee22e82e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f369120d&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Media Channels](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/c3efeefb-654e-4893-8a16-ede851b62007/mediachannels)
 module will allow you to define channels where only images can be sent. Regular text messages will be deleted when sent into one of these channels.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#settings)

Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#channel-setup)

Channel Setup

In this area, you can choose which channel you would like to become a media channel. Once these settings are configured, click the add button in the bottom right shown in the image below.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FksJurcVJDA0D1TGKnZEr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73c443ba-412a-41a5-a534-76c3c84c8678&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b59abadb&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#channel-type)

Channel Type

With this selection you can choose what type of channel will become a media channel. You may choose from either a regular text channel or a forum channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#text-channel)

Text Channel

From this dropdown you can choose the channel from your server that you would like to become a media channel. Reminder that a media channel only allows for images to be sent so no message can be sent without an image.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#whitelisted-roles)

Whitelisted Roles

In this selection you can pick roles that you would like whitelisted. Whitelisted roles will not be moderated by the module and users with these roles can send any content they wish.

To save the media channel's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another media channel.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#active-media-channels)

Active Media Channels

Once you have added a media channel from the settings above, a new area will appear that contains all the active media channels. Currently the maximum is 10 media channels. You may edit / delete any of these active media channels on the bottom right of the image below.

To save the edits you made on the media channel's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Ff9beWCMVGhrES8JfHMhA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3a1ced6-6926-4b0a-b335-7d4b5def6b5a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d635a08e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#channel-settings)

Channel Settings

In this section you can configure the channel limits and moderation for your media channels.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FIIMeG2180BrbPgiBnuX1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7688c343-dee4-439c-8bdc-9dde5f6e2647&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcb17130&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#allow-text-content)

Allow Text Content

This toggle will allow you to choose if you would like any message's content to contain text alongside an image.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#allow-gifs-and-embeds)

Allow GIFs and Embeds

This toggle if enabled, will allow gifs and embeds to be sent to your media channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#block-duplicated-attachments)

Block Duplicated Attachments

If this toggle is enabled it will block attachments that are sent more than once in a media channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#maximum-attachments-and-embeds)

Maximum Attachments and Embeds

With this field you can decide how many attachments or embeds can be sent before the message is deleted. The maximum is 100 and the minimum is 0. This field only accepts integers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#channel-rate-limit)

Channel Rate Limit

With this field you can enable a channel rate limit or in other terms, a slowmode in seconds, for your media channel. This field only accepts integers and the maximum is 3600 seconds. If this option is set to 0 that will disable it.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#allowed-media-type)

Allowed Media Type

Here you can choose the type of media you want to allow in your channel. If you are looking for customizing the possible file extensions that can be sent, choose the Advanced type.

All Media Types

Images only

Videos only

Advanced

This option will allow all media types to be sent.

This option will only allow images to be sent.

This option will only allow videos to be sent.

This option will allow you to input certain file types that are allowed in the channel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1BCQELJVh68pAd1hANux%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadbe42cc-7e0a-4823-81d1-447614872bfe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=138c550b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#restrict-file-types)

Restrict File Types

This field allows you to specify the file types you want to be allowed in your media channel. Input the file extension in the box in the left and click the send key on your keyboard to add it to the list.

Type

Details

All Media Types

This option will allow all media types to be sent.

Images only

This option will only allow images to be sent.

Videos only

This option will only allow videos to be sent.

Advanced

This option will allow you to input certain file types that are allowed in the channel.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1BCQELJVh68pAd1hANux%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadbe42cc-7e0a-4823-81d1-447614872bfe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=138c550b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#enable-error-message)

Enable Error Message

This toggle allows you to enable an error message when a message gets deleted inside a media channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#error-message)

Error Message

If enabled by the toggle above, you can customize the error message that will be sent if a user sends a message without attachments to your media channels. The message will appear for 10 seconds in the media channel, and mention the user. You can use all [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 and the {reason} variable to get the deletion reason.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FpMFthnr20E28zoDx6fqe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc5304ed-1637-4e13-879e-2db1297298e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b990ca6a&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#events)

Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Media Channels module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOB3dg3hadTdUESjtokMh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ec0b98c-a381-4ed0-9892-66f6c18da885&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b95ce8cf&sv=2)

MediaChannel Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#mediachannel-handler)

This is the main event for the module, this will handle the deletion of text messages sent into the media channel.

MediaChannel Edit Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/media-channels#mediachannel-edit-handler)

This is the same as the other handler, except it will only look for messages that get edited to moderate.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Counting | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhH6hTAcMuzVPXkMGyhm0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da70fd64d-454a-4b13-a7f9-15632dcdea6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=503a75bb&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Counting](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/5206b1e7-f841-4d04-8c09-2f0bfe28b50e/counting)
 module allows your server members to engage in a fun counting activity, see how high you can go with this unlimited counting module!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#settings)

Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#general-settings)

General Settings

Here you can configure the main settings for the counting module, from setting the counting channel to changing the counting mode.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FzKSisNsposhiyHlaDjLf%252Fimage_2024-07-22_210628809.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05bd8af7-2fd7-4fb5-9d94-8e702cf752d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3261ab6&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#counting-mode)

**Counting Mode**

Here you can change the mode of the counting which will adjust the behavior of the bot in the counting channel.

Mode

Details

Normal

This mode will simply add a reaction to the users message if they send the correct number to the channel.

Webhook

This mode will delete the users message and repost it in a webhook format to make it appear as though a bot version of the user sent it if the count is correct.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#channel)

**Channel**

Here you can select the channel you want the counting event to work in, channels not selected here will not trigger the counting module.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#reactions)

**Reactions**

If this toggle is enabled, and if [Counting Mode](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#counting-mode)
 is set to 'Normal', then the bot will add a reaction to the correct number.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#reaction-emoji)

Reaction Emoji

If [Reactions](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#reactions)
 is enabled, then you can add the reaction that you want the bot to add to the messages.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#allow-multiple-counts)

**Allow Multiple Counts**

If this toggle is enabled, users will be able to count more than once in a row.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#cooldown)

**Cooldown**

Here you can enable / disable a 5 second channel wide cooldown which will prevent users from sending another count for 5 seconds after one has just been sent.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#error-settings)

Error Settings

Here you can configure the error settings for the counting module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FltrouuaThxJPRN0teGoa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defe7b6a4-99aa-4d60-b9d6-56edcce78a26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d558dab&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#return-errors)

**Return Errors**

If this toggle is enabled, all errors described in the settings below will be active.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#error-message-for-wrong-count)

**Error Message For Wrong Count**

If [Return Errors](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#return-errors)
 is enabled, you can set the message that will be displayed to user for sending the wrong count to the channel. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#error-message-for-counting-twice)

**Error Message For Counting Twice**

If [Return Errors](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#return-errors)
 is enabled and if [Allow Multiple Counts](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#allow-multiple-counts)
 is also disabled, you can set the message that will be displayed to user for sending 2 or more counts without waiting for another user to count.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#error-message-for-the-cooldown)

**Error Message For The Cooldown**

If [Return Errors](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#return-errors)
 is enabled, you can set the message that will be displayed to the user if they try to count during the 5 second cooldown if [Cooldown](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#cooldown)
 is enabled.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#commands)

Commands


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Counting module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvfyNNPNCc2rInnNVPoqw%252Fimage_2024-07-22_211952298.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De190edd5-2fbd-4a47-bc43-b3b1b19d1334&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=145c042e&sv=2)

/counting-set[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#counting-set)

This command allows you to set the current count of the module to any new number.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#events)

Events


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Counting module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1wO28L5N22rv5LSbSlUR%252Fimage_2024-07-22_212134184.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7437b1e4-f5c2-4d24-8563-a11338f63962&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45f8d6a8&sv=2)

Counting[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/counting#counting)

This event handles all the module functions such as the errors, tracking the number, and all other settings.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Temp Voice Channels | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJmByNxLWUxCqFByvnVRn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84831d2d-e7a8-46b5-a051-c0e60a547843&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=efeab39b&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Temp Voice Channels](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/ca3589f7-3846-4f70-8863-7f601cb29e9f/tempvoicechannels)
 module allows you to setup an advanced temporary voice channels system in your guild. This module allows users to connect to a main voice channel to create their own cool private temporary channels.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#main-settings)

Main Settings

Find out about what customization options are available with the module and what each of them does.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXaLa7fy5xK1Ap9vytVWI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6e5106b-e72e-4452-adaa-259fb37b79a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5429950&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#channel-creator-hub)

Channel Creator Hub

This setting allows you to define the 'hub' voice channel users will connect to, to create their own temp voice channels. Only one can be selected.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#channel-category)

Channel Category

This setting allows you to define what category the new temp voice channels will be created in.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#role-permission-criteria)

Role Permission Criteria

This setting will allow you to choose to disable / enable the module functionalities for users with the defined roles. By default this is set to 'No Restrictions'.

Type

Details

No Restrictions

All server roles can create temp voice channels.

Enabled for these roles only

Users with only these certain roles selected will be able to create temp voice channels.

Disabled for these roles

Users with all other roles besides the ones selected will be able to create temp voice channels.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#channel-settings)

Channel Settings

Here you can customize the channels settings for the newly created voice channels.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJTUo9X5Hd4NFb7vp9yOX%252Fimage_2024-07-18_210646850.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5c2a544c-6808-458d-a5c3-bb99a47ae023&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49a60840&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#created-channel-name)

Created Channel Name

Here you can define the name which the channels uses when it is created. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#channel-lock)

Channel Lock

Here you can choose whether newly created channels should be locked or unlocked by default. Locked channels only allow whitelisted users to join! The default option is set to unlocked.

Type

Details

Follow Server's Permissions

The channel will follow your server's permissions.

Unlocked

No restrictions will be applied and users can join.

Locked

The channel is restricted and not all users can join unless they are whitelisted.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#owner-permissions)

Owner Permissions

This toggle option will allow you to disable / enable the creator of the voice channel having access to the Manage Channel, Priority Speaker, Move Members and Manage Permissions permission flags to the voice channel they created.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#mention-creator)

Mention Creator

This toggle option when enabled, will ping the voice channel creator once the channel is made along with sending the information.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#deletion-wait-time)

Deletion Wait Time

Here you can define the amount of seconds the module deletes a temporary channel in after all members have left. The maximum is 3600 seconds and only integers are allowed as an input.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#user-limit)

User Limit

Here you can select the maximum number of users allowed to join your channel. When the member count in the channel reaches this defined number, no one else will be able to join unless someone else leaves. The maximum is 99 users and only integers are allowed as an input.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#channel-bitrate)

Channel Bitrate

In this field you can input a number of seconds that discord should handle the voice channels with. Maximum is 96000 and the minimum is 8000. Only integers can be used.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#commands)

Commands


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Temp Voice Channels module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

All Commands that come with this module must be used in the created voice channels chat.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FRtWZNzL9srMEjqfb6JwC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debf7b049-1cba-4a6a-9151-49cc1bcb4206&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=483c49dc&sv=2)

/tempvc-whitelist[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#tempvc-whitelist)

This command will allow voice channel owners to whitelist a user, once whitelisted they will be able to join their locked voice channel.

/tempvc-blacklist[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#tempvc-blacklist)

This command will allow voice channel owners to blacklist a user, once blacklisted they will not be able to join their voice channel.

/tempvc-lock[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#tempvc-lock)

This command will allow voice channel owners to lock their voice channel. Once locked, only whitelisted users will be able to join it.

/tempvc-unlock[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#tempvc-unlock)

This command will allow voice channel owners to unlocked their voice channel. Once unlocked, all users will be able to join it.

/tempvc-kick[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#tempvc-kick)

This command will allow voice channel owners to kick users from their voice channel.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#events)

Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Temp Voice Channels module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FgN4z81IUG5uMh7YlE9sz%252Fimage_2024-07-18_211958774.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac62493e-a840-4848-a111-a672f9d6ff02&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f25cd01&sv=2)

VC Join Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#vc-join-handler)

This event handles the system that procs when users join a temp voice channel.

VC Leave Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#vc-leave-handler)

This event manages deleting the channel after the specified period once all users have left.

VC Switch - Join Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#vc-switch-join-handler)

This event tracks users swapping voice channels to adjust the total member count for the channel they joined.

VC Switch - Leave Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/temp-voice-channels#vc-switch-leave-handler)

This event tracks users swapping voice channels to adjust the total member count for the channel they left.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Chance Condition | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/chance-condition.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FShzi0vv3w0Jq47u5jZGd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d77563c-ce41-40df-8a1e-da6f2d4ed85e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4e50787&sv=2)

This condition sets a percentage chance for actions to be taken. You cannot exceed 100%. The remainder of the blocks percentages are gathered in the else block.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/chance-condition#percent-chance)

Percent Chance


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This field is where you enter the percentage of how likely the action will be occurring. This field only accepts integers as values.

Click the Add Condition button to add the block to your builder.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPsm4zlyYuhNti3PuzA1R%252Fimage_2024-06-09_224145065.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0fdfd5b-b033-4a95-b825-78ca1465b612&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f08bb54&sv=2)

Here is an example layout of this condition:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FqKCiDcfpMT5fCwPMzwuR%252FBildschirm%25C2%25ADfoto%25202023-02-13%2520um%252021.01.56.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd17f4728-0b8c-4fe2-9dd3-e6f1df1ef122&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c428b5e0&sv=2)

# Events | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events.md)
.

The [Custom Events](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/customevents)
 module is where you can trigger actions based on things that occur in your server, on a timed basis, from an IFTTT trigger, and even from a BotGhost webhook.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#getting-started)

Getting Started


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Located in the Custom Events module, you will see the "New Custom Event" section, click the "Custom Event Builder" yellow block to create a new event.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXDICfQq2LnlzI7wYKpHa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9ba49a8-0191-4802-af24-5659dbe680ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec546e75&sv=2)

Click the "Custom Event Builder"

2

Select a custom event from the options currently provided.

These options will activate when a condition is met. For instance, if a user joins your server, you can then have the bot greet them, like the announcement module, and DM them.

3

Under the yellow main block, click on it and set an "Event Nickname". This will be shown in the dashboard if you are ever looking to edit a certain event. You can name it to whatever you'd want.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#blocks)

Blocks


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the custom event builder, the blocks you can use vary to the custom command builder. While creating an event, you cannot use options or certain conditions. As an example, you cannot use a "User Condition" in a timed event as the event has no user trigger. You can however use it if you have at least one button or select menu in your event.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#available-events)

Available Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The type of events you may use in the custom events builder can be found below.

Action Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#action-events)

Action Events are a category of pre-built, powerful events in BotGhost that combine multiple actions into a single block. They are designed to simplify the creation of common bot features, allowing you to accomplish complex tasks without needing multiple custom event blocks. Check out the [Action Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/action-events)
 page for more information.

Timed Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#timed-events)

Timed events are a special type of events that can run on a scheduled (every day at 5 pm) or a set interval (every 10 minutes). Check out the [Timed Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events)
 page for more.

IFTTT Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#ifttt-events)

IFTTT events can be triggered by IFTTT when something occurs (ex. you've created an applet that triggers a custom event when a video is posted on YouTube). Learn more on how to use them [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/ifttt#trigger-a-custom-event-ifttt-actions)
.

Webhook Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#webhook-events)

Webhook events can be triggered by an API Request sent to BotGhost. Learn more on the [Webhooks](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks)
 page.

Application Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#application-events)

The application events are based on actions in your server related to application command permissions.

*   When an application command’s permissions are updated
    

Audit Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#audit-events)

The audit events are based on actions in your server related to Discord’s audit log system.

*   When an audit log entry is created
    

Auto Moderation Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#auto-moderation-events)

The Auto Moderation events are based on actions in your server related to Discord’s built-in AutoMod feature.

*   When an Auto Moderation action is executed
    
*   When an Auto Moderation rule is created
    
*   When an Auto Moderation rule is deleted
    
*   When an Auto Moderation rule is updated
    

Boost Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#boost-events)

The boost events are based on actions in your server related to server boosts.

*   When a member boosts the server for the first time
    
*   When a member unboosts the server
    
*   When a server boost level increases
    
*   When a server boost level decrease
    

Bot Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#bot-events)

The bot events are related to actions that occur within your bot.

*   When the bot joins a server
    
*   When the bot leaves a server
    
*   When the bot starts or is restarted
    
*   When a custom variable's value changes
    
*   When the bot is updated through the dashboard
    

Channel Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#channel-events)

The channel events are based on actions in your server that are related to channels.

*   When a channel is created
    
*   When a channel is deleted
    
*   When a channel is updated
    
*   When a channel's permissions are updated
    
*   When a guild channel’s topic is updated
    
*   When a channel’s pins are updated
    

Invite Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#invite-events)

The invite events are based on actions in your server that are related to invites.

*   When a invite is created
    
*   When a invited is deleted
    

Member Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#member-events)

The member events are based on actions in your server that are related to users.

*   When a new user joins the serer
    
*   When a user is banned from the server
    
*   When a user is unbanned from the server
    
*   When a user leaves or is kicked from the server
    
*   When a role is added to a user
    
*   When a role is removed from a user
    
*   When a guild member is updated
    
*   When a user changes their nickname
    
*   When a user changes their status
    
*   When a guild’s features are updated
    
*   When a guild’s ownership is transferred to another user
    
*   When a guild becomes a Partner
    
*   When a guild loses its Partner status
    
*   When a guild’s name is changed
    
*   When an AFK channel is set
    
*   When the AFK channel is removed
    
*   When a guild banner is added
    
*   When a guild banner is removed
    
*   When a member passes membership screening
    
*   When a guild’s integrations are updated
    

Message Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#message-events)

The message events are based on actions in your server that are related to messages.

*   When a new message is sent
    
*   When a message is updated or edited
    
*   When a message is deleted
    
*   When a message is pinned
    
*   When a user starts typing
    

Music Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#music-events)

The music events are events triggered by [music actions](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/music-actions)
 and the [music module](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music)
.

*   Track Events
    
    *   When a track starts playing
        
    *   When a track finishes playing
        
    *   When the queue finishes playing
        
    *   When a track encounters an error
        
    *   When a track gets stuck/frozen
        
    
*   Player Controls
    
    *   When playback is started
        
    *   When playback is paused
        
    *   When playback is resumed
        
    *   When a track is skipped
        
    *   When seeking in a track
        
    *   When queue is shuffled
        
    *   When playback is stopped
        
    
*   Queue Events
    
    *   When a track is added to the queue
        
    *   When a track is removed from the queue
        
    
*   Settings Events
    
    *   When AutoPlay is toggled
        
    *   When AutoLeave is toggled
        
    *   When the player volume is changed
        
    *   When player loop mode is changed
        
    
*   Connection Events
    
    *   When bot connects to voice channel
        
    *   When bot disconnects from voice channel
        
    *   When bot is moved to a different voice channel
        
    *   When bot automatically leaves voice due to inactivity
        
    
*   System Events
    
    *   When a music player is created
        
    *   When a music player is destroyed
        
    *   When a music player switches Lavalink node
        
    *   When a music player's WebSocket connection closes
        
    *   When a music player state updates (fires frequently)
        
    
*   Other Music Events
    
    *   When audio filters are changed
        
    *   When player is resuming playback
        
    *   When player has successfully resumed
        
    *   When player mute status changes
        
    *   When player deaf status changes
        
    *   When a user joins the voice channel with the bot
        
    *   When a user leaves the voice channel with the bot
        
    

Poll Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#poll-events)

The poll events are based on actions in your server related to the discord builtin poll feature.

*   When a user votes on a poll
    
*   When a user removes their vote on a poll
    

Reaction Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#reaction-events)

The reaction events are based on actions in your server that are related to reactions on messages.

*   When a reaction is added to a message
    
*   When a reaction is removed from a message
    
*   When all reactions are removed from a message
    
*   When a specific reaction is removed from a message
    

Role Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#role-events)

The role events are based on actions in your server that are related to roles.

*   When a role is created
    
*   When a role is updated
    
*   When a role is deleted
    

Scheduled Events Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#scheduled-events-events)

The scheduled events events are based on actions in your server that are related to the scheduled events feature.

*   When a scheduled event is created
    
*   When a scheduled event is updated
    
*   When a scheduled event is deleted
    
*   When a user joins a scheduled event
    
*   When a user leaves a scheduled event
    

Stage Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#stage-events)

The stage events are based on actions in your server related to stage instances.

*   When a stage instance is created
    
*   When a stage instance is deleted
    
*   When a stage instance is updated
    

Sticker Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#sticker-events)

The sticker events are based on actions in your server related to stickers.

*   When a sticker is created
    
*   When a sticker is deleted
    
*   When a sticker is updated
    

Thread Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#thread-events)

The thread events are based on actions in your server that are related to threads or forum posts.

*   When a thread is created
    
*   When a thread is deleted
    
*   When a thread is updated
    
*   When thread lists are synced
    
*   When thread members are updated
    
*   When a thread member is updated
    

Voice Events[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#voice-events)

The voice events are based on actions in your server that are related to voice channels and users inside of them.

*   When a member joins a voice channel
    
*   When a member switches voice channels
    
*   When a member leaves a voice channel
    
*   When a member starts streaming in a voice channel
    
*   When a member stops streaming in a voice channel
    
*   When a member is server muted
    
*   When a member self mutes
    
*   When a member is server unmuted
    
*   When a member self unmutes
    
*   When a member is server deafened
    
*   When a member self deafens
    
*   When a member is server undeafened
    
*   When a member self undeafens
    
*   When a voice server is updated
    

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#variables)

**Variables**

All specific and special variables can be found in the variable tab, the variable list changes per event type.

All event specific variables can be found in the variable list (represented by a clipboard icon), that appears on every input in your event builder. Those vary per event type. Learn more about variables and other variable types in the [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 page.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhYDnO4FSTrjFPNFSetsD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e56828f-fe4c-470a-ac1a-3056304f164d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe972deb&sv=2)

Last updated 7 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Getting Started](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#getting-started)
    
*   [Blocks](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#blocks)
    
*   [Available Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#available-events)
    
*   [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events#variables)

# Weather | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FwEFJFILZg4JeuNVsj0Dq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d17c41c-2de0-490b-a7e3-b2b33cce669b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c79dc6&sv=2)

The [Weather](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/e09631dc-4f8f-4bf7-a02c-27ea0187d78f/weather)
 module is a simple way to get the weather of any location in the world directly to your bot.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#settings)

Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#measurement-scales)

Measurement Scales

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FSWiThaBzzzJ0TXB65GUF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82823ef2-f7be-456a-8e56-b241ba97351a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be9893bc&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#temperature-scale)

Temperature Scale

The unit of temperature to display the weather temperatures in. Can be set to Celsius or Fahrenheit.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#wind-scale)

Wind Scale

The unit of speed to display the wind speeds in. You are able to display the speeds in miles per hour (MPH) or kilometers per hour (KPH).

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#embed-configuration)

Embed Configuration

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fko0LMupHPBzQxd2Z2j4e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D762a8778-f5de-4693-b9d9-a931ad9f41b8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1376e82&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#display-images)

Display Images

The option to display weather related images in the command's embed.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#embed-color)

Embed Color

The embed color for all outputs in the weather command.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#commands)

Commands


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the command of the Weather module. Below you may find some information on the command of the module.

/weather[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/weather#weather)

Obtain the current and future weather information for any location in the world by providing a base location.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FuJqJh40j1pNyMvLY23Ri%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bf4ef52-35d8-4502-a2bf-488fcc1e534d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54565700&sv=2)

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the command unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited command will be created if you update the module.

# Data Storage | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage.md)
.

[Data storage](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/datastorage)
 is the first step in unlocking the ability for your bot to store data to be used by your bot, either per server or globally.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#what-are-variables)

What are variables


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom variables are 'placeholders' to store and access data across different commands, interactions and servers!

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#variable-types)

Variable Types

Variables can be set to text or numbers, but can also be made specific to a user or channel. Variables can also have a server specific or global scope, meaning it will be the same in all servers. Currently, we offer the following data types:

Variable Type

Information

Text

Stores a text value.

Number

Stores a simple number value.

Collection

Collections, that are also known as arrays, can store multiple data of the same type. Example, a collection made of User IDs. Learn more [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/collections)
.

Object

Object variables are variables that can store other sub-variables (or properties). Learn more [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage/objects)
.

Which can be either:

Type

Information

Can be Global / Server Specific?

Not user / channel specific

This means it can't contain a different value basing on the user or channel provided. It can also be global or server specific

User Specific

This means you can store a different value for every user.

Channel Specific

This means you can store a different value for each channel in your server.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#creating-a-new-variable)

Creating a New Variable


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create a new variable, head over to the [data storage](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/datastorage)
 module and go to the "New Variable" window.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FEPmGIDxwFoBG8javSlP2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a1e066c-b294-4272-99d9-689ad113e62a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=307ff665&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#variable-name)

Variable Name

In this field you can enter the name of your new variable. This will also be the reference for your variable.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#variable-reference)

Variable Reference

This is your variable reference, it will be `{BGVAR_variable_name}`, depending on what variable name you add. You can use this variable anywhere in your bot to get the variable value.

You do not need to enter anything in this field when creating a new variable.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#variable-type)

Variable Type

In this field you can enter the [type of your variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#variable-types)
, variables can be set to text or numbers, but can also be made specific to a user or channel.

If you select "User" or "Channel" here, you will get another field where you can choose to set the variable type to text, number, collection or object.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#default-value)

Default Value

In this field you can enter a default value that will be in the variable when nothing else has been set.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#scope)

Scope

In this field you can select whether you want to make your variable server specific or global, meaning it will be the same in all servers.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#editing-or-deleting-a-variable)

Editing or Deleting a Variable

To edit a custom variable, simply press the variable you want to edit in the module. You can then edit the variable in this window:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fmn1MixfZf9MOs2MrkaWM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D219d3a88-b87c-4c7b-a39c-3798c6f68548&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35eb3b13&sv=2)

Don't forget to press the "Edit Custom Variable" button and save changes!

You can also delete a custom variable from storage by pressing the "Delete" button.

Deleting a variable will not just clear the value of the variable, this will delete the variable from the storage

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#using-your-variable)

Using Your Variable


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#updating-your-variables-value)

Updating Your Variable's Value

Interacting with a variable on a non-premium bot will use 1 [call](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#free-database-usage-calls)
. This includes retrieving it in a response and updating it via the actions described below. The delete variable action won't use any calls.

To set or clear (delete) custom variables, you can use the Set Variable, Run Equation on Variable or Delete Variable actions in the [command and event builder](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/command-and-event-builder)
. You can read more about these actions [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/custom-variable-actions)
!

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FCaN7hQtOMTeOA9swDhaX%252FEFF436DA-6625-413E-8549-5C552E43495F.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D872007de-387a-4342-9a13-cf0e16409f5c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=481337b6&sv=2)

Command Builder actions: Set Variable, Run Equation on Vaiable & Delete Variable

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#retrieving-your-variable)

Retrieving Your Variable

You can get data stored in the data storage module by using an associated `{BGVAR_}` variable in other action blocks, for example: `{BGVAR_example}`.

You can get user and channel specific variables by targeting them, for example: `{BGVAR_example[ID]}`. You can learn more about targeting [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables#targeting)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FWpY1dzb1srmj125IfSqM%252F51ED887D-5F9D-4305-8FBF-2EF4617B2FDC.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24536b64-5266-44f4-8c45-2ca6c8fc2ff2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=104cc596&sv=2)

Plain Text Reply with a custom variable, {BGVAR\_exampe}

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#free-database-usage-calls)

**Free Database Usage (Calls)**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FNnCYBgD7gTNFgSrZKdG4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D317d49dd-e868-41c4-bd44-19f1b60a1f00&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5419f8c6&sv=2)

Every month, users get 500 calls to use across their **free** bots. Free bots will use 1 call every time they either create a variable or update the value of a variable. Only free bots use calls, premium bots can use unlimited data storage.

Your calls can not be reset manually, they will automatically reset on the first of each month. The data stored in them will not reset.

Experiencing issues with this module or need help? Check out our support options [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/support/botghost-support)
!

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [What are variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#what-are-variables)
    
*   [Variable Types](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#variable-types)
    
*   [Creating a New Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#creating-a-new-variable)
    
*   [Editing or Deleting a Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#editing-or-deleting-a-variable)
    
*   [Using Your Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#using-your-variable)
    
*   [Updating Your Variable's Value](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#updating-your-variables-value)
    
*   [Retrieving Your Variable](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#retrieving-your-variable)
    
*   [Free Database Usage (Calls)](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/data-storage#free-database-usage-calls)
    

Was this helpful?

# Autoresponder | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMZW2hY9KBccAFGsVFZTS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4d16829-50bc-4242-a77d-f98cd9281ea1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=84365334&sv=2)

The [Autoresponder](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/8de92a0c-1e68-4577-900d-26e2bda7b396/autoresponder)
 module will allow you to set keywords that will trigger a response from the bot. This can be from a simple "hello" to a whole sentence under the settings you select.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#settings)

Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#autoresponder-setup)

Autoresponder Setup

Customize the autoresponder in it's entirety and modify certain aspects or nothing at all. Click on the add button at the bottom right to add the autoresponder to the active list.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMUCxTAiaKb5NQYGBJhsS%252Fimage_2024-07-09_221223244.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9073427-4e81-4029-bf8a-d0694f78d57f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58e85ef5&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#trigger-detection-type)

**Trigger Detection Type**

Define how the bot should handle the trigger keywords, whether the message contains, is equal to, starts with, or ends with a keyword.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#trigger-keywords)

**Trigger Keywords**

Set the keywords that will trigger the autoresponder. Currently, up to 100 keywords for each active autoresponder.

To add the keyword, you may press 'Enter' in your keyboard. Added keywords will appear on the right.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#message)

Message

Configure the message content and type, whether you wish to send an embed or plain text. All [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#channel-cooldown)

**Channel Cooldown**

In this field you can input the channel cooldown in seconds between autoresponders.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#mention-users)

**Mention Users**

With this selection you can choose whether you to mention the user triggering the keyword or not.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#channel-selection-type)

**Channel Selection - Type**

This section is where you can choose whether to enable all channels except those whitelisted, or the selected channels that can trigger the autoresponder.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#channel-selection-channels)

**Channel Selection - Channels**

Based off [Channel Selection - Type](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#channel-selection-type)
, you can choose channels that will either block or allow the autoresponder to trigger.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#role-selection-type)

**Role Selection - Type**

In this field you can choose whether to enable all roles except those whitelisted, or the selected roles.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#role-selection-roles)

**Role Selection - Roles**

Based off [Role Selection - Type](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#role-selection-type)
, you can choose roles that will either block or allow the autoresponder to trigger.

To save the autoresponder's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another autoresponder.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#active-responders)

Active Responders

These are the active autoresponders that will trigger based off many factors such as roles, channels and keywords. The current maximum is 100 for premium users. Once opened, at the bottom right you can edit / delete the auto responder.

To save the edits you made on the autoresponder's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FybBOKX2UWWtATHMZhYnf%252Fimage_2024-07-09_222401622.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dade866e5-3436-4f9c-8876-1b8950182b66&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c85d932&sv=2)

Potential active responders of the Autoresponder module

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#events)

Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Autoresponder module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module. All Autoresponders will be ordered by the number in which they were created.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9gLmucpJbZQElkiEdWrd%252Fimage_2024-07-09_222634101.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D919c6560-d5b4-48a7-9b3b-b2dde934e2aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=503a6e5f&sv=2)

Potential Custom Events of the Autoresponder module

Autoresponder #...[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/autoresponder#autoresponder)

Once a autoresponder is added, it's corresponding event will be added as an event. These events control how the autoresponder functions based off the settings you chose and send the message to the channel.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Invite Tracker | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FbbtNlk2mNzQ76TL6UtKF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01754363-3705-43f1-b2fc-418c50fd2514&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5a2e39f&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Invite Tracker](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/4cb902a6-dc80-439c-a650-6af2564e8ee6/invitetracker)
 module will enable members of your community to retrieve leaderboards and specific member statistics for individuals they invite.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#settings)

Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#counter-settings)

Counter Settings

In this area is where you can configure specific messages sent when a new member is invited, roles, restrictions and more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjMWi0ky5SqLg77JBgic7%252Fimage_2024-07-22_203035482.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72693db9-d940-4ffa-a024-4237a27b40f2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f90b7ff5&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#update-message-type)

**Update Message Type**

This is where the type of message sent can be configured when a user is invited.

No Message

Direct Message

Message to Channel

No Message will be sent in the server if this option is chosen.

If this option is selected, when a user is invited they will receive this message in their direct messages.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#update-message)

Update Message

Here is where you can configure the message being sent. You can use [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 such as `{invites}` and `{inviter}` to show stats and more. You can also toggle the message type to choose between [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 or a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 response.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fsdc0I8dwrLGmQF07k5Nh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2051d9d-b5e8-40f7-969c-b90b165d3230&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aee22793&sv=2)

If this selection is chosen, a message will be sent to a specific channel when a user is invited into the server.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#updates-channel)

Updates Channel

Here you can choose a text or announcement channel to serve as the channel that receives the invite messages.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FkkdjZRd9XH8EPidRWrKR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc86a5382-5ccf-4f6b-bfee-ffe6256db26a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6430e6aa&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#update-message-1)

Update Message

Here is where you can configure the message being sent. You can use [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 such as `{invites}` and `{inviter}` to show stats and more. You can also toggle the message type to choose between [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 or a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 response.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fsdc0I8dwrLGmQF07k5Nh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df2051d9d-b5e8-40f7-969c-b90b165d3230&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aee22793&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#ignored-roles)

**Ignored Roles**

In this field you can choose certain roles to be excluded from the invite counter. This means that if they invite a user it doesn't count towards their total invites.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#filter-suspicious-invites)

**Filter Suspicious Invites**

If this toggle is enabled, when a user with a relatively low account age is invited, it will not count towards the inviter's total invites.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#minimal-account-age)

**Minimal Account Age**

Configure the account age in days to trigger the [Filter Suspicious Invites](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#filter-suspicious-invites)
 filter. Only integers can be accepted in this field. _This setting is only visible when_ [Filter Suspicious Invites](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#filter-suspicious-invites)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#hide-left-inviters)

**Hide Left Inviters**

If this toggle is enabled, users who left the server will not show up on the leaderboard when `/invite-leaderboard` is used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#register-leaves)

**Register Leaves**

When this toggle is enabled, if a user that got invited by someone in the server leaves, the inviter's total invite count will decrease by one.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#role-rewards)

Role Rewards

Here is how to setup roles to be given to members when they meet a certain amount of people invited. You can have up to 10 rewards.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FYsCWkDqPAWAtjYxDpjo9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd42ff6d-b0a2-4c0e-9ea3-145bd58e2e24&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6bed654b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#required-invite-count)

**Required Invite Count**

This field input is how many people need to be invited by a member for the role in this reward to be given.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#role-reward)

**Role Reward**

The role to be given when the required invite count is met or gone beyond. Only 1 role can be selected per reward.

To save the reward's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another reward.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#active-rewards)

Active Rewards

This area is where you can manage your active role rewards and their settings.

To save the edits you made on the reward's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FoxGMyRTPgf8GRGbnxy71%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc763551c-30ca-4884-893e-dada50a3cb21&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80d92315&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#commands)

Commands


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Invite Tracker module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FBREfzPf0daD1aF43XHt7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42a9d291-3f34-4a20-99ca-e16b2bf7bf04&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=652479ab&sv=2)

/invites[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#invites)

This command allows you to check the number of invites of anyone in the server.

/invites-leaderboard[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#invites-leaderboard)

This command displays the leaderboard of members who invited the most users to your server. You can browse through the leaderboard by using the buttons at the bottom of the leaderboard message.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#events)

Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Invite Tracker module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUwJriTMW5R9IqbeteAje%252Fimage_2024-07-22_205543705.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaf035ad-cb8b-4d4f-8add-c0753211cb47&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f913dbdf&sv=2)

Invites Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#invites-handler)

This event edits the invite count for when a user gets invited to your server.

Leaves Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#leaves-handler)

This event tracks when a user is removed or leaves the server and adjusts the invite count accordingly.

Reward #...[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#reward)

When a active reward is made from [Role Rewards](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/invite-tracker#role-rewards)
, the corresponding event will be created and automatically gives a user a role dependent on the reward settings.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.
