# Channel Condition | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/channel-condition.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FmHzqoSzfJLopmvpwtyeU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf91306d-2d36-4af5-8bd8-fdfc7223a238&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d9dd3cb&sv=2)

This condition will run actions based off the channel that the command / event was triggered in or where a [menu option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/send-a-message-with-a-select-menu/menu-option) / [button](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/send-a-message-with-attached-buttons/buttons)
 was clicked.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/channel-condition#run-multiple-actions)

Run multiple actions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option allows you to set the condition to run multiple actions at the same time. This means if multiple conditions are met, then each true condition will be run simultaneously. When disabled, only the first met condition will be executed.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FgkJsf2QwTvFRQTCrgkB4%252Fimage_2024-06-10_222911587.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f9bcc2e-b7ee-4105-b330-75db316f8e85&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5a65ff3&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/channel-condition#channel)

Channel


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section is a dropdown menu of channels that may be selected for the condition to compare. Click the refresh icon next to the title if the channel you're looking for isn't showing.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FIiuS98uhw8ZRNifTtAhu%252Fimage_2024-06-10_223010960.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd07235a6-826d-4610-ba20-4a08b2598e79&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c99540c3&sv=2)

Click the add condition button to add one or more compared channels to the condition

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvfEmBi39cGBdDFMqLG8P%252Fimage_2024-06-10_223133483.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6942865e-67d2-47e6-bc6a-a1bce1bbdbc1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=827b105c&sv=2)

You may individually click on a compared channel to edit the values and more.

Click the block on the builder to access the following menu.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FrbQd732p4ikjVVHPRLVb%252Fimage_2024-06-10_223350820.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafb43533-1644-4afe-9db4-0e71f5db0777&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4f2850&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/channel-condition#channel-id)

Channel ID


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this section you can edit the compared channel by switching the channel ID. [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 may be used this in field or a plain channel ID.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/conditions/channel-condition#run-when-the-command-is-not-used-in-this-channel)

Run when the command is NOT used in this channel


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option, when enabled, allows you to run the actions below the selected block when the user does not use the command in the specific channel, instead of running when the user does.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXjDAcrgciHtR0zxChxTA%252Fimage_2024-06-10_223740851.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def88cb73-73e2-4267-a7c4-26ec9105ec44&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd926a1d&sv=2)

Here is an example layout of the condition:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F0zhvDuRjZmpZWqTIfJVO%252FScreenshot%25202023-02-13%2520at%25201.52.03%2520PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77ac6a8a-5490-4dbe-90ec-53c565b32889&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc5663ef&sv=2)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Webhooks | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXaHp2YvYuFkDtN1FOHpR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5067e885-79bb-49f9-828e-55c904fdba79&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e1901d2&sv=2)

[BotGhost webhooks](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/webhooks)
 allow you to trigger custom events by sending a POST HTTP request to the internal BotGhost API. This lets you connect external services and pass along data to your BotGhost hosted bot.

A BotGhost webhook is NOT the same as a [Discord webhook](https://support.discord.com/hc/en-us/articles/228383668-Intro-to-Webhooks)
.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#api-key)

API Key


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To secure your webhook, the module requires you to authenticate with an API key. The owner of the bot can view, copy, and regenerate this key at any time on the Webhooks module. Treat this key like a password to your custom event, and only share it with those who should be able to trigger it.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FguFULuaLFqfQORpDSjYQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9aadfec9-0ec0-419f-b0af-ae6c05fa0684&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2ab4130&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#setting-up-webhooks)

Setting Up Webhooks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#creating-a-webhook)

Creating a Webhook

![](https://docs.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9IPyeLmhnwxap8wVYKUJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8032ef2-693d-47ea-9d38-394dcca50975&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=568f459d&sv=2)

To trigger an event from an external source you must first create a new webhook in your BotGhost dashboard. Enter a descriptive name for your webhook and click **Add Webhook Event**. An Event ID will be prepopulated and a new webhook will be created.

![](https://docs.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FSOKA3z0Oa4c2CKvxtxnq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D255cc0ee-a10a-43e4-a745-fcdbf78a2f3f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa5230f&sv=2)

In the example request section of the newly created webhook, you will see the webhook URL and the required headers and body of the request. View the API reference at the bottom of the page for more information about the required information of the POST request.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#creating-a-custom-event)

Creating a Custom Event

Once you have created a webhook, you need to create a custom event to be executed when you submit a POST request to your webhook. This is the same process as creating a normal BotGhost custom event however you must select your webhook as an event type.

Go to the Custom Events module and create a new event. Select your webhook as the event type for your new event.

![](https://docs.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F53zgYGR3pGWpIPgoQbo5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c2f2696-c325-4dcd-b053-1ee26db84647&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dc5272dc&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FquBEg4MKVek1ySjndRvo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf67e3d2-b923-402d-b05b-360bc97e93bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=387b2d23&sv=2)

Once you have created your event, you must also set a server id as a base for the event. This is so it can retrieve information about channels and members when your event is executed.

![](https://docs.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMFwD47NH5hmcPlvmD8ub%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D038240ce-79ed-446d-b166-ef747aa33683&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d522add&sv=2)

After entering a server id, you can configure your custom event like normal. This event will be triggered when its associated webhook receives a valid HTTP POST request.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#sending-your-post-request)

Sending your POST request

Once you have created a webhook and custom event you must send a POST request to the webhook URL.

The webhook URL is always in the format `https://api.botghost.com/webhook/{bot_id}/{event_id}` replacing `{bot_id}` with your bot's id and `{event_id}` with the generated webhook event id.

You must pass along your API token as an Authorization Header to authenticate your `POST` request.

![](https://docs.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FZkSPrF92pXgDsjYIxkkr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad3f324f-824c-43f3-b55d-86dac5a57e35&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77300ae0&sv=2)

You can also optionally pass along an array of variables to act as event variables with your request. The BotGhost Webhook API expects a JSON formatted array of objects with each variable object having:

Key

Info

`name`

A descriptive name for your variable.

`variable`

The actual variable itself. This must start with `{` and end with `}`.

`value`

The value of the variable that will be replaced when it is used in the webhook event.

Pass these variables along in the body of your request. You can then use any of these supplied variables in the custom event being executed by your webhook.

![](https://docs.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FwUyCMaQOszP0qHoAmay0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbcb0de05-c581-48bd-93e5-084528ce49b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90bb5c4f&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#api-reference)

API Reference


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Submit a `POST` request to the following endpoint. On success, if a custom event with that webhook event id exists that event will be triggered.

Replace `{bot_id}` and `{event_id}` in the URL with your bots id and a webhook event id.

`POST` `https://api.botghost.com/webhook/{bot_id}/{event_id}`

Send a POST request to trigger a custom event on a bot. Replace `{bot_id}` and `{event_id}` with your bot id and an event id. Event ids are generated after creating a webhook in the webhook module.

**Headers**

Name

Type

Description

Authorization\*

API\_KEY

Auhthorization header with your API\_KEY from the webhooks module page.

**Request Body**

Name

Type

Description

variables

Array

An array of optional variables to pass along to the webhook. Each variable object should have a name, variable, and value.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#response)

Response

When you send your `POST` request to your BotGhost webhook, you may receive different status codes. These codes let you know whether the webhook event was successfully triggered, or if an error occurred. Below you can find detailed information about each status code, what it means, and what to do from there.

200: OK

400: Bad Request

401: Unauthorized

404: Not Found

405: Method Not Allowed

429: Too Many Requests

Success! This status is returned when the webhook event has successfully been triggered. If you didn't get the result you expected, double-check your event's logic and try again.

Error. This status is returned when the request hasn't been formatted properly.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#what-went-wrong)

What Went Wrong

The most common occurrences of this error happen when:

*   The variables parameter was not formatted as an array
    
*   The variables parameter was missing the `name`, `variable`, or `value` key(s)
    
*   The variables parameter had an improperly formatted `variable` key
    

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#how-to-fix)

How to Fix

Head back to the variables settings under [Sending your POST request](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#sending-your-post-request)
 and try setting up again.

Error. This status is returned when the provided API key is invalid.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#what-went-wrong-1)

What Went Wrong

The most common occurrences of this error happen when:

*   The API key was not provided
    
*   The API key has been provided incorrectly
    
*   The API key has been regenerated
    
*   The bot has been removed from BotGhost
    

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#how-to-fix-1)

How to Fix

Head back to the [API Key](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#api-key)
 settings and try setting up again.

Error. This status is returned when the provided URL is invalid.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#what-went-wrong-2)

What Went Wrong

The most common occurrences of this error happen when:

*   The webhook URL has been provided incorrectly
    
*   The webhook event has been deleted
    
*   The bot has been removed from BotGhost
    

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#how-to-fix-2)

How to Fix

Head back to the webhook URL settings under [Sending your POST request](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#sending-your-post-request)
 and try setting up again.

Error. This status is returned when you have sent an API request to your webhook that is not a `POST` request. To fix it, set your request type to `POST` and try again.

Error. This status is returned when you have sent too many requests to this URL in a too short amount of time. To fix it, wait a while before trying again.

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Creating a Webhook](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/webhooks#creating-a-webhook)

# Choice Option | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/choice-option.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJQ1xkB7heN8B6p8AU5lv%252FBildschirm%25C2%25ADfoto%25202023-02-17%2520um%252005.23.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da265fdf8-deb3-4588-8b1e-20add4291d1c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=567c7c5b&sv=2)

This option block is a choice between `True` or `False` that can be used in later actions / conditions of the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FSVDaanfvzoGywnRxUmaL%252FBildschirm%25C2%25ADfoto%25202023-02-17%2520um%252005.24.36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D487ecc2a-d862-42c3-a02b-fee326952173&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=348acfb9&sv=2)

You can retrieve the variable of the option via the **Clipboard** or the block itself. The format of the variable is `{option_optionname}`, where `optionname` is the [name](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/choice-option#option-name)
 of the option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F7l53Sjd6fgU8sGvJLYBy%252Fimage_2024-06-08_124418534.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfcc434ee-5711-442d-a092-00502a3c6905&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6b67a02&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/choice-option#option-name)

Option Name


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This field requires an input for your unique option name. The designated name will then be the reference for your option variable.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F5Xsz9M6Zbq78M181Nbqo%252Fimage_2024-06-07_183434741.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6e30549-8f2f-448b-a843-ec8c700abbe7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77270026&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/choice-option#option-description)

Option Description


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The option description field allows you to assign a custom description to your option. It is useful to describe what the option is used for.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FBLA0U2rli29wlyMnQslm%252Fimage_2024-06-07_183520597.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31fcbdc6-5d1f-4f56-9006-62f530139aff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a0f550c4&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/choice-option#set-required)

Set Required


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this switch you are able to toggle if the option should be required or not in order to execute the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FZdasaits2xqKe9Prpu8h%252Fimage_2024-06-07_182514963.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c293fc9-954e-4a5d-9496-5fbb04ae304a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0b59302&sv=2)

# Options | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options.md)
.

Options are purple in color and are used for users to input values into the command, which can then be referenced anywhere within the command with the variable {option\_optionname}. Options function when a command is about to be executed, which creates fields to be able to input values into. Additionally, options are automatically connected to the command when added. They are also only available in commands and aren't required to be in the command.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options#option-blocks)

Option Blocks


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Block

Information

[Text Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/text-option)

The text option block allows for a text value to be input.

[Number Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/number-option)

This block allows a number value to be input.

[User Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/user-option)

This option allows you to select a user from a list of server members.

[Channel Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/channel-option)

This option allows you to select a channel from a list of server channels.

[Role Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/role-option)

This option allows you to select a role from your server.

[Choice Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/choice-option)

With this option you are able to select true or false from a dropdown.

[Attachment Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/attachment-option)

The attachment option allows you to upload an attachment to the command.

[Music Smart Search Option](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option)

The music smart search option can be used to let users search for music tracks when using a command.

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

# Image Generation | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMivVpG4eUIt34074YbGl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86ca2c97-2dfb-4fe5-8cfb-b382a0e6ede6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d7c7046&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

The [Image Generation](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/fab3a781-88c6-4bd6-9db0-6c2f68b36931/imagegeneration)
 module allows users to trigger a command to send a request to the Dall-E API to generate a imaged based off of the prompts the user inputs while using the command.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#credentials-setup)

Credentials Setup


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

Click [here](https://platform.openai.com/account/api-keys)
 to get started. Log into OpenAI. If you haven't already, Open AI might ask you to verify your phone number before proceeding.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fq9GPD8gYEEKSUJUdOUT0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21258ead-278d-4369-9e6e-8c74720216e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4db4d6a7&sv=2)

2

Once you logged in, click on the "Create new secret key button.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FS7gwMVMFJzgROIn9FgNg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c28f2f7-66d6-4ffc-a30c-fca4aa336669&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a7c3f78&sv=2)

3

This will prompt you to make a key. Set Owned by "You" and give your app a name. Set the "Permissions" to all. Once done, click on "Create Secret Key"

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8jDcjid6nM0pn1C4FEQY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def74a1c9-be35-4a97-8993-e0f087a4c170&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=372fc88c&sv=2)

4

Copy your key. Make sure to not share it with anyone.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Ft5wYLfCDF4amFI8F4pjO%252FUntitled%2520design.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92f2b404-4afc-45c8-93ba-6316f89c861f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60a63e3b&sv=2)

5

Paste your key into the BotGhost Dashboard in the [OpenAI API Key](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#openai-api-key)
 field.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#settings)

Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area you can configure the main settings for the image generation module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FohNwUVd8hueO1Aff1HzJ%252Fimage_2024-07-10_214158577.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6fbc6fcb-8e1c-4352-a7b3-73f9e0c541b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93dd7461&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#openai-api-key)

**OpenAI API Key**

In this field is where you will need to enter your OpenAI API key to be able to use the module, you can follow this guide [here](https://platform.openai.com/docs/api-reference/authentication)
, to generate your own API key.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#generate-multiple-variations)

**Generate Multiple Variations**

With this toggle you can enable / disable the option for the bot to generate multiple variations of the image, this will allow you to see multiple versions with one trigger.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#default-image-size)

Default Image Size

You can choose the image size from one of the following options:

*   1024x1024 Pixels
    
*   512x512 Pixels
    
*   256x256 Pixels
    

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#commands)

Commands


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Image Generation module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FP9pir62xIQyw2lHYbHSt%252Fimage_2024-07-10_214943606.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb28d0a2-2f1d-45d3-bcd0-57a6cccc883c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=51632cd9&sv=2)

/imagine[](https://documentation.botghost.com/ai/image-generation#imagine)

Upon being triggered this command generates the image(s) based upon the prompts you submit, here you can edit the command to add additional features or expand on the base module.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

# Embed Builder | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjWceEKQde1WxxAOhPRSm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6b02938-5585-498b-8d7f-631bc57d8765&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=100e22b9&sv=2)

The Embed Builder makes it very simple and easy to send multiple embeds to server with no effort! Using the Embed Builder you can send, edit, and maximize customizability!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#general-settings)

General Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#embed-selector)

Embed Selector

The Embed Selector lets you choose from all previous / running embeds that have been sent to all servers! Just select which embed you want to edit from the dropdown and get editing right away, taking away the hassle of having to find the message and copy the ID to edit it. Only embeds you've saved using the 'Save Embeds' button will appear here!

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FoUdLAWkUOfyHYj4EAC0o%252Fbg_embed-selector_noembeds.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9eefd8a5-9e7a-4aec-bdba-942804ed17f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e692b704&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FftEN7qd9iWoJ0NNAzSU7%252Fbg_embed-selector_embedlist.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33669b77-5203-43b7-937a-65d50fba13ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffe536ff&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#message-link)

Message Link

The Message Link feature lets you edit embeds without having to re-send the embed, this means all reactions and content underneath it will remain where they are and the message itself with just show as edited. You can only edit messages that are saved in your embed selector, if they aren't there then you wont be able to edit that message.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJ948bqBVDymA7reDvGzo%252Fbg_message-link_linkpreviewe.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5302e9e-169b-460b-8fba-ec97d9fd6988&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d093431&sv=2)

If your link contains discordapp.com, remove the 'app'

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOrysQ4xIRdJ2MzCQqkdU%252Fbg_message-link_editedmessage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0b813b4-33d4-4566-a70c-02bd87a27938&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2f2753a&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#channel)

Channel

The channel option is the place that your embed is going to be sent to, simply select the channel you want your embed to be sent to and it'll be sent there.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FJFLyHf1gy2Iz4gucsBOJ%252Fbg_channel.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9b49e835-accc-4d65-a011-3cca2cda5f28&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=96d3c167&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#embed-content)

Embed Content

The Embed Content is the non-embedded - plain - text above your embed. This text will appear as a normal message but will remain connected to your embed, meaning they're apart of the same message. If you want to ping channels, roles, or members above your embed and have them get the notification, you can use <#CHANNEL-ID> for channels, <@&ROLE-ID> for roles, and <@!USER-ID> for members of your server. _How to get a Channel, Role or User ID? Click_ [_here_](https://btghst.info/copyID)
_!_

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FTZchapQNIqMRaI19B03T%252Fbg_embedcontent.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0cdbab41-615b-4c7c-a0e5-9936f0ba5862&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c46dc115&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#author-settings)

Author Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#name)

Name

The name of your author, this will appear at the top of your embed, even above your title.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhrH94MPkNOYpsQN9EEcF%252Fbg_authorname.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33d3fc3a-aaf8-44e8-ad6c-418bc19fed60&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81ae1297&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#url)

URL

The URL that people will be redirected to after clicking the authors name!

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fys3KKQYAagLoLoM1B65o%252Fbg_authorurlex.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3dbcf60-5485-4374-a48e-b60901cb052f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4fe47a7f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#image-url)

Image URL

The Image URL is the image that will appear next to the authors name. Perfect for adding extra decoration and detail to your embed!

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9ZhXzZablGf5vmtOotMI%252Fbg_authorimageurl.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D127eb2f0-14f6-4879-b033-0c73f5d57fc9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5426ed1a&sv=2)

_\*For images the links (URLs) should end with .jpg .jpeg .png or .gif_

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#body-settings)

Body Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#title)

Title

The title of your body, this will represent all of your body's content and will stick out much more than other text, being bold and bigger.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FDT8N2VVITJ6kPkrtrTxk%252Fbg_bodytitle.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D730f6f99-3c8b-46d8-a59d-c4978de5b224&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=68fe32a0&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#description)

Description

The description of your body can contain much more information compared to the title but comes in more of a smaller size. Better for containing more information than any other option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2bbwl1vxbjaF4QxJr1al%252Fbg_bodydescription.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da38ed06e-76de-47c2-8d85-d97c9cadc14a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c30642f6&sv=2)

The Body's Description can contain up to 4096 characters!

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#url-1)

URL

The URL of the body is the place where the person will be redirected to when they click the title of the body.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9crr1PRqtkPEPYJlbmDa%252Fbg_bodyurl.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bac509b-55f9-4c9b-ab08-692ad877cc8b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e66cb2a5&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#fields)

Fields


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#field-name)

Field Name

The field name is the 'title' of the field, except it doesn't act like all other titles. Your field names won't appear bigger than the field content in any way other than being bold, it'll just be above the content.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9dF3azBp8A10qzhj0rUW%252Fbg_fieldname.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De28e2ce6-4dca-425f-acb8-3c4df44f7112&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ba3af813&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#field-content)

Field Content

Your field content is all of the writing you want to appear below the field name, used to organize your fields with information underneath the field name.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FBjYC2Z2Lt9svzDx60Ezr%252Fbg_fieldcontent.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a4bdc66-a18c-42d4-982c-4acd48d87b5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f33c8d1d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#inline-field)

**Inline Field**

The Inline Field option will make fields arranged in a line form from left to right. You must have at least two fields with both Inline's toggled on for them to appear in a line. You can't have more than three fields Inlined with each other.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F92gegJLExnhuv6GexZuo%252Fbg_fieldinline.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da04c80a2-a015-4f8c-8b6e-006655c2bbe5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d66161a&sv=2)

Inlines only show up on desktop!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#images)

Images


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#image-url-1)

Image URL

The Image URL is the image that will appear at the bottom of the embed. This will show as a bigger image compared to the Thumbnail URL!

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8snU4ahBmdO3GpMbetEM%252Fbg_imageurl.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a7b3a8f-196b-4cb5-a8dc-c10b90ff612c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8ab7daf&sv=2)

_\*For images the links (URLs) should end with .jpg .jpeg .png or .gif_

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#thumbnail-url)

Thumbnail URL

The Thumbnail URL is a image that will appear in the top right of the embed, this image will be in a smaller form than the Image URL but can appear bigger if the image has the right dimensions.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2zB8Pb8vsWUo4JdzEGRC%252Fbg_thumbnailurl.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D652a0ae2-04d6-49dc-a68b-a6b3bc485d22&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17a167a3&sv=2)

_\*For images the links (URLs) should end with .jpg .jpeg .png or .gif_

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#text)

Text

The content of your footer, this will display at the bottom of your embed with very tiny, yet, noticeable text.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FB4YNOOPqOIbeBtWVpWQa%252Fbg_footer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9482ad1-e859-4d19-bc80-899eb3eb1ebf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44bff3ea&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/messages/embedbuilder#image-url-2)

Image URL

An image appearing to the left of your footer, similar to the author image but appears at the bottom near the footer.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FfOCQwDSTX7IVDbXOmqgb%252Fbg_footerimg.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52f404f1-1f5c-400b-ac38-64516be7edf5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a0f2ae5f&sv=2)

_\*For images the links (URLs) should end with .jpg .jpeg .png or .gif_

Experiencing issues with the embed builder module or do you just need help? Checkout our support options [**here**](https://documentation.botghost.com/support/botghost-support)
**!**

# Channel Option | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/channel-option.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FC1rOFMDsts0bOcFi0HlD%252FBildschirm%25C2%25ADfoto%25202023-02-17%2520um%252005.11.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94c6c2cf-f7d7-4e44-95c7-0532554c3b99&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55d39da3&sv=2)

The channel option block allows for any channel to be selected from the server and used later in the commands actions. Channel IDs may also be used.

Only the channels to which the user has access can be selected.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FuJDosAF1anl1TEjsdzkC%252Fimage_2024-06-07_182707065.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a8786d1-e222-45a9-8c3e-8d699ed87ed8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21380ce4&sv=2)

You can retrieve the variable of the option via the **Clipboard** or the block itself. The format of the variable is `{option_optionname}`, where `optionname` is the [name](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/channel-option#option-name)
 of the option.

Additionally, channel option variables can be combined with other variables to target the channel selected in the option. `{}` brackets must be excluded from the option when used as a target, like in the example below:

❌ Wrong

☑️ Correct

`{channel_name[{option_channel}]}`

`{channel_name[option_channel]}`

`{BGVAR_status[{option_channel}]}`

`{BGVAR_status[option_channel]}`

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FBMurDZ83qS9cQFG9aPYe%252Fimage_2024-06-08_124226997.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81cedb03-d5b3-44dd-9a16-516f13a55493&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48699c1a&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/channel-option#option-name)

Option Name


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This field requires an input for your unique option name. The designated name will then be the reference for your option variable.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FS6wg4mRllZDMAUpGXVUq%252Fimage_2024-06-07_182337413.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D779b567a-efdb-46b4-a741-7bdf066409e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=719880c8&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/channel-option#option-description)

Option Description


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The option description field allows you to assign a custom description to your option. It is useful to describe what the option is used for.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FOEMYz42Odl90gX96iLpc%252Fimage_2024-06-07_182500325.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa137d0e-e8f6-4f7a-881a-493eda720693&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53702f3e&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/channel-option#set-required)

Set Required


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this switch you are able to toggle if the option should be required or not in order to execute the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FZdasaits2xqKe9Prpu8h%252Fimage_2024-06-07_182514963.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c293fc9-954e-4a5d-9496-5fbb04ae304a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0b59302&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fk23vtJSDb2r494fZKlYo%252FBildschirm%25C2%25ADfoto%25202023-02-17%2520um%252005.29.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd7dcd62b-6349-4892-8670-2a3699ba31c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3630877e&sv=2)

 of the option.

 of the option.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F18FlPPhO8MoeP8LQCOYk%252Fimage_2024-06-08_124323925.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8957f65d-2346-4c90-88e5-feee695d52c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17f9c938&sv=2)

# User Option | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/user-option.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvTwyYYn7aU3W7Fq7xq7g%252Fimage_2024-06-07_184134753.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D753f22a2-86d7-40fa-bb4c-d842af558528&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d40b57c&sv=2)

The user option block allows for any user to be selected from the server and used later in the commands actions. User IDs may also be used.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F3KO5VcIieRrSMmHCLJXc%252Fimage_2024-06-07_181816651.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94c9074d-ba6a-4f09-850c-61d5a6064d4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e88cbfb&sv=2)

You can retrieve the variable of the option via the **Clipboard** or the block itself. The format of the variable is `{option_optionname}`, where `optionname` is the [name](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/user-option#option-name)
 of the option.

Additionally, user option variables can be combined with other variables to target the user selected in the option. `{}` brackets must be excluded from the option when used as a target, like in the example below:

❌ Wrong

☑️ Correct

`{user_name[{option_user}]}`

`{user_name[option_user]}`

`{BGVAR_money[{option_user}]}`

`{BGVAR_money[option_user]}`

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fm3ugQGknMQb0fQnt0Yea%252Fimage_2024-06-08_124138860.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D074a7375-02e5-44e5-b3b4-91af5ffbef7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2dfb993f&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/user-option#option-name)

Option Name


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This field requires an input for your unique option name. The designated name will then be the reference for your option variable.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FepV9xmmJooC5PYrDwyyY%252Fimage_2024-06-07_181906364.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D737b237a-bbcb-4b9f-945d-a707484541c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5065b43c&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/user-option#option-description)

Option Description


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The option description field allows you to assign a custom description to your option. It is useful to describe what the option is used for.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FskxkjohGIbNV7dgMjVk5%252Fimage_2024-06-07_181923947.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df548faec-e349-4c0b-a4e5-b8ef67fdeedf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=139b04a&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/user-option#set-required)

Set Required


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this switch you are able to toggle if the option should be required or not in order to execute the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FrObC5usM1A0DZ35MHPx8%252Fimage_2024-06-07_182022364.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfde69d8c-e568-42be-9d63-1dbdceff1611&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d7b4cc3&sv=2)

Last updated 2 years ago

# Translation | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F4dH0Z7aS6U8JAr2qNwBr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4986c8a3-21fe-474e-9d0c-be0b773c5159&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da195813&sv=2)

This module is only available to users with a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
.

The [Translation](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/6fef2574-418b-47cd-adef-22c9c3e88051/translation)
 module allows you to translate texts via a Custom Command, quick-translations by reacting with a specified emoji, daily translation limits, and more!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#credentials)

Credentials


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Translation module requires you to add your own DeepL API key in order to handle translations, allowing you to select the account tier and the daily translations limit.

To create an API key, follow the steps below.

1

Create an account or log in the official [DeepL website](https://www.deepl.com/pro#developer)
.

2

Select the tier you wish to use for your translations, whether it is the Free Tier or Paid Tiers. If you wish to have the free tier, please select 'Sign up for free'.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FGSXZCSOb2a5WF1NmcNks%252F2.%2520DeepL%2520Tiers%2520for%2520the%2520Translation%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a732973-a0ca-457c-a02f-1ec6b3da61f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9ab10c39&sv=2)

DeepL Tiers for the Translation module

3

Fulfill the following details. This is used to avoid potential misuses of their free API. DeepL will not charge you unless you manually upgrade your current subscription to a paid one.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FgmRCiSBQOKOYjanpgHiN%252F3.%2520DeepL%2520Details%2520for%2520the%2520Translation%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28ac782e-bdf4-40c3-b855-f865c6b84b7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=729ff8aa&sv=2)

DeepL Details for the Translation module

4

Once you have successfully fulfilled all the details, accept [DeepL's Terms & Conditions](https://www.deepl.com/en/pro-license_embedded)
 and press 'Sign up for free'.

5

A similar page will appear upon signing up for free, click on 'Account management' to go to your account settings. If this page does not appear, please go to your [account settings](https://www.deepl.com/your-account/plan)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FK7UvxrSMo3paNxFY2a1C%252F4.%2520DeepL%2520Account%2520Management%2520for%2520the%2520Translation%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd975bc2-593e-4938-9433-e4aa97aa05a4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a97d26&sv=2)

DeepL Account Management for the Translation module

6

Get the Authentication Key for DeepL in your [account summary](https://www.deepl.com/your-account/summary)
 settings located in the bottom right corner.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FfdBnQBDixHujHrpcXwHc%252F5.%2520Authentication%2520Key%2520for%2520DeepL%2520API%2520for%2520the%2520Translation%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6727d967-6eda-4f78-b841-79a006a5019c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13b1dd6f&sv=2)

Authentication Key for DeepL API for the Translation module

7

Once copied, paste it in the 'DeepL API Key' field in BotGhost.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#settings)

Settings


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#credentials-1)

Credentials

This section is where you input the API Key found from [Credentials](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#credentials)
 and also change other account settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUHte3YdwLhZBplf1AaZJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17d25b05-944a-4e35-9111-0409d115ebdb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0247cbf&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#deepl-api-key)

**DeepL API Key**

Paste your DeepL API Key here. Learn how to get one in the [Credentials](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#credentials)
section. Make sure to not share it with anyone!

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#deepl-account-tier)

**DeepL Account Tier**

Set the account tier you selected when getting your API key. Remember to select the correct one as DeepL handles different API domains for free and paid tiers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#daily-translation-limit)

**Daily Translation Limit**

Define the maximum amount of translations that can be executed per day. Setting this to 0 will disable this limit.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#quick-translation)

Quick-Translation

The following parameters allow you to react with a specific emoji to automatically translate the content of the message, select the channels for quick translations, the required roles, the target language, and toggle if you wish to delete the original message upon successful translation.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FQXzNup6uVKdYuVkxmd4r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd10673af-bf20-41b1-91ff-f9f47c00d67b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a4c42d1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#trigger-reactions)

**Trigger Reactions**

Select up to 10 different emojis to trigger the quick-translations.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#quick-translation-channels)

**Quick-Translation Channels**

Choose the channels you wish to allow for quick-translation. If none is chosen, this feature will be available across all channels.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#required-roles)

**Required Roles**

Select the roles that will require users with these roles to be the ones to use the quick translation.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#target-language)

**Target Language**

Define which language should the messages be translated to when triggering the quick-translations.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#delete-original-message)

**Delete Original Message**

Enable or disable to delete the original message after a successful quick-translation.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#translate-command)

Translate Command

Define the allowed roles and the default DeepL language when using the /translate custom command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FCYH9Gam9f8Yty085bBtV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1ca540b-973b-492f-a877-1835986397cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eccbfdaf&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#allowed-roles)

**Allowed Roles**

Select the roles that users must have to run the `/translation` custom command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#default-language-deepl)

**Default Language (DeepL)**

Choose the language to translate messages to when using the custom command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#translation-command-reply)

Translation Command Reply

Customize the reply in the /translate custom command. You can use `{original_message}` and `{translated_message}` to return the content of the original message and the translated content, respectively. All [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used. You can also toggle the [embed](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/embed-reply)
 to a [plain text](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/legacy-reply-actions/plain-text-reply)
 response using the switch in the top right.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#character-limit)

**Character Limit**

Define the maximum amount of characters the command should allow to translate.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#command)

Command


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Find the command for the Translation module and modify them. This will allow you to fine-tune the command's logic to your liking.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjzpAjGTbAsqoAQTxAK93%252F9.%2520Custom%2520Command%2520for%2520the%2520Translation%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D829ae27f-7002-4df3-925d-0881bac561a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc4a12dd&sv=2)

Custom Command for the Translation module

/translate[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#translate)

Translate the given text to the target language.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#events)

Events


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the events within the Translation module and customize them to your preferences. This allows you to change the events' logic according to your liking and needs.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FHUe5Oi4bzPxTAR0UlIyk%252F10.%2520Events%2520for%2520the%2520Translation%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba5f002c-9d2e-4958-b705-c2b7b0a549d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd0f363c&sv=2)

Custom Events for the Translation module

Quick-Translation[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#quick-translation-1)

This event handles the quick-translations, triggered with each reaction added to a message.

Daily Limit Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/utility/translation#daily-limit-handler)

The timed event triggered daily to handle the daily limits.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Music Smart Search Option | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FqglyZZ1TbBLmAe7iu9yq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59a0a07e-c789-408f-b522-1185d28322c8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d935197&sv=2)

This option can be used to let users search for music tracks when using a command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjodlsS6oDMrCyVlOtEaz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7295256-61f8-47e3-9f65-f485a0188482&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af0f715f&sv=2)

There are multiple variables you can use from this option. The format of the variable is `{option_optionname}`, where `optionname` is the [name](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option#option-name)
 of the option.

Variable

Information

`{option_optionname.result}`

This variable should be used in the [Music Queue Add](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/music-actions/add-to-queue)
 and [Music Search](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/music-actions/search-tracks)
 actions. If the user selected an option from the list, this will return the unique ID of the track.

`{option_optionname.title}`

This variable can be used for messages to a user. It returns the song's title.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option#option-name)

Option Name


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This field requires an input for your unique option name. The designated name will then be the reference for your option variable.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FgpwfEiu7d0zjtj5hoLPS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9cee7e0-6b8a-4caf-a6b5-7c11bacc08a6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edfbef66&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option#option-description)

Option Description


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The option description field allows you to assign a custom description to your option. It is useful to describe what the option is used for.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fne27L0Xe7BZkaHHo6bvC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bc3dd12-f3c6-4bc1-9493-211656920d31&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70758aa8&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option#set-required)

Set Required


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this switch you are able to toggle if the option should be required or not in order to execute the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8ZGjl7ltB5dMKqO6Xbja%252Fimage_2024-06-07_153303596.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De487b34e-973a-4c52-93db-c2ebebfb6669&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60842cc5&sv=2)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Option Description](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option#option-description)
    
*   [Set Required](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/options/music-smart-search-option#set-required)
