# Economy & Minigames | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F70zmIOlTpTwHIywdw8cw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4de844d8-b1e2-408b-b05c-4947bb002513&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb967114&sv=2)

Some of the features of this module require a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function. You can however use the module with a free subscription.

The [Economy module](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/5bda821f-56fe-4318-be20-1d2815a04dc3/economy&minigames)
 will allow you to play minigames and set up a custom currency system, daily bonuses, message awards, and economy roles.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#common-issues)

Common Issues


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Experiencing issues with the module? Check out the common issues below. If your issue is not listed in this page, make sure your module is updated to the latest version. If you are still experiencing issues with the module, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#minigame-commands-not-working)

Minigame Commands Not Working

If you're not able to play certain minigames such as `/5dice` or `/blackjack`, please try to solve the issue with the steps below:

1

You will need to upload all emojis of the module in your server. If you don't have enough emoji slots in your server to do that, you can upload them in another server you own and invite your bot to it.

2

Run the `/ec admin` command in the server you want emojis to be uploaded in. This command allows you to get access all economy's admin tools.

3

Pick the "Minigame Configuration" option in the menu. Select the minigame you want to upload the emojis of (5dice or blackjack).

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FHb8pbDWTD9TCrvVZdhXs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08a64866-009d-4c0a-8007-6d89703bd8c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ecf348d&sv=2)

4

Confirm and wait a few seconds

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FINQX5bzI9bdnoNl3nmBa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd95fd29d-ec1a-40b0-a7ea-6ca593801e79&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12108826&sv=2)

5

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help, we'll do our best to solve your issue!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#settings)

Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-settings)

Economy Settings

Customize the currency name, prefix, or emoji for the currency, daily bonus, bank interest rates, colors and a lot more.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhnFkfgoMSs3BjPwhfS4I%252Fimage_2024-07-27_173548368.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23d595eb-f0ec-4e87-bc6e-a9b63dc85c17&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f744ab97&sv=2)

Economy settings of the Economy & Minigames module

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#currency-name)

**Currency Name**

In this field you can define your currency name for the whole economy system.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#currency-prefix-or-emoji)

**Currency Prefix or Emoji**

In this field you can specify a prefix or emoji for your currency to be referenced next to. Learn how to add a custom emoji [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/getting-started/standard-practices/advanced-practices#how-can-i-get-a-custom-emojis-id)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#daily-bonus)

**Daily Bonus**

Here you can set a daily bonus which can be claimed via the `/daily-bonus` command. This field only accepts integers.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#bank-interest)

**Bank Interest**

In this field you can input an interest amount that is earned when you deposit money into the bank via the `/bank-deposit` command. This is limited to a maximum of 5% a day.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#earn-currency-for-messages)

**Earn Currency for Messages**

If this toggle is enabled, users will earn currency for every message sent.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#message-award-cooldown)

**Message Award Cooldown**

This field will allow you to set a cooldown in minutes between each message before giving currency. _This setting only shows when_ [Earn Currency for Messages](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#earn-currency-for-messages)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#message-award-amount)

**Message Award Amount**

**If** [Earn Currency for Messages](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#earn-currency-for-messages)
 is enabled, this field will allow you to customize the amount of currency to give per message to the user. _This setting only shows when_ [Earn Currency for Messages](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#earn-currency-for-messages)
 _is enabled._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#lottery-channel)

Lottery Channel

With this setting you can select a channel to serve as the place where the lottery notification of the winner is sent. This setting refers to the `/lottery` command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#success-color)

Success Color

This setting changes the color for embeds that are sent with the context of being positive or a winner such as the lottery notification.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#main-color)

Main Color

This setting controls the color for informative embeds.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#alert-color)

Alert Color

This setting controls the color for alert / warning type embeds.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#enable-job-editing)

Enable Job Editing

If this toggle is enabled, a new section will appear that allows you to customize and better integrate jobs in your economy system.

Economy Jobs

If the [Enable Job Editing](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#enable-job-editing)
 toggle is enabled, this section will appear and allow you to add and also customize added / available jobs. This correlates to the `/job-apply` and `/job-list` command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMcE1wlS1LfEPuN0vJ6at%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47932077-d327-4226-aebe-f9c34bfdf7be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62e6efd4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#job-title)

Job Title

In this field you can input the name of the job you wish to add.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#job-description)

Job Description

In this field you can input a description for the job you wish to add.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#job-salary)

Job Salary

In this field you can input the amount of currency earned for users with this job.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#shifts-required)

Shifts Required

In this field you may set a specific amount of shifts in order to receive this job.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#custom-value)

Custom Value

This field serves as an "Extra info" field where you can input any additional info or values needed.

To save the job's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another job.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#jobs-title)

Jobs Title

Here is where all active and available jobs are listed and can be edited or deleted. There is a bunch of prebuilt jobs that come with the module and can be changed, as well as there being a maximum of 30 jobs.

To save the edits you made on the job's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FN3FSeAMkTPYIYc0iNwFB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69b46d9a-008e-4d30-b17d-0b508c6fd0f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=764479af&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-items)

Economy Items

In this section you can create and edit Items that users can buy with the `/shop-buy` command and see with the `/inventory` command. Click the "New Item" box to create a new item with the settings below.

Only [Premium](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 users can add one or more items. Free users who delete one or more items have to reset the module to get them back.

Once created you can click on an existing item to delete or edit it.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FSEvBgJyyWqCNNNS34CEQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfecdabad-1fa1-4ff3-91de-84d9a9bae387&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd2b3c16&sv=2)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUe2c7jEexgfzBzlAF2hR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05014c43-fcc1-4ca5-9d53-c7f158ab30ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4a81700&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#name)

Name

In this field you can input the name of the item you are creating.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#description)

Description

In this field you can input the description for the item.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#price)

Price

Here you can give the item a price that it can be bought at.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#item-limit)

Item Limit

This field sets the maximum amount of this item that users can buy from the shop via the `/shop-buy` command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#image)

Image

Select an Image for the item.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#type)

Type

This dropdown changes the type of item it will be.

Role Item

Usable Item

Static Item

If this option is selected, it will make the item be based off a role, so when used it grants the user a role.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#roles)

Roles

In this field you can select role(s) that the user will receive upon using the item.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#destroy-on-use)

Destroy On Use

If this toggle is enabled, the item will be removed from the users inventory if used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#allow-multiples)

Allow Multiples

If this toggle is enabled, users can hold more than one of this item in their inventory.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#use-on-buy)

Use On Buy

If this toggle is enabled, when a user purchases this item, it will be automatically used when purchased.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#unlisted)

Unlisted

If this toggle is enabled, this specific item will not show up when users browse the shop.

If this option is chosen then the item is treated as a regular usable item that does something.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#destroy-on-use-1)

Destroy On Use

If this toggle is enabled, the item will be removed from the users inventory if used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#allow-multiples-1)

Allow Multiples

If this toggle is enabled, users can hold more than one of this item in their inventory.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#use-on-buy-1)

Use On Buy

If this toggle is enabled, when a user purchases this item, it will be automatically used when purchased.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#unlisted-1)

Unlisted

If this toggle is enabled, this specific item will not show up when users browse the shop.

If this option is chosen then the item won't do anything on it's own and needs another item to have a purpose.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#destroy-on-use-2)

Destroy On Use

If this toggle is enabled, the item will be removed from the users inventory if used.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#allow-multiples-2)

Allow Multiples

If this toggle is enabled, users can hold more than one of this item in their inventory.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#unlisted-2)

Unlisted

If this toggle is enabled, this specific item will not show up when users browse the shop.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-roles)

Economy Roles

In this section you can configure and add the role that can be received if a user reaches a certain currency balance threshold.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FMGx128QRq5AsDWzjG3l8%252F3.%2520Economy%2520Roles%2520settings%2520of%2520the%2520Economy%2520Rework%2520module.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd05756f4-f476-4327-bdc7-84aaa779ceb2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1af7e362&sv=2)

Economy Roles settings of the Economy & Minigames module

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-role-amount)

**Economy Role Amount**

In this field you can specify the amount of currency needed for the user to receive the role from [Economy Roles](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-roles-1)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-roles-1)

Economy Roles

Select the role that users should earn when they reach the specified criteria above.

To add the role, click on 'Add' in the right bottom corner to save your new economy role. Existing ones will appear in the 'Active Economy Roles' field below.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#active-economy-roles)

Active Economy Roles

In this area you can edit or delete the active economy roles. There is a maximum of 10 active roles.

Click on an active economy role to edit or delete it.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FnXV4Yrg8V1rDxhR5a5YZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79f3da59-eb8e-4da8-9c48-2c66c075f249&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=332ad796&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#commands)

Commands


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Economy & Minigames module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FmKutnkwiAUygrCi5xO4P%252Fimage_2024-07-27_192007487.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4aed73aa-ee59-4b34-a1cc-b3aa28f1df6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=213fd17a&sv=2)

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#admin-commands)

Admin Commands

/ec admin[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#ec-admin)

Allows you to manage the server economy, like resetting a user's balance, managing command cooldowns, or the entire server economy.

/money remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#money-remove)

This command is for economy admins only and removes currency from a users existing balance.

/money add[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#money-add)

This command is for economy admins only and adds currency to a users existing balance.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-commands)

Economy Commands

/money give[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#money-give)

This command gives a user some of your currency.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FzIZfbt1ojqSCycaHjtTE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5dc7e9c4-8275-4326-9b8e-622f6f06ffb7&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cbb0b23&sv=2)

/balance[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#balance)

This command allows you to check a users currency balance.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fbpbr8WUEO0SHYEf21djv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1496b0f9-cd54-4476-9d9c-d358d490b49a&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=144c345d&sv=2)

/daily[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#daily)

This command allows you to claim your daily bonus. [Daily Bonus](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#daily-bonus)

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F01hcT0rf6sXTbgNnK4r7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f8f820d-a8e6-47ff-afe6-ca836a3949f9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1559f30f&sv=2)

/ec leaderboard[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#ec-leaderboard)

This command displays the 10 top users with the most currency, either holding or bank.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FhmxYzuHBBn3RKrjHUs38%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54de1076-9389-4343-8e6c-d26a822297cc&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7aeb3ce9&sv=2)

/item give[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#item-give)

This command allows a user to give another user an item from their inventory.

/shop view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#shop-view)

This command allows you to browse through the shop and displays the shop.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FQxpVN8Nk0GWKBnbtnbeC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf0293e4-ac2c-42ce-9d7d-274d8445b67f&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85caa56b&sv=2)

/inventory[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#inventory)

This command displays your inventory.

/bank deposit[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#bank-deposit)

This command allows you to deposit currency into the bank that gains interest.

/bank withdraw[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#bank-withdraw)

This command allows you to withdraw money from the bank.

/beg[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#beg)

This command allows you to beg for currency with a low risk.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F4XJlb7kmVR2ZuN4rdHzV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4825000a-e5d4-4a1b-af28-6825d1195b0e&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bee0686e&sv=2)

/lottery[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#lottery)

This command allows you to view the next lottery and also enter into it.

/crime[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#crime)

With this command you can commit a crime that is high risk but also high reward.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FbDYfDM5eR6RAGKoPzvQ5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded0778f1-a3a2-4bc7-a2bc-541b78acb271&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af0381e7&sv=2)

/work[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#work)

This command allows you to work and gain currency from doing so. ![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2X4wssM95PKCB362YDBG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec1f111a-35f7-4435-8a87-7537bbbc0a4a&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afb07075&sv=2) /shop buy[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#shop-buy)

This command allows you to buy something from the shop.

/fish[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#fish)

This command allows you to go fishing.

/job list[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#job-list)

This command shows the active job list. [Economy Jobs](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-jobs)
 ![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FdzzJramtmGn33ky9j1oa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d44a434-67da-4af0-bda4-68e133f0f370&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46f27f12&sv=2) /rob bank[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#rob-bank)

This command will attempt to rob a bank, multiple users will need to be in on this.

/ec stats[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#ec-stats)

This command shows your economy stats.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FQs0grhJlqgtCz5WDOtKw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8163bebb-cf55-48fa-8083-cc4d15fbc613&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f711c21&sv=2)

/job apply[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#job-apply)

This command allows you to apply for a job.

/ec cooldowns[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#ec-cooldowns)

This command checks and shows all your active minigame and economy cooldowns.

/rob player[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#rob-player)

This command will make you attempt to steal an amount of currency from a player but if they catch you then you lose some money.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#minigame-commands)

Minigame Commands

/scratchcard[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#scratchcard)

This command allows you to buy a scratchcard that could potentially give you a lot of currency.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPPdn0rfUN5GIE03Wb6e9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14963dd5-60ba-45cc-9201-b3c8d414979f&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7edc7e00&sv=2)

This command serves as a minigame and challenges a player to a dice bet.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FDKkSkq6OIyCM9l3oDSp5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dddc5a718-ef69-42e4-b7f7-16d8a1d71a74&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ff02a57&sv=2)

/dos[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#dos)

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of double or steal against a user.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FiM0HHeXj2zmGDNPD9660%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D323ede87-1b59-4820-90ff-7cff5497eb27&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5039cdbd&sv=2)

This command servers as a minigame and plays a game of hangman.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FryGcSmaCmj4jptH3ohXw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ddc2fa5-8f07-4e33-a465-a12f8f975659&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b679f6&sv=2)

/high-low[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#high-low)

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of higher or lower.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FZQUCThwVaePyyG5ytP3p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd279bbad-db7d-4a8b-9c2d-20aad871e652&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd96f678&sv=2)

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of rock paper scissors.

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of tic tac toe.

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of blackjack.

/matchpairs[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#matchpairs)

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of match pairs.

/5dice[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#id-5dice)

This command serves as a minigame and plays a game of 5dice. ![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FkzgG5VkCN79UA3f0XChb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9833604f-abf3-4988-a097-c6b515d74baf&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da7ac06c&sv=2) /lightout[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#lightout)

This command allowes you to play Lights Out. It is a puzzle game where the objective is to turn off all the lights on a grid. Pressing a button toggles that light and the adjacent lights directly above, below, and to either side.

/mastermind[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#mastermind)

This command allowes you to play Mastermind, the goal of this game is for the Codebreaker (you) to guess the exact colors and positions of a secret code created by the Codemaker (the bot) in as few attempts as possible.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#add-command)

\[👑\] Add Command

By clicking the add command button you can create your own command for the economy using all the module [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 and settings.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#events)

Events


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Economy & Minigames module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Ftm1TlITi3p6SGZCULm1h%252Fimage_2024-07-27_225839672.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd93f300c-2dd1-4e3e-99f0-dd77963edf6a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64fb924c&sv=2)

Custom Events of the Economy & Minigames module

Bank Interest[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#bank-interest-1)

This event controls the entire banking system with the related commands.

Economy - Lottery[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-lottery)

This even controls the lottery system and the correlating commands.

Economy Autorole[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-autorole)

This event controls the entire [Economy Roles](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#economy-roles)
 system.

Currency for Messages[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#currency-for-messages)

This event adds currency to users based on specific criteria if [Earn Currency for Messages](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#earn-currency-for-messages)
 is enabled.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/economy-and-minigames#add-event)

\[👑\] Add Event

By clicking the add event button you can create your own event for the economy using all the module [variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 and settings.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Music | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FaSwU0kGfIvvoUC7ZgviX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1ae7a1c5-8b71-41d8-9c28-dc7855711c9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9aee6765&sv=2)

This module requires a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function.

If you are looking for instructions on how to use the Music Blocks, please see [Music Actions](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/actions/music-actions)
.

The [Music](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/music)
 module gives you access to pre-built commands for the music blocks, allowing your bot to play music in your Discord server!

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#commands)

Commands


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Music module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F9Ltl6i3C4L4fXQ7xQvQi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6229c2c-0f89-4c84-82ac-d967face445b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c9be54d&sv=2)

/music seek[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-seek)

This command allows you to go to (or "seek" to) a specific time in the current song that is playing.

/music pause[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-pause)

This command will pause the currently playing song. Use `/music resume` to resume playing the song.

/music queue[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-queue)

This command will return every song that is currently in the music queue and information about the currently playing song.

/music clear-filters[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-clear-filters)

This command will clear all filters added with the `/music apply-filter` command.

/music track[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-track)

This command returns information about the song that is currently playing, including the title, artist, progress and album art.

/music play[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-play)

Plays a song in the voice channel you or the bot is currently in. Accepts song titles, URLs, or playlist URLs.

/music stop[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-stop)

Stops playing music and clears the queue.

/music replay[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-replay)

Replays the current song from the beginning.

/music disconnect[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-disconnect)

Disconnects the bot from the voice channel and resets the queue, filters, and settings.

/music resume[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-resume)

Resumes playback of music paused with `/music pause`.

/music set-autoleave[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-set-autoleave)

Configure whether to automatically disconnect the bot from the voice channel when the queue ends.

/music set-autoplay[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-set-autoplay)

Configure whether to automatically queue similar songs when the queue ends.

/music apply-filter[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-apply-filter)

Apply various sound filters to the music playback. Use `/music clear-filters` to clear them.

/music skip[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-skip)

Skips the currently playing song.

/music remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-remove)

Remove a specific song from the queue based on queue position.

/music shuffle[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-shuffle)

Shuffles the music queue.

/music set-volume[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-set-volume)

Sets the volume of the music (0-200).

/music loop[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#music-loop)

Choose whether to loop the currently playing track or queue.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#events)

Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

The music module is also provided with two events:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F8pkjDvYRQlhoTgKlcJON%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbfa4027-3e31-49eb-a55e-c79e3b9a18fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a036c430&sv=2)

Set voice channel status to song data[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#set-voice-channel-status-to-song-data)

This event will set the voice channel status to information about the currently playing song when a song starts plating

Remove voice status song data[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#remove-voice-status-song-data)

This event will remove the status set by `Set voice channel status to song data` when a song finishes playing.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Commands](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#commands)
    
*   [Events](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/music#events)
    

Was this helpful?

# Birthdays | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUAqkyhsqbDWwFbRsdZWq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df39b3ab2-8df8-4e1d-8aef-7691ca0a3336&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7f5b8e&sv=2)

Some of the features of this module require a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function. You can however use the module with a free subscription.

The [Birthdays module](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/99761223-9984-460d-a847-e16e64498099/birthdays)
 allows users to set their birthdays, view users' birthdays, and receive automatically personalized birthday wishes.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#common-issues)

Common Issues


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Experiencing issues with the module? Check out the common issues below. If your issue is not listed in this page, make sure your module is updated to the latest version. If you are still experiencing issues with the module, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthdays-are-not-being-detected)

Birthdays are not being detected

If no birthday message gets sent on an user's birthday, they don't receive their birthday role or they aren't able to use the `/birthday showcase` command, please try the steps below.

1

Ensure the module is updated to the latest version. You can update it by clicking the "Update Module" button at the top of the settings page of the module.

2

Ensure that the "Default Server" option in your [Timed Events](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/timedevents)
 page is set to the server your birthday module runs in.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F6pI9kVUm6PfCZ4a9udzE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca50b855-bcca-4a2d-8364-6b9dbe2f0719&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a4157da&sv=2)

3

If you're still experiencing issues, join our [support server](https://discord.gg/botghost)
 to ask for further help, we'll do our best to solve your issue!

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#watch-the-tutorial)

Watch the Tutorial


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#settings)

Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#general-settings)

General Settings

In this area, you can setup and customize the general settings for the commands and events of this module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FjFtaqediq9IuqBYPd4Kn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded01a297-6e3d-4e1c-b7ea-91642c06f20c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28bdd15b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#timezone)

Timezone

Here you may choose the timezone you'd like to set times in for this module. It is recommended that you select [your local timezone](https://www.google.com/search?q=what+is+my+timezone&oq=what+is+my+timezone&gs_lcrp=EgZjaHJvbWUyBggAEEUYOTIJCAEQABgKGIAEMg0IAhAAGJECGIAEGIoFMgkIAxAAGAoYgAQyCQgEEAAYChiABDIJCAUQABgKGIAEMgcIBhAAGIAEMgcIBxAAGIAEMgkICBAAGAoYgATSAQgzNzAzajBqNKgCALACAA&sourceid=chrome&ie=UTF-8)
.

If you want to know more about timezones, the following links may be helpful:

*   [List of all timezones](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_UTC_offsets)
    
*   [Timezones by country](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_time_zones_by_country)
    
*   [Daylight saving time countries](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daylight_saving_time_by_country)
    

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#time)

Time

Here you may choose the time that birthday wishes will go off on a users' birthday. This will sync to the timezone you chose above.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#save-birth-year)

Save Birth Year

Here you may choose whether the birth year of a user should be allowed to save, not be allowed to save, or be required to save.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#embeds-color)

Embeds Color

Here you may choose the color for the embeds of the Birthdays module. This will be used in all messages.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-card)

Birthday Card

In this area, you can setup and customize a custom card that can be used across all messages of the module using the `{card}` variable.

Features in this section are limited to [Premium](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 users.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F2dFd0gNLjhDu0LTcGpO7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e8a9e5d-5543-4787-a1fd-4739b1d4e2bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e601c9e&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#enable-custom-card)

\[👑\] Enable Custom card

This toggle option allows you to enable the `{card}` variable

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#background)

\[👑\] Background

This setting allows you to set the background type for your card. Below you may find some information on each background type.

Default Background

Plain Color

Custom Image

By selecting this option, the default background image will be used. Cards generated with the default background will look like this:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F4mmmtEjRsFwENWhARhpl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70ecdfc2-c994-4971-a4f3-cc5f0eaa86f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37dbe9d5&sv=2)

By selecting this option, you will be able to select a custom plain color for your card's background.

The following settings will appear:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F1XwRTQDdpQSWN0paC9MQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5583500f-33e8-4224-a8e3-31423db57af4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dce00588&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#background-color)

\[👑\] Background Color

Here you may choose the color for the background on the custom card.

By selecting this option, you will be able to paste a custom image link for your background

The following settings will appear:

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FZTbcqpZ0PjHDAPus09g0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D929901fe-b461-432c-8be8-6f585ee56387&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75d03392&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#background-image)

\[👑\] Background Image

Here you may set the background image on the custom card. This must be a valid image URL.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#title-color)

\[👑\] Title Color

Here you may choose the font color for the "title" text on the custom card.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#description-color)

\[👑\] Description Color

Here you may choose the font color for the "description" text on the custom card.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#avatar-border-color)

\[👑\] Avatar Border Color

Here you may choose the color for the circular border around the user's avatar on the custom card.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#card-title)

\[👑\] Card Title

Here you may set the "title" text on the custom card. All [default variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used, as well as some additional variables that can be found [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#module-variables)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#card-description)

\[👑\] Card Description

Here you may set the "description" text on the custom card. All [default variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used, as well as some additional variables that can be found [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#module-variables)
.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-message)

Birthday Message

In this area, you can setup and customize a birthday message to display on a users' birthday.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FqBhFt8Ab4Iu83wDrsfYP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D782be4d0-a8cf-41a8-afb5-acbcc66eaac4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b7e476f&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#send-message-on-birthday)

Send Message on Birthday

Here you may toggle whether a message is sent on a user's birthday.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#channel)

Channel

This menu allows you to select the channel where the birthday message will be sent. If you don't see your channel, make sure to click on the refresh button next to the "Channel" text.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#message)

Message

Here you may set the message that is sent on birthday. This message will be sent only if the user has set a birth year. All [default variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used, as well as some additional variables that can be found [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#module-variables)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#message-without-birth-year)

Message Without Birth Year

Here you may set the message that is sent on birthday. This message will be sent only if the user did not set a birth year. All [default variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used, as well as some additional variables that can be found [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#module-variables)
.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#reactions)

Reactions

Here you may choose up to 5 custom reactions to be added to the message sent.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#create-thread)

Create Thread

Here you may toggle whether a thread is created on the message for users to leave their birthday wishes in.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#lock-thread)

Lock Thread

Here you may toggle whether the thread created on the message is locked after 24 hours. The [create thread](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#create-thread)
 setting must be enabled. _This setting is only visible with_ [_Create Thread_](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#create-thread)
 _enabled._

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#add-role-on-birthday)

Add Role on Birthday

In this area, you can setup and customize a function to add a role to the user on their birthday and remove it after 24 hours.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FoxqXy9II9zwY5iyDJNTq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da70da63e-67b1-4687-847e-52b9358e8ce8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc5bce5b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#add-a-role-on-birthday)

Add a Role on Birthday

Here you may toggle whether a role is added on a user's birthday for 24 hours.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#role)

Role

Here you may choose the role that is added to the user on their birthday for 24 hours. If you don't see your channel, make sure to click on the refresh button next to the "Channel" text.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-showcase-command)

/birthday showcase Command

In this area, you can setup and customize the functions of the /birthday command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FkTzKS4Oi1kC7F7jrxTZv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f90c077-80ca-4c67-80a1-510e69df1343&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f520ccd1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#enable-birthday-showcase-command)

Enable /birthday showcase Command

Here you may enable and allow the usage of the `/birthday showcase` command.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#command-cooldown)

Command Cooldown

This input allows you to set a cooldown for the command in minutes. Users won't be able to use this command twice wiithin this time range. It cannot be higher than 1440 minutes (24 hours).

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#command-response)

Command Response

This field allows you to setup the response the bot will return when the command is ran. All [default variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 can be used, as well as some additional variables that can be found [here](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#module-variables)
.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#commands-permissions)

Commands Permissions

In this area, you can setup and customize the permissions for running each command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FyySzq80lDGx5GCFL581Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9d540dc-bb24-4ca4-95ce-5e5f731e991f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e8dc2a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#admin-roles)

Admin Roles

Here you may choose the roles who can use the [/birthday-user-manage](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-user-manage)
 command. They will be able to set, update, remove birthdays or blacklist users from adding their own birthday.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#channel-restrictions)

Channel Restrictions

You can setup channel restrictions to allow the usage of the module's commands only in certain channels.

Blacklist Type

Information

No channel restrictions

Users will be able to use the command everywhere.

Disable for these channels...

Set this blacklist type if you want the commands to work in all channels except the channels provided in the menu below.

Enable for these channels...

Set this blacklist type if you want the commands to work only in the channels provided in the menu below.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FoauM4WtWXGRfB2gSYsZR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4fe62802-c2e5-4fae-993d-2c50423f7085&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45894fba&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#role-restrictions)

Role Restrictions

You can setup role restrictions to allow the usage of the module's commands only to certain roles.

Blacklist Type

Information

No role restrictions

Everyone will be able to use the commands of the module.

Disable for these channels...

Set this blacklist type if you want the commands to work for all users, except users with at least one of the roles provided in the menu below.

Enable for these channels...

Set this blacklist type if you want the commands to work only for users with at least one of the roles provided in the menu below.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FFwOqnq51U6ywR2wVk5iz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7e6f22e-1dfc-437d-87d3-7cce619f26e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1173da2b&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#module-variables)

Module Variables


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Birthdays module collects information about all users who record their birthdays. This information can be referenced using variables in the text settings of the module page, or in the builders. You can use any of these variables to provide accurate information in birthday messages, cards, etc.:

These variables can only be used in the Birthdays module.

Variable

Description

`{target}`

Returns an @mention for the target user

`{target_id}`

Returns the user ID for the target user. Can be used in other [default variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/variables)
 or to return the ID in general.

`{target_name}`

Returns the name for the target user.

`{card}`

\[👑\] Returns the image URL of the birthday card for the target user. Will return nothing if you have the Enable Custom Card setting disabled. Recommended for use in a plain text message or the image in an embed. This variable requires a premium subscription to work.

`{age}`

Returns the current age for the target user.

`{birthday_timestamp}`

Returns the UNIX timestamp of the birthday for the target user.

`{day}`

Returns the day of birth for the target user.

`{month}`

Returns the month of birth for the target user.

`{year}`

Returns the year of birth for the target user.

`{current_year}`

Returns the current year.

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#commands)

Commands


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the commands of the Birthdays module. Below you may find some information on each command of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FvjgP8AgSk2utz5MkwqN5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47ddf352-ed36-41e8-ad04-2ba6840e1222&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77ccdc92&sv=2)

/birthday set[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-set)

The birthday set command allows you to set your own birthday to a given date. The date must be provided in DD/MM/YYYY format. You can choose whether you want the birth year to be required in the [Save Birth Year](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#save-birth-year)
 setting. You cannot use this command if you're currently celebreating your birthday.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FPKDYvq36c9jnfqtqksdW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D089fe18c-e97a-4c3d-be81-3debcc282a3e&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=577ec9b5&sv=2)

/birthday remove[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-remove)

This command allows users to remove their birthday from the system. They can always add it back using [/birthday set](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-set)
.

/birthday view[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-view)

This command allows users to view their own or someone's else birthday. They can also update their personal settings by selecting themselves when running the command.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fuwip3lCJlGHjt3z5qdW8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc02e8e5-0b19-489f-80f4-95ff6d20c268&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb8ef833&sv=2)

/birthday upcoming[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-upcoming)

This command allows users to get a list of all upcoming birthdays.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FqzEkNuzXXhl4FoerUedd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6b6676b-dd20-4eee-b9af-805b0defb4f9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a4c8192&sv=2)

/birthday showcase[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-showcase)

Users who are currently celebrating their birthday can use this command. You can configure it from the [/birthday showcase Command](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-showcase-command)
 section.

/birthday user-manage[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthday-user-manage)

This command can only be used by server's [admins](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#admin-roles)
 and allows them to update / edit certain information of the selected user. The list of available settings depends on the current birthday status of the user.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FVv1dVZNdzGzjPi5b3PAH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D844b65d4-ef7f-41af-9eb6-69d0a9b8bac5&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e83ad6&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#events)

Events


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this area, you can view and modify the events of the Birthdays module. Below you may find some information on each event of the module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FyZC5npIznxeD0luUS7FJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4130fb5-3c32-468a-821d-afdf0ad94971&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5b07614&sv=2)

Birthdays Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#birthdays-handler)

This event is the core of the module: it triggers every 30 minutes and ensures to wish your members a happy birthday. Make sure to not delete the associated timed event in the [timed events](https://documentation.botghost.com/custom-commands-and-events/events/timed-events)
 module.

Leaves Handler[](https://documentation.botghost.com/fun-modules/birthdays#leaves-handler)

This event automatically resets birthday data of users who left the server.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intended.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.

# Leveling | BotGhost Documentation

[Download now our new iOS App on the\
\
App Store!](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/botghost/id6757778695)

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://documentation.botghost.com/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling.md)
.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FRJNWMiGBVTcm1mqgH4vP%252FScreenshot%25202024-07-16%2520123743.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e4faddf-9319-4d5f-be59-98aeaaacce6a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93d6bd6a&sv=2)

Some of the features of this module require a [Premium Subscription](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 to function. You can however use the module with a free subscription.

The [Leveling](https://dashboard.botghost.com/dashboard/module/7c393ff6-f182-44d6-883c-bebd890a2594/leveling)
 module will allow you to setup a highly customizable leveling system for both text based interactions and voice interactions.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#watch-the-tutorial)

Watch the Tutorial


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#settings)

Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#general-settings)

General Settings

In this area, you can setup and customize the general settings for the commands and events of this module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FGQEOriv5fDvD3HFVOroV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7e54947-5fe0-46a0-932c-151a8ed65949&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6b29ab2&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#embeds-color)

Embeds Color

Change the embed color for the public embeds that are set alongside this module such as the leaderboard.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#max-level)

Max Level

This option will allow you to define a maximum level users can reach with the leveling module. Setting this option to **0** will disable it meaning there will be no level limit. If a limit is defined, users will not be able to surpass it.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#additional-required-xp-per-level)

Additional Required XP Per Level

This option will allow you to change the default XP increment upon level up. On level up, the required experience will increase by the set amount. For instance, if this setting is set to 50 and the previous level required 200 XP to level up, the next level will require 250 XP. Also, the set amount will correspond to the required experience to reach the level 1.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#clear-leveling-data-on-leave)

Clear Leveling Data on Leave

This option will allow you to toggle on/off data clearing on user leave, if enabled (default) once a user leaves the server it will automatically clear their activity data.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#send-a-message-on-level-up)

Send a Message on Level Up

This option will allow you to define how and if a level up message should be sent once a user levels up. By default this is set to disabled however, you can choose between:

Selection

Action

**Disabled**

Does not send any message on level up.

**Current Channel**

Send the message to the channel the user leveled up in.

**Custom Channel**

Send the message to a selected channel.

**Direct Message**

Send a direct message to the user that leveled up.

**Current Channel & Direct Message**

Send a message to the channel the user leveled up in and send a direct message to the user that leveled up.

**Custom Channel & Direct Message**

Send the message to a selected channel and send a direct message to the user that leveled up.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#custom-channel)

Custom Channel

In this dropdown you can pick the channel that you would like level up messages to be sent to. _This setting is only visible when a custom channel option has been selected in_ [Send a Message on Level Up](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#send-a-message-on-level-up)
_._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#level-up-server-message)

**Level Up Server Message**

Here you can edit the level up message that is sent to the server when a user levels up. All variables can be used. A list of additional variables you can use is listed in [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#variables)
. _This setting is only visible when a server message option has been selected in_ [Send a Message on Level Up](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#send-a-message-on-level-up)
_._

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#level-up-direct-message)

**Level Up Direct Message**

Here you can edit the level up message that is sent to the user when they levels up. All variables can be used. A list of additional variables you can use is listed in [Variables](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#variables)
. _This setting is only visible when a direct message option has been selected in_ [Send a Message on Level Up](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#send-a-message-on-level-up)
_._

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FXL7gMKBVAREdZlM9Nacc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86233ded-e760-4aef-b88e-876559cbec72&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a1841a2&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#maximum-xp-per-message)

Here you can set the maximum number of XP points that will be given per message in numerical format (1, 2, 3, 4, etc).

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#cooldown)

Cooldown

Here you can define the cooldown period between messages receiving and not receiving XP points, messages sent during the specified cooldown period will not grant the user any experience points. This option takes a numerical format (1, 2, 3, 4, etc). Setting this to 0 will disable the cooldown completely.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#voice-xp-settings)

Voice XP Settings

Features in this section are limited to [Premium](https://documentation.botghost.com/premium/premium-and-priority-hosting-plans#premium-plans)
 users.

The leveling module also comes with a voice channel XP function which allows users to accumulate XP points by partaking in a voice channel. By joining a voice channel, the bot will follow a precise formula, which is: `A * ( 1 - e ^ ( - B * secs in voice ) )`. This will give a different amount of XP basing on the time in seconds the user has remained in the voice channel.

However, the amount of XP given per second will slowly decrease, to prevent spam / AFK users (example if the user stays for a second he will get 1 point, 2 secs 2.9 points, 3 secs 3.7 and so on). It will be calculated once the user leaves the voice. A and B are parameters and can be edited using the 'Voice XP Settings'.

A is the max XP that can be gained in a session, and B the "speed" that value A will be reached. However, the recommended values are 1000 and 0,0005. The user does not need to talk to gain XP.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FKVWdhHV1GR5YPMHbKUAQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ebca788-94ad-43f5-828a-40f548d5c7bb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37fe634a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#enable-voice-xp)

\[👑\] Enable Voice XP

Enabling/Disabling this option will activate/deactivate the ability to use the voice XP function, respectively. The below settings will only be displayed when it is enabled and hidden when disabled. By default this option is disabled.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#minimum-time-in-voice)

\[👑\] Minimum Time in Voice

This setting allows you to configure the minimum time in seconds required to stay in the voice channel to gain at least 1 experience point. This is defined by seconds and takes a a numerical format (1, 2, 3, 4, etc).

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#xp-per-session-a)

\[👑\] XP per Session _(A)_

This option will allow you to define the maximum amount of XP an user can gain by staying in a voice channel without leaving. The recommended value for this setting is 1000. Do not change this value if you don't know what you're doing, otherwise the XP may be given incorrectly.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#xp-gain-speed-b)

\[👑\] XP Gain Speed _(B)_

This option will allow you to define the bot will give users XP by staying in a voice channels. The recommended value for this setting is 0,0005. Do not change this value if you don't know what you're doing, otherwise the XP may be given incorrectly.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#cooldown-1)

\[👑\] Cooldown

Here you can define the cooldown period between receiving and not receiving XP points, during the specified cooldown period XP points will not be granted to the user. This option takes a numerical format (1, 2, 3, 4, etc). Setting this to 0 will disable the cooldown completely.

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#channels-and-roles)

Channels & Roles

Find out about the Channel & Role settings for the Leveling module.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FoyYPdSDGdX3HJGYNDIHQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4021d1a7-cf49-4371-8442-796519904cde&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0f02a0a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#admin-role)

Admin Role

Here you can select the role which will be considered admins. users with these roles will be able to edit other users' XP.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#channel-restrictions)

Channel Restrictions

Here you can set some channel restrictions choosing between None, Disable on all channels except or enable on all channels except. When enabled a new channel selection box will be displayed allowing you to input channels.

Type

Details

No Channel Restrictions

If this option is selected, no channel restrictions will be applied.

Disable for these channels

Based on the channels input, they will not provide XP for users.

Enable these channels

Based on the channels input, only these channels grant XP, the rest won't.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#role-restrictions)

Role Restrictions

Here you can set some role restrictions choosing between None, Disable on all roles except or enable on all roles except. When enabled a new role selection box will be displayed allowing you to input roles.

Type

Details

No role restrictions

If this option is selected, no role restrictions will be applied.

Disable for these roles

Based on the roles input, users who have these roles won't gain XP.

Enable these roles

Based on the roles input, only users with these roles gain XP, the rest won't.

To save the edits you made on the role reward's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FE3KQtIWF2myW7FevJxGP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4640af0f-4c26-4383-819e-f0ae7be37b89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1629e5b3&sv=2)

###

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FS9lxlhd69BiMHUPOwS1f%252Fimage_2024-07-17_182240998.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd2d2e88-a34d-48f3-bd4a-9f764c85fc4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b387679e&sv=2)
