#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#randomize-boosts)

Randomize Boosts

Enabling this option will make it so instead of giving the set amount of xp boost to the user, the amount of experience received from the boost will go around 1% and the boost percentage assigned to the user.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#boost-percentage)

Boost Percentage

This field modifies the percentage of XP that the user will receive when boosted.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#boost-type)

Boost Type

Channel Boost

Role Boost

This type of boost will make an increase in XP in a certain channel.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#boosted-channel)

Boosted Channel

In this selection you can choose the channel in which you want the boost to occur in.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FSiFOSfbSUf0LHigK7Aye%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D930140a5-03b9-41a5-ae94-1c468bb4f4d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd37a5e&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#enable-in-threads)

Enable in Threads

If this toggle is enabled then the boost will also apply to the threads in the channel that the boost is occurring in.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FdEIE5G7OIL8YorjGPKGc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8cf4ab4-8e94-40f7-a365-a58b9fb11d9a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44bcd66f&sv=2)

This type of boost will affect users with a certain role.

#### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#boosted-role)

Boosted Role

In this selection you can choose the role that the boost is affecting.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FDCJQ42r8AToKLaA7CkH9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db70ba8fa-556c-47ce-97aa-9b81d62ea27b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b199aed4&sv=2)

To save the boost's settings, you need to click "Add" in the bottom-right corner of the settings. This will reset the fields so you can set up another boost.

### 

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#your-boosts)

Your Boosts

In this section is where the added boosts can be edited / deleted. There is a maximum of 100 boosts.

To save the edits you made on the boost's settings, you need to click "Edit" in the bottom-right corner of the settings.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FUzcPqSrBltICEXdG726O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D609b54b1-781e-480a-8fdb-8bd83e1afde2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d423851&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#variables)

Variables


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The leveling module collects leveling data and sorts out levels for each user and their XP. These variables below can be used to reference that data in this module.

These Variables can only be used in this module.

Variable

Details

`{level}`

Displays the user's current level

`{xp}`

Displays the user's experience

`{required_xp}`

Displays the required experience to reach the next level

`{rank}`

Displays the rank of the user

* * *

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#commands)

Commands


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The leveling module has a wide range of commands, you can find these below.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F97pBsSmDQ1EVe0aGiBBS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe9ed0a8-fae6-4d55-a904-107510556f31&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dd6141e&sv=2)

/rank[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#rank)

This command will allow users to display their current XP progress as well as others.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FbZv2mA1hAb0xxWI2B6JU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D835b1f82-c255-4f79-b679-0a09302e29eb&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d33ec12&sv=2)

/level leaderboard[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#level-leaderboard)

This command will display the server's level leaderboard when triggered. Use the buttons below to navigate through the leaderboard. The button in the middle allows you to go to a specific position in the leaderboard. Change the value of the users-per-page option to show a different amount of users per page (defaults to 10).

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FkKAgGnJBbHeeinor9VyO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e0e2554-edb4-467c-b89f-c4526fe1c769&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4c9692f&sv=2)

/level edit-xp[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#level-edit-xp)

This is one of the admin commands for the module, users with the defined admin roles will be able to use this command to edit a user's XP points. You can add / set / remove a custom amount of levels / XP.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252Fc2jpi2d4vF9M3oL2aXdq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4df63dc-8992-4cb4-8a75-cb78ffbf57b4&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0317a3b&sv=2)

/level reset-leaderboard[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#level-reset-leaderboard)

This is one of the admin commands for the module, users with the defined admin roles will be able to use this command to reset the servers level leaderboard.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252FNX3iTDbaRyZTC2cMO7mY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4dc3260c-e0c0-4429-b5e8-732e65413477&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c50ab23c&sv=2)

[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#events)

Events


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The leveling module has a wide range of events, you can find these below.

![](https://documentation.botghost.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1937909199-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-Lm_hW5MApY3J0lRhi0M%252Fuploads%252F0FZsGSzw0lEB44RGIH19%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df97a169b-b734-4eff-b531-9fd36160d27c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc2623de&sv=2)

Level Up[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#level-up)

This event will track when a user levels up and send the level up message to the appropriate destination.

Message Experience[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#message-experience)

This event will track user messages and add XP points to a users total for each message, following the defined settings in the module.

Voice Experience - Join[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#voice-experience-join)

This event will track when a user joins a voice channel and start giving them XP points if you have the [Voice XP Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#voice-xp-settings)
 function enabled.

Voice Experience - Leave[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#voice-experience-leave)

This event will track when a user leaves a voice channel and stop giving the user XP points, the voice events will only work if you have enabled the [Voice XP Settings](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#voice-xp-settings)
 function above.

Clear on Leave[](https://documentation.botghost.com/community-engagement/leveling#clear-on-leave)

If you have the clear on Leave option enabled, this event will trigger when a user leaves the server and clear their Leveling data, this includes XP, Levels, etc.

* * *

It's advised that you do not edit the commands and events unless you have a good understanding of BotGhost and its Command Builder. If you encounter any issues, you might want to reset the module for it to work again as intented.

Additionally, a copy of the edited commands / events will be created if you update the module.
